## SC-01 新警局故事 / Fresh Police Story

相传商周时期，天地间魑魅魍魉横行，有恶兽为祸人间，令神州萧条、生灵涂炭。\
It is said that during the Shāng and Zhōu Dynasties, our land was plagued by malevolent creatures. They roamed the land, bringing havoc and leaving the nation and its people in endless suffering.

幸有大贤方相氏受天子之托，向十二摄提神请愿得巫舞之力，降伏恶兽，收为己用，更名为险道兽。\
On the emperor's order, Fāngxiàngshì the Wise sought the assistance of the twelve gods of Shètí. Bestowed with their divine might, Fāngxiàngshì bound the creatures and turned their monstrous power to the service of the people. These creatures became known as the Xiǎndào Beasts, guardians of the perilous path.

险道兽得摄提神感召，化为驱逐世间鬼疫、护一方安宁的神兽，得万民敬奉。\
Now reformed, the beasts were used to drive away evil and protect the land, and thus earned the reverence of the people.

然至唐末时，战乱频起。\
However, by the end of the Táng Dynasty, there arose many wars and troubles.

为守险道兽之传承延续，最后的方相氏在仙去之前将其分别托付给十二侲子。\
To preserve the legacy of the Xiǎndào Beasts, the last Fāngxiàngshì entrusted them to the Twelve Zhènzǐ, servants of the ritual, before passing away.

其中，险道兽强梁状虎衔蛇，凶悍无匹。\
Among the Xiǎndào Beasts, Qiángliáng, whose body was like a tiger with a serpent's tail, was considered unmatched in ferocity.

得强梁之人后以兽为名，改姓为梁——世代相承。\
The Zhènzǐ who was entrusted with Qiángliáng took Liáng as their surname, passing this knowledge down through their descendants.

**梁父**：时至今日，虽说世间已不再有妖魔肆虐，梁家也已不像过去那样风光，但家族上下都始终牢记祖训。\
**Liang's Father**: Until today, while the world no longer suffers from the evil spirits of the past and the reputation of our family has lessened, we have never forgotten our ancestors' teaching.

**梁父**：守礼克己、秉公持正、将为世间惩奸除恶视为己任。翻开家谱，每一个名字后面必定都是一个行得端坐得正、响当当的梁家子弟。\
**Liang's Father**: That is, self-restraint, propriety, righteousness, and the art of banishing evil. Study our family's history, and you will find each generation has lived up to our family name and our motto. To practice restraint, seek justice and expel evil.

**梁父**：……然而，险道兽强梁却已有近百年未曾现身了。\
**Liang's Father**: Yet, Qiángliáng had not appeared to us for almost a hundred years.

**梁父**：——直到你，我最引以为傲的女儿。直到你再一次唤醒了强梁。\
**Liang's Father**: That was, until you, my daughter—my pride, successfully summoned it after these long years.

**梁父**：你可知自己肩负着何种重望？\
**Liang's Father**: Do you understand the weight of the expectations you now carry?

父亲的手落在女孩的肩膀上，重如千钧。\
His hand rests on the girl's shoulder, its weight like that of the world.

**女孩**：……我知道的，爸爸。你就相信我吧。\
**Girl**: I understand. You can trust in me, Father.

不需要父亲再次提点，无数次的耳提面命早已让女孩有了答案。\
那是她唯一被允许拥有的答案。\
She has heard this story a thousand times, and for years, this answer has been engraved in her mind, for it is the only answer she has ever been allowed to give.

**梁月**：——请您相信我。我一定会完成强梁之主的使命，绝不会辜负家族的期望。\
**Liang Yue**: I will not fail our family. I will fulfill my destiny as a worthy master of Qiángliáng.

**波蒂埃**：早上好，伙计们。\
有谁能给我些配得上这个阳光明媚上午的好消息吗？\
**Poitier**: Morning, guys. Alright, who wants to hit me with some good news and make my day a little easier?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：召唤阵事件的分析报告出来了，它们连通的是郊外的一座牧场——\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: The report on that summoning ritual is done. Seems like the destination was some farm out in the sticks.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：嘿！谁拿走了署里的公共灵摆？\
我还要用呢，怎么也不打一声招呼？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Hey! Did someone take the pendulum without signing it out? We've only got one to go around.

神秘学犯罪科办公室内，每一名警员都忙得热火朝天，没人理会这位刚刚进门的同僚。\
Everyone in the Division of Arcane Affairs is caught up in the chaos of their own work, too busy to notice the officer who has just stepped in.

**波蒂埃**：……我带了咖啡，一共三杯，先到先得！\
**Poitier**: Let's try this another way. First three of you to give me some good news will earn yourselves a coffee, my treat.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：哦亲爱的，你真是个天使！今天这是刮的什么风？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Get ready, Poitier, cause what I'm about to tell you next is gonna blow your mind.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：给我留一杯！我找出那个拿走了灵摆却没有登记的混蛋后就来！\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Save me a cup. I gotta find our pendulum thief first.

高个子的年轻女警立刻成为了整个办公室中最受欢迎的人，但愤慨的咒骂声打破了这忙里偷闲的咖啡时间。\
Apparently, it doesn't take much to become the most popular person in the office. But before anyone can earn a steaming cup of joe, an angry shout interrupts them.

**？？？**：——嘿，我还在这呢！\
**???**: Hello. Excuse me. I'm still here.

**？？？**：你们这些警察总是这样浪费纳税人宝贵的时间和金钱。\
真係“上梁不正下梁歪”……\
**???**: *tut* I'm a tax-paying citizen. I pay your salary, so why don't you stop gossiping and do your job?! A crooked stick will have a crooked shadow!

男子瞪了波蒂埃一眼，骂骂咧咧地走出神秘学犯罪科的大门。\
He shoots Poitier a glare before stomping his way out of the Division of Arcane Affairs, muttering curses under his breath.

**波蒂埃**：……他怎么又来了，这次是投诉什么？\
**Poitier**: Him again? What's he complaining about this time?

找回公共灵摆后匆匆返回的警员接过咖啡，向波蒂埃耸了耸肩。\
Having brought the missing pendulum back to its place, the officer strides over and grabs a coffee. He shrugs.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：说我们不分青红皂白，就跑去唐人街里面寻找市民丢失的狗。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Ah, some nonsense about making a mistake while we were out searching for a dog in Chinatown.

**波蒂埃**：什么？狗？\
**Poitier**: A missing pooch? Since when are we the dog patrol?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：是啊，然后又是那老一套，说我们的人都是些搞不清楚状况的愣头青。\
接着当然少不了那个我们耳朵都听出茧子来的例子——\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Ah. I know. It's not our job. And then he got all huffy about us being brash and naive, and then it was right back to complaining about the incident last year.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：一年前，一名年轻的警员把一个孩子身上留下的中式按摩痕迹，误以为是虐待的伤痕通报了儿童保护组织，险些害那对可怜的父母失去抚养权……\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: You remember? When that rookie saw bruises on a kid and kicked up a whole fuss about child abuse? Turned out it was just some traditional Chinese massage. After they got cleared of the charges, the kid's parents were fuming about it for weeks.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：那件事上我们的人的确不够谨慎，但误会很快得到了澄清，那个年轻人也亲自登门道歉得到了原谅，不知道他一个无关人员还在耿耿于怀什么。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: But like, come on, it's literally a rookie mistake. He apologized, and they forgave him. You'd think that'd be problem solved, right? But this guy just wouldn't let it go. He's not even related.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：但我猜那件事就是他看我们科不顺眼的契机，因为这次他根本投诉错地方了。找狗这种事就不归我们管，找魔精才归。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Still, must have left a bad taste in his mouth, I guess. I just don't get why he's complaining about it to us. We don't find missing dogs. We find critters.

他们对视了一眼，叹了口气。\
They exchange a glance, and Poitier lets out a sigh.

**波蒂埃**：……我只能说，我很庆幸并不是所有的市民都是这样的。\
**Poitier**: Well, at least most folks are friendly.

**波蒂埃**：来吧，今天有什么好消息吗？\
**Poitier**: Yeah, yeah. Well, I was asking for good news. So how about something upbeat?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：遗憾。只有坏消息。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Sorry. I've got nothing of that particular flavor. Just the opposite.

**波蒂埃**：……那家伙又动手了？\
**Poitier**: Let me guess. Our "vigilante" struck again?

今晨的报纸被递到了她的眼前。\
在看清最上面格外醒目的标题后，手中咖啡的香气似乎也不再诱人了。\
The officer drops the morning paper in front of her. As her eyes land on the headline, her coffee suddenly smells bitter.

**波蒂埃**：“正义的英雄‘针人’现身洛杉矶？恶人再次得到审判”……那些媒体还是这么喜欢夸大其词。这次又是什么人？\
**Poitier**: "The Vigilante 'Nightpiercer' Bestows Justice to L.A. Streets." Urgh, so melodramatic. Who got hit this time?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：一伙富家公子哥为了取乐，把自己的队友弄进了重症监控室，结果连拘留室都没进，派去的警察直接被老爹们安排的律师请回去了。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Some rich varsity boys. They got in the news over some hazing incident that put a teammate into the ICU. But, you know how it is. Strings were pulled, and all the charges went away.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：今天早上，他们被发现叫人钉在了学校体育场的围栏上……\
别说打球了，大概下半辈子都要和轮椅拐杖打交道。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: But, get this: all of them were found pinned up on the school's fencing this morning, and with those injuries, looks like they can kiss college football goodbye.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：如果要是问我个人的感想，我肯定没办法同情那群家伙，我太清楚学校里的那种货色是什么德性了。但……\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Hate to say it, but I gotta side with the vigilante on this one. Those kids were monsters. Still ...

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：我们是警察，而我们那位“正义的英雄”是在犯罪，他的所作所为绝不是值得推崇的。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: We're the police, and crime is crime. Doesn't matter how scummy the victims might be.

波蒂埃烦闷地将手中的报纸丢到了一旁不知道哪个同事乱糟糟的桌子上。\
Irritated, Poitier tosses the newspaper onto one of the many cluttered desks around her.

**波蒂埃**：如果真的是个为民除害的英雄也就罢了，但使用“飞针神秘术”？\
他是在模仿C07吗？透着一种哗众取宠的味道……\
**Poitier**: The arcane skill this guy cast, using those needles? It's like he's trying to imitate Detective C07. What's up with that?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：哦，你说那个电影《神秘警探C07》？我看过，我爱神秘学电影。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: C07, like from the movie series? Don't act so surprised I've seen them. You know I love movies about arcanum.

**波蒂埃**：这次有什么线索了吗？\
**Poitier**: So, do we got anything?

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：埃尔登警长的脸色会告诉你答案。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Ha. Have you seen the look on Chief Elden's face yet?

波蒂埃疑惑地望向角落的警长办公室，透过半开的百叶窗观察屋内的情形。\
Poitier looks over at the Deputy Chief's Office, squinting as she tries to see through the slatted blinds.

**波蒂埃**：……我的天呐！上一次埃尔登的脸变成这个颜色，还是他发现女儿交了个瘪三男友那时候吧？\
**Poitier**: Hot damn, I know that look. Wasn't the last time when he found out his daughter was dating some jackass crook?

**波蒂埃**：“针人”一向神出鬼没，就算这次还是没有线索，也不必这样吧？\
**Poitier**: I know this Nightpiercer guy's been tricky, but is it really that bad?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：你有所不知……就是那个“上面”，说看我们迟迟抓不住“针人”的尾巴，所以派了个外援过来。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: You don't know the half of it. The pressure's been building on him. Now, apparently, the up-tops are sending us some support.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：一名来自那个夜巡特遣管理局的见习执夜人即将大驾光临，帮助我们这些没用的神秘学警察解决这座城市的麻烦。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Some cadet, from the Vigiles Bureau. I guess they've decided we're not working hard enough, or something.

**波蒂埃**：你是说基金会的那个？\
他们不是专门负责那些“可能造成极其严重后果”的神秘学犯罪事件的吗？\
**Poitier**: Vigiles? From the Foundation? Aren't they only responsible for the arcanum crimes that'll "cause serious consequences"?

**波蒂埃**：虽然“针人”的确很棘手，但我并不认为他的危险性有那么高。\
**Poitier**: I don't see how this Nightpiercer guy is their kind of trouble.

**波蒂埃**：再说这是我们的城市，用不着夜巡特遣的家伙来“热心帮忙”，他们对这里了解多少——\
**Poitier**: Besides, how's a vigil even going to help us? They don't know this city like we do. And not even a full agent, just a cadet.

**波蒂埃**：等等，你刚才说“见习”？\
**Poitier**: Wait, did you say cadet?

她终于意识到同僚方才的话语中有一个不该被忽视的关键词，不禁瞪大了眼睛。\
Poitier's head snaps back to the officer, her eyes wide. She can't just let that word slide by without notice.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：他们选拔新人的考核中有那么一些实习项目。\
看起来我们这里成了给未来的超级精英练手的幼儿园了。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: You heard me. Apparently, they decided this is gonna be a thing. Send the cadets along to assist and test their chops. So now we're not just dogcatchers. We're babysitters, too.

**波蒂埃**：……这是什么新式笑话吗？\
**Poitier**: Is this some kind of joke?

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：我刚听说的时候也和你一个反应。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Your words, my lips.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：但我们的局长大人认为这是个好主意——和未来的超级精英、夜巡特遣管理局还有背后的圣洛夫基金会打好关系总不是坏事。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: The Chief said it's a chance to develop a better working relationship between us and the Vigiles. I think brass just wants to cozy up with the St. Pavlov Foundation.

她喝干手中的咖啡，将空杯精准地掷进一旁的垃圾桶。\
She downs the rest of her coffee and tosses the empty cup into the trash.

**波蒂埃**：怪不得埃尔登那个表情……那家伙什么时候来？有人知道那人的底细吗？\
**Poitier**: Yeah, that would explain the look on Elden's face. So, what? Anyone know when this cadet is due? Or hell, anything useful at all?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：听说是个来自东方的小丫头，家里很有来头，有一头祖传的强大“密友”，也正因为这个原因被选进了夜巡特遣管理局。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: I heard tell it's some Chinese girl from a famous family of arcanists. She's got a mega-powerful familiar, and that's why the Vigiles recruited her.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：我很想说既然我们的新朋友通过了那场选拔，那么无论她是否靠的是祖传的好帮手，多少都能够派上些用场。但……\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Really, just for her familiar? That can't be the only reason. Did she at least like score well on her tests?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：据可靠消息称，我们的小精英是从警校被直接挑选过去的。\
这意味着这位援兵实际上并没有任何工作经验。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Apparently, she didn't even take the test. She was still in training when she was picked. No field experience at all.

波蒂埃沉默了一会儿，怒火从她的胸口熊熊燃起。\
Poitier tries to maintain her steely demeanor, but the frustration proves too much to contain.

**波蒂埃**：……所以你们是说，我们即将迎来的是一个刚毕业的菜鸟、一个背靠家族的世家大小姐，要来我们这里给简历镀一层金。\
**Poitier**: So you mean this girl's a total liability? Some spoiled rich kid debutante looking for a chance to polish her resume?

坐在波蒂埃对面的警员嗤笑一声，刚想接话——他的目光落在波蒂埃的身后，忽然口风一转。\
The officer lets out a dry chuckle, but as her reply is about to leave her lips, her eyes flick behind Poitier, and her tone changes.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：这可不是我说的。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: That's not exactly what I said.

缺根筋的家伙很难被选上这个岗位，方才还嘈杂无比的办公室很快安静了下来。每个人都望向门口那个陌生的小个子身影。\
They wouldn't put just anyone in this position. The office falls silent as all eyes turn to the unfamiliar figure standing in the doorway.

**梁月**：不好意思，打扰一下。\
**Liang Yue**: Excuse me.

**梁月**：我是来报到的见习执夜人梁月，来自圣洛夫基金会夜巡特遣管理局。\
请问我在哪里可以找到埃尔登警长？\
**Liang Yue**: I'm vigil cadet Liáng Yuè from the St. Pavlov Foundation, Vigiles Bureau, reporting for duty, ma'am. Could you please point me to Deputy Chief Elden?

**波蒂埃**：……那边。\
**Poitier**: Hmm. He's in his office.

最终是波蒂埃回答了少女。\
她扬了扬下巴，向来人示意角落办公室的方向。\
Poitier is the one to break the silence. She jerks her head toward the office in the corner as she speaks.

**梁月**：我知道了，谢谢您。\
**Liang Yue**: I see. Thank you.

这位单枪匹马闯入神秘学犯罪科的不速之客微微点头示意，在众人的注视下穿过鸦雀无声的办公室。\
She offers a slight nod and, under the scrutiny of every officer present, makes her way to the Deputy Chief's Office.

窃窃私语在警长办公室的门关上后一发不可收拾。\
As soon as the door is shut, murmurs break out like wildfire.

**波蒂埃**：就这家伙？她像一只刚出生的小老鼠，我单手就能把她拎起来。\
**Poitier**: That's our princess? I've seen street rats bigger. I bet I could lift her up with one hand.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：你忘了她的好帮手。没有跟在身边……那应该就是召唤系的了。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Don't forget her familiar. Though, I don't see it now, so she must be a summoner.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：我还能说什么呢？\
真希望我的曾曾曾爷爷也能留下个什么东西给我继承。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Lucky her. I wish my great-great-great grandpa left me something like that.

**波蒂埃**：不知道埃尔登打算怎么处理她，难道真的让这大小姐参与调查？我想帮忙都被埃尔登拒绝了。\
**Poitier**: So, what's Elden gonna do? No way he's letting this baby rat scurry into our investigation. I'll show her the door myself if he'll let me.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：万一还有个什么大小姐脾气，那就更完蛋了。一毕业就是精英警探的天之骄子，我想象不出她老老实实听从命令的样子。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Guaranteed our vigil-to-be is a spoiled, air-headed legacy pick. I can't imagine she's the type to follow orders.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：我说伙计们，我们光是在这里瞎琢磨也不会有什么结果的。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Guys, we won't get any answers just sitting here.

**波蒂埃**：唉，你说得对，我去忙今天的工作了。自从乔什休了假，本来该两个人干的活就都落在我身上了……\
**Poitier**: Yeah, you're right. I need to get back to work. Josh is out on leave, so I've gotta cover all his cases.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：等等，别着急走啊。\
我有个方法能解答咱们的疑问。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Hey, hold on. I've got a way to get the scoop on this girl.

刚欲离开的波蒂埃被拉住了。同僚望向警长办公室的方向，向她挤了挤眼睛。\
Before Poitier can walk away, she grabs her sleeve and, with a knowing look on her face, indicates toward the Deputy Chief's office.

**埃尔登警长**：夜巡特遣管理局见习执夜人，由圣洛夫基金会东亚分部特别推荐参与选拔，培训期间综合成绩第一名……\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Liáng Yuè, specially recommended by the Foundation's East Asia branch for selection into the Vigiles Bureau, top-of-class during your training, selected to serve as the pilot for the vigil cadet field training program with the LAPD Division for Arcane Affairs.

**埃尔登警长**：听着可真了不得啊。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Hmph. It's an impressive resume.

**梁月**：您过奖了，这不算什么——\
**Liang Yue**: Thank you, sir. Actually, it's not that—

**埃尔登警长**：我让你说话了吗？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Did I ask for an explanation?

警长办公室中少女的声音明显停顿了片刻。\
Her voice falters for a moment.

**梁月**：……没有，长官。\
**Liang Yue**: No, sir.

**埃尔登警长**：那就闭嘴。在这里我让你说话你才可以说话，让你坐下你才可以坐下，让你做什么你就做什么。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Then don't give me one. You talk when I tell you to talk, you sit when I tell you to sit, and you do exactly as I say, when I say.

**埃尔登警长**：明白了吗？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Do I make myself clear?

**梁月**：我……明白了，长官。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, sir.

一墙之隔外的好事者们互相交换了一个心照不宣的坏笑。\
On the other side of the thin walls of the office, the officers exchange smirks as they listen in to their conversation.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：来了，埃尔登的下马威。\
这还真让人有些怀念啊。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Classic Elden. Reminds me of the good old days.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：我可一点都不怀念。\
但……那个大小姐似乎比我想象中的要老实听话。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Good? The hell was so good about them? Think you've taken one too many smacks on the noggin. Still, she isn't as stuck-up as I expected.

**波蒂埃**：她要是能给埃尔登呛回来那倒还有趣些。\
没胆的家伙。\
**Poitier**: Then she's probably a wuss. I figured she was gonna back talk him—more like a meek little mouse than a rat.

短暂的交头接耳后，他们再次安静下来，将耳朵贴到墙壁上捕捉办公室内的对话。\
They press their ears against the wall and fall silent once again.

**埃尔登警长**：上面告诉我，你是为协助我们抓住那个连续袭击犯“针人”而来的。\
但我对于你是否能做到这一点持怀疑态度。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: I've been told you're here to assist us in catching the vigilante known as Nightpiercer. But one look at you tells me you don't have the chops.

**埃尔登警长**：坦白说，我对你是否已经做好准备成为一名神秘学警察也持怀疑态度。\
回答我，梁。你准备好了吗？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: I'll bet you're greener than any rookie on my force. Now, Liáng, answer me. Are you ready?

**梁月**：是的，长官。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, sir.

**埃尔登警长**：作为神秘学警察，我们往往会遇到超乎你想象的神秘学案件。\
你对此有心理准备了吗？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: On this beat, you're going to encounter arcane crime that is worse than anything you've seen in your training—beyond your imagination. Are you prepared?

**梁月**：是的，长官。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, sir.

**埃尔登警长**：你需要灵活运用你的智慧和力量逮捕那些危险的神秘学家罪犯，而不是把名字列在受害者那一栏里给司里丢脸。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: When it comes to dealing with arcanist criminals, you need wits and you need strength. One mistake, and you could end up in a casket on that long flight back home.

**埃尔登警长**：你确定你做好准备了吗？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: So I ask again, are you up to this challenge?

**梁月**：是的，长官！我做好准备了。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, sir. I'm ready.

**埃尔登警长**：不，你没有。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: No, you aren't.

一份报纸被埃尔登从柜子里抽出，拍在了办公桌上。\
He pulls a newspaper from a drawer and slams it onto the desk.

**埃尔登警长**：读读上面写了什么。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Read it.

**梁月**：通过电话作案的神秘学家诈骗犯“棍骗约翰”落网，他用专属神秘术“唯命是从”控制受害者向自己的账户汇入大笔金钱。\
**Liang Yue**: The arcanist scammer, Johnny Three-Times, has been apprehended. Using his arcane skill "Omnis Obeisance," he manipulated his victims to do anything he asked, specifically, transferring all their money to him.

**梁月**：而他的神秘术发动条件是，让目标在一分钟内回答……三个“是的”。\
**Liang Yue**: In order to successfully cast his arcane skill, he requires his target to answer "yes" three times in one minute.

**埃尔登警长**：如果我是这家伙，你现在已经在掏钱包了——或是更糟。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: If you had been dealing with him, he'd already have you dumping your trust fund into his bank account, or worse.

**梁月**：……恕我直言，长官。\
您是我的长官，我不可能拒绝回答您的问话，这个测试并不公平。\
**Liang Yue**: With all due respect, sir, that isn't a fair evaluation. I wouldn't have answered you that way if you were not my commanding officer.

**埃尔登警长**：涉及神秘术的案子打从一开始就没有所谓的公平。\
绝大多数时候，你都要在对犯人神秘术一无所知的情况下面对他们。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Fair? There is no fair when it comes to arcanists. You've read the headlines about this guy and think you know what to expect, but what if he had abilities the news didn't know about? What if he could disguise himself?

**埃尔登警长**：还是说怎么，你需要每个犯人都在案发现场留下一份圣洛夫基金会神秘学家登记信息的复印件吗？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Or do you think that crooks just leave their resumes behind at the crime scene?

少女语塞了片刻。\
For a brief moment, she is at a loss for words.

**梁月**：……不，长官。\
**Liang Yue**: No, sir.

**埃尔登警长**：看看日期，这份报纸是上周的东西。如果你做好了准备，你就会知道这件事，如果你足够敏锐，就能在我问话时察觉到不对劲。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: This article was published a week ago. If you were as ready as you claimed, you should've known about this conman and his arcane skill. If you had any smarts, you'd have at least figured out I was probing you.

**埃尔登警长**：但你没有。也许你在某些方面十分出色，但刚才的测试结果已经证明，你在实战方面仍然缺乏经验。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: But you didn't. I don't know what the Foundation and your Vigiles teachers taught you. Frankly, I don't care. Because you don't have the practical skills necessary to keep yourself alive on these streets.

**埃尔登警长**：我不会让你参加“针人”事件的调查。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: I will absolutely not put a kid like you on the Nightpiercer case.

办公室内传来的声音冷若冰霜，门外偷听的警员们互相交换了一个眼神。\
His cold voice carries through the wall. The officers outside exchange glances.

**波蒂埃**：埃尔登说话还是这么不客气，也怪不得他这么多年一直没办法升职。\
**Poitier**: Cold and ruthless as a Minnesota winter. Elden's never been a people person. Guess that's why they keep him stuck down here with us.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：他说的这些的确就是我想说的话，不过……是不是稍微有点过火了？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: I don't know. I agree with him. But he's being pretty rough on her.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：那个少女有多大，成年了吗？嘿……有人能看到她的表情吗？她不会哭了吧？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: She's definitely too young for this. Whatcha think? She gonna cry?

**波蒂埃**：如果她连这点心理承受能力都没有，那我建议她趁早回家找妈妈去。\
**Poitier**: Look, if she can't handle the Chief, then she can't handle the city.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：奇怪，是我记错了吗？我记得波蒂埃警官报到那天，从警长办公室里走出来的时候是红着眼睛的……\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Is that right? I seem to remember someone's eyes going red a few times on her first day.

**波蒂埃**：什么——胡扯！你苦目糖吃太多，把脑子吃坏了吧！\
**Poitier**: What? Shut up. I didn't.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：伙计们！嘘——！\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Shh. Listen.

警员们重新安静下来，他们都好奇地等待着，警长究竟会对那名见习执夜人少女做出怎样的发落。\
They fall silent again, waiting to hear what fate will befall the young vigil cadet.

**埃尔登警长**：——这就是我要说的了。\
如果你想要哭着找你爸爸或是老师之类的大人物更换你的实习场所，请便。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: End of discussion. If you want to call home to your daddy or the Foundation and get reassigned somewhere else, be my guest.

**埃尔登警长**：但既然目前你被分到了我的地盘，一切就要按照规矩走。\
我给你的安排是处理“基础神秘学警情”，这是每个新人的必经之路。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: But as long as you're in my department, you'll follow my rules. For now, I'll assign you some of the lighter cases. This is grunt work, kid. Try not to mess it up.

**波蒂埃**：……嗯？等等。\
**Poitier**: Hold on. I've got a bad feeling.

波蒂埃瞪大了眼睛，但已经太迟了。\
Poitier's eyes widen, but it's too late to act.

**埃尔登警长**：——你的搭档是艾丽娅·波蒂埃，她同时也将担任你的临时教官。\
事实上，她现在就在门外。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Arya Poitier will be your partner and field training instructor. She'll be happy to help you adjust. Isn't that right, Officer Poitier?

听到这里，门外波蒂埃没忍住低声咒骂了起来。\
Poitier can't help but mutter a curse under her breath.

**波蒂埃**：该死……真是个配得上这个阳光明媚早上的“好”消息。\
**Poitier**: Crap. Guess my day isn't getting any easier.

## SC-02 最高危机 / Total Crisis

**波蒂埃**：我们到了，下车。\
**Poitier**: Here we are. Get out.

**波蒂埃**：这就是今天我们要处理的第一起警情了。\
**Poitier**: First case of the day.

**波蒂埃**：每当巡警发现神秘术相关的非紧急案情时，就会上报给调度中心，这些案子随后会被交给我们处理。\
**Poitier**: Any time regular beat cops find a case related to arcanum, they'll call it in to Dispatch, then we get to come mop it up.

**波蒂埃**：“基础神秘学警情”，这就是我们的主要工作。有时也会有紧急情况需要我们处理，不过那种时候比较少。\
**Poitier**: This is what we call a Basic Arcanum Incident, the bread-and-butter of our work, kid. It's not often that we get anything urgent, but you've gotta stay on your toes.

**波蒂埃**：我个人希望今天不会遇到那种情况，我可不想在穿越枪林弹雨时还要照顾一只第一天出勤的菜鸟。\
**Poitier**: But to be honest, I hope we don't get anything big today. Last thing I want is to take a rookie like you into a real emergency.

**梁月**：好的。\
**Liang Yue**: I hope so, too.

**波蒂埃**：你该说“是的，波蒂埃教官”。\
**Poitier**: That's "Yes, ma'am." You got me?

**波蒂埃**：我知道你心里大概不服气，觉得像我这样草根出身的家伙居然敢对你这样的精英颐指气使。\
**Poitier**: You're probably thinking I'm trying to put you in your place, huh? That I'm just bossing you around.

**波蒂埃**：但你记住，尽管只是临时的——可无论如何，现在我就是你的教官。\
**Poitier**: But get off your high horse, princess. Cause as long as I'm your field instructor, you need to show some respect.

这是临行前同僚们教给她的“小技巧”。当你的学员大有来头时，要么选择巴结到底，要么必须在一开始就告诉对方：你不是好惹的。\
This is the "pro tip" her colleagues gave her before she left. If your trainee has powerful connections, you've got two choices: either make sure they know who's in charge from day one, or spend the rest of your day sucking up to them.

然而，她和她的同僚们似乎有些杞人忧天了。\
But it seems she and her colleagues were worrying over nothing.

**梁月**：我没有觉得不服气，波蒂埃教官。\
我很荣幸能够得到您的指点，希望您能够多指点。\
**Liang Yue**: But I don't have a horse, and I didn't think you were bossy. I'm honored to have you as my partner and field instructor. I look forward to learning under you.

**波蒂埃**：……哦？\
**Poitier**: Hmm?

这位“大有来头”的学员态度格外谦逊。波蒂埃狐疑的审视只得到了对方带着几分恰到好处的疑惑不解的坦然回望。\
Pretty humble coming from a big-shot cadet. Poitier narrows her eyes, only to be met with an earnest, slightly puzzled gaze.

**梁月**：波蒂埃教官？怎么了吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Is there something wrong with what I said, ma'am?

**波蒂埃**：倒是装得挺乖巧……或者真是个没脾气的怂包？不会吧？\
**Poitier**: Are you just that much of a pushover, or is this all an act?

**梁月**：抱歉，我没有听清，您说什么？\
**Liang Yue**: P-Pardon? I don't quite understand.

**波蒂埃**：我是说我们要处理的案子可能和精英小姐想象的不同，你最好做好准备。\
**Poitier**: Nothing. Just keep close. You never know what can happen with these cases.

波蒂埃按响街边一户人家的门铃，伴随着隔着门板传来越来越近的沉重脚步声，门在少女错愕的目光下被猛地掀开。\
They take their last few steps up to the door and ring the bell. Heavy footsteps approach from within, and the door is flung open with a bang.

**市民Ⅰ**：你们终于来了！\
你知道我等了多久吗？那些怪物又来了，就在那里！快做点什么！\
**Citizen I**: Oh, finally. Do you know how long I've been waiting? Those monsters are at it again. Do something.

如此“热情”的欢迎显然不在见习执夜人的意料之中。\
Such an "enthusiastic" welcome isn't exactly what the vigil cadet was expecting.

但当她下意识地转过头，却发现自己的教官早已退到了几个台阶下远离战场的有利地势。看来她需要独自应付这一切了。\
She turns her head, only to see her instructor comfortably positioned a few feet behind her. Looks like she'll have to handle this one on her own.

**梁月**：……请您冷静一些，女士。我们在这里，没有什么能够伤害您。\
**Liang Yue**: Um, please remain calm, ma'am. We're here now, and we won't let them hurt you.

**梁月**：我看到您报告说有魔精屡次闯入您的住宅中，您能描述一下袭击您的魔精的具体外形吗？它们一共有几只？\
**Liang Yue**: Am I correct that you reported there are critters that have broken into your house? Could you describe them for us? Do you have an idea how many?

**市民Ⅰ**：很多！它们有很多，那些该死的恶魔！\
**Citizen I**: I don't know. Like a ton, a bunch, two and a half butt-loads. I didn't stick around to count them.

即便是夹杂着愤怒与恐慌的歇斯底里，其中仍然存在着有效信息。\
见习执夜人略作思考，给出了自己的方案。\
Even among the woman's chaotic shouting, useful information can be extracted. Liáng quickly formulates a plan.

**梁月**：存在复数的危险对象……既然如此，波蒂埃教官，我提议我们分头行动。\
**Liang Yue**: So, there are many of them. Hmm, in that case, I suggest we split up, ma'am.

**梁月**：能否请您负责保护这位女士，将制服魔精的任务交给我？\
这里并不是野生的危险魔精会喜爱的环境，背后可能有人操控那些魔精。\
**Liang Yue**: You could stay here and keep the lady safe, and send me to take the critters down? Given we're in the city, I suspect them to be tamed, and it's possible that someone may be controlling them.

**梁月**：根据魔精的种类，我可以推断出操控它们的术法。如果是提线魔咒、拟影魔咒这类的神秘术，我们可以快速找出施术者——\
**Liang Yue**: Once we've established their type, we may be able to deduce the incantation that's controlling them. Some incantations can be easily traced, such as the Manipulation incantation or the Shadow incantation—

**市民Ⅰ**：它们来了！就在那里！\
**Citizen I**: Ahhh. Over there. There they are.

**梁月**：请躲到我身后去，女士！它们在哪——\
**Liang Yue**: Please stay behind me, ma'am. Where are ...

**梁月**：里……\
**Liang Yue**: ... are ... they ...?

摆出警戒姿态的少女僵在了原地，目光凝结在院子的角落。\
那里有几个胖乎乎的身影排着队，慢悠悠地转了出来。\
She freezes mid-step, her eyes locking onto a corner of the yard. From the shadows, a row of plump creatures waddles into view.

**慢慢吞**：呒——\
**Munchalo**: Mooo.

**梁月**：这是……慢慢吞……？\
**Liang Yue**: Is this ...?

**梁月**：由拉普拉斯科算中心背书的“新巴别塔”魔精公司培育出来的新品种魔精，体型中等偏大，但基本无攻击性。\
**Liang Yue**: This appears to be a Munchalo, a new breed of critter from the Ms. NewBabel Critter Rehabilitation Center, endorsed by the LSCC. They're medium to large in size, and classed as non-aggressive.

**梁月**：它们会缓慢地吃下各种神秘学材料，并在萃取其中的能量后将其排出体外，现在世界各地的魔精牧场中都开始大范围养殖……\
**Liang Yue**: The Munchalo consumes base arcane materials and extracts the energy from them. They're intended to assist in the arcane production industry. They've been slated for worldwide distribution.

**梁月**：但它们为什么会出现在这里？\
**Liang Yue**: But, why are they here?

**市民Ⅰ**：不要光傻站着了，做点什么！快把它们给我杀掉！\
**Citizen I**: Well? What are you waiting for? Do something. Kill them, ah!

**梁月**：杀掉？可是女士，它们并不会攻击人。\
我想“杀掉”是有些反应过度的，这也不符合我们的操作流程。\
**Liang Yue**: Kill them? Oh, ma'am. Please don't worry. They will not attack people, and it's against our procedures to kill non-aggressive critters without authorization.

**市民Ⅰ**：但它们在攻击我好不容易修整好的草坪！还嚼碎了我的花盆和台阶！\
我的小甜心都让这群傻大个给咬秃了尾巴！\
**Citizen I**: But they're destroying my azaleas. And the stairs and my lawn. And they almost bit my sweetie's tail off, ah.

饶是始终一本正经的见习执夜人少女似乎也因为这个答案而语塞了片刻。\
Even the ever-composed vigil cadet is momentarily at a loss for words.

**梁月**：您的小甜心是指……不，我是说我明白了，女士。\
我会将它们赶出去的——\
**Liang Yue**: Your sweetie? Um, I see, ma'am. I will do my best to get them out—

见习执夜人少女决定暂时不再深究“小甜心”的真面目。\
但她的话并没能说完，便被一道从院子外飞进来的尖叫声打断了。\
She decides to put off investigating "sweetie's" identity for now. But before she can act, a shrill voice interrupts from outside the yard.

**市民Ⅱ**：不！你敢碰一下我的心肝宝贝试试！\
**Citizen II**: Hey! Don't you dare lay a finger on my precious munchies.

**梁月**：什——先生，您又是谁？\
**Liang Yue**: Wha—Can I help you, sir?

**市民Ⅰ**：隔壁的厚颜无耻的混蛋！就是这个怪咖养了这群臭烘烘的傻大个！\
警察小姐，请把他和他的恶心宠物一起丢到监狱里去！\
**Citizen I**: I-I knew it. This jerk is my next-door neighbor. He keeps all kinds of these ridiculous, smelly critters around. I order you to throw him and all his disgusting little pets in jail.

**市民Ⅱ**：你这个疯子，它们只是一群可爱的慢慢吞，你为什么要和它们计较？\
你那恶毒的心灵里难道没有哪怕一小块柔软的部分吗？\
**Citizen II**: Are you out of your mind? They're just some adorable Munchalos. What kind of sicko would wanna hurt them?

他们开始隔着围墙争吵起来，越加不堪入耳的词汇开始被填充上膛，街区沐浴在让人眉头直皱的枪林弹雨之中。\
The shouting match quickly escalates as a barrage of increasingly colorful insults fills the air.

**梁月**：………………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

梁月看向自己的教官。波蒂埃好整以暇地向她耸了耸肩。\
Liáng glances at her instructor. Poitier simply smirks and shrugs.

**波蒂埃**：我说了，你最好“做好准备”。\
**Poitier**: What did I tell you, huh?

**慢慢吞**：呒——\
**Munchalo**: Mooo.

**波蒂埃**：终于，午餐时间！\
我绝对会点一份芝士汉堡，再加一杯黑咖啡。\
**Poitier**: Finally, lunchtime. I'll grab the cheeseburger and an Americano—large.

波蒂埃推开餐馆的大门，熟门熟路地带着自己的学员来到吧台处点餐。\
The front door to the diner has barely closed by the time Poitier has shouted out her order. It seems this is just another part of a beat cop's routine.

**波蒂埃**：一起魔精非法入侵、一起炼金术事故、一起狼人诅咒感染者扰民的投诉，还有一个驾驶未报备的神秘学物品在道路上超速行驶的……\
**Poitier**: So, some fluffy trespassers, an alchemy incident, a noise complaint for a werewolf-infected, and a speeding ticket on an unregistered arcane vehicle ...

**波蒂埃**：这个上午比我预想中的忙碌，但也比我预想中的顺利。\
我想不论是你还是我，都应当获得一份美味的午餐。你要什么？\
**Poitier**: Honestly, busier than I expected, but it all went smoother than I expected too. We've earned ourselves a decent lunch, I'd say. So, what do you want, princess?

黑发少女盯着墙上的菜单看了一会儿，迟迟没有给出回答。\
Liáng studies the menu on the wall, hesitating to answer.

**波蒂埃**：……怎么，不合你的口味？\
**Poitier**: What? Don't tell me our little vigil princess can't stomach a bit of fast food?

**波蒂埃**：那还真是抱歉了，但我们的午休时间有限，通常只能在这种小餐馆解决。\
**Poitier**: Better get used to it, kid. We're on a tight schedule. There's no time for fancy dining.

**梁月**：不是的，我没有什么忌口。只是……这边的餐厅都是这个价格吗？\
我刚刚来到洛杉矶，它比我想象的要贵一些。\
**Liang Yue**: Oh, it's not that. It's just ... Are all the restaurants here so expensive? This is the first time I've been to L.A., and it seems things cost more than I expected.

这个答案显然不在波蒂埃的意料之内。\
Poitier is taken aback.

**波蒂埃**：……你还需要担心钱的问题？\
我听说你的工资是基金会那边发，大名鼎鼎的基金会难道其实那么吝啬吗？\
**Poitier**: What, you broke? You telling me the Foundation—THE FOUNDATION—can't afford to pay you a decent wage?

**梁月**：不是的，夜巡特遣给我们发的补助是够用的，不过……\
我最初还以为能够存下一些，但现在看来是我太贪心了。\
**Liang Yue**: Oh, no. No. It's ... My subsidy should be enough for daily necessities. It's only that I was hoping to save some money, but it seems the prices here won't allow me to.

**梁月**：抱歉，请您忘了我刚才说的吧。\
我想我要一份三明治就可以了。\
**Liang Yue**: Sorry, please forget it. I'll have a chicken sandwich. Thank you.

**波蒂埃**：……行。\
**Poitier**: Okay.

二人点过餐后，在波蒂埃的老位置坐下。\
Their orders placed, the two take a seat at Poitier's usual spot.

**波蒂埃**：好吧……看来我对你有一些误解。\
**Poitier**: Alright, question time, rookie. Cause I think I've got the wrong impression.

**波蒂埃**：我之前还以为你是个有钱人家的大小姐之类的，毕竟我们听说了一些事——关于你的家族。\
**Poitier**: What I heard was that you were some pampered rich kid from a crazy old legendary family.

梁月在片刻的惊讶后，很快露出了了然的神情，就好像她早已预料到，或是早已习惯了这类疑问。\
After a brief flicker of surprise, Liáng's expression shifts. It's as if she expected to hear this question, or at least has grown accustomed to it.

**梁月**：梁家的确有着很长时间的历史，我的祖先中也确实出过不少令人景仰的人物。\
**Liang Yue**: It's true. The Liáng family have a long history and many legendary ancestors.

**梁月**：但那些都是很久以前的事了，到了我们这一代，梁家基本上和普通的人家没有什么区别。\
**Liang Yue**: But that was a long time ago. Nowadays, we're not so different from any other ordinary family.

**波蒂埃**：一个没落的古老家族这可不叫作“和普通人没两样”，至少我身边没有这种普通家庭。\
**Poitier**: Mhm, sure. "Ordinary," that's definitely what I think of when I see you.

**波蒂埃**：我们都听说了，你有个厉害的“好帮手”。\
**Poitier**: I also heard that you've got a familiar.

**梁月**：您是说“强梁”？\
**Liang Yue**: You mean Qiángliáng?

**波蒂埃**：一只来自遥远东方的强大神秘学生物——科里的所有人都对它很是好奇，我当然也不例外。\
**Poitier**: Yeah, sure, that. Come on. It's some mysterious arcane creature from the Far East. Everyone in the DAA's curious about it, myself included.

**波蒂埃**：放出来看看？\
**Poitier**: So, you gonna show me?

黑发女孩露出为难的神色。\
Liáng looks a little troubled.

**梁月**：现在吗？\
抱歉，波蒂埃教官。我想我不能这么做。\
**Liang Yue**: Um, now? I'm sorry, but I must refuse your request, Ms. Poitier.

**梁月**：您可能不太了解，在我的故乡，强梁是备受尊敬的神圣存在。\
**Liang Yue**: With all due respect, the Qiángliáng is a sacred being. It is deserving of great respect.

**梁月**：它肩负着驱除鬼怪、疫病以及其他邪恶存在的使命，从古至今无数次为了守护人世间的安宁挺身而出。\
**Liang Yue**: It has a divine mission to expel diseases and evil beings and has guarded the world through the ages.

**梁月**：这不是传说故事，而是事实。\
强梁的每一次战斗都会被记录在梁家的典籍之中。\
**Liang Yue**: Maybe that just sounds like old legends, but it's the truth. We've recorded every battle it fought in our family chronicles.

**梁月**：但另一方面，只有遇到人力无法对抗的危机时，我们才被允许召唤强梁、借助这只古老神兽的力量。\
**Liang Yue**: And we're only allowed to borrow its power when we are in the greatest of danger.

**梁月**：我不能仅仅为了向人展示它的英姿就将它唤出，还请您谅解。\
**Liang Yue**: Please understand that I can't just summon it simply to show it to others.

**波蒂埃**：……不行就算了，我也不是那种蛮不讲理的人，你不必说那么一大串的。\
**Poitier**: Okay, okay. I'm not unreasonable, princess. If it's a sacred thing or whatever, I won't bother you over it.

少女言辞诚恳，因此尽管要求被拒绝，波蒂埃也并未因此恼火，只觉得对方一板一眼的回答颇为无趣。\
From Liáng's sincerity, it's clear that this isn't just an excuse. Poitier isn't annoyed by it, but she does seem a little bored by the overly serious response.

相对无言，餐桌被尴尬的沉默笼罩，直到服务生端上二人的午餐。\
An awkward silence falls at the table. Luckily, the waitress breaks it with the arrival of their meals.

**波蒂埃**：不过说真的，你的表现比我想象中的好。\
我很少夸人的，你可以稍微骄傲一些。\
**Poitier**: Anyway, I guess I should say, you're doing a lot better than I thought today. And I don't just give out compliments, you got that? So, take some pride in it.

**波蒂埃**：但可不要以为这就是全部了，这份工作的困难程度远超你的想象。\
**Poitier**: But don't get cocky either. This was all chump work. You haven't seen the ugly side of this job yet.

**波蒂埃**：看着大多是些鸡毛蒜皮的小事，但稍有疏忽就会倒大霉，你不会想要体验那种滋味的。\
**Poitier**: This morning might have been a cakewalk. But this job can blindside you just like that. Never underestimate anything.

波蒂埃一边大口咬着汉堡，一边对自己带的第一个新人滔滔不绝了起来。\
但对方却始终没有回应。\
She takes a hefty bite of her burger and launches into a monologue, the food still rolling around in her mouth. Liáng simply looks blank. Poitier finally swallows.

**波蒂埃**：……你怎么不说话？\
**Poitier**: Hey? You in there, princess?

**梁月**：请原谅，我的家中一直要求“食不言寝不语”，意思是吃饭和睡觉的时候不该说话。\
**Liang Yue**: I apologize, but in our family, we have a rule, Shí Bù Yán, Qǐn Bù Yǔ. It means we believe you shouldn't talk when eating or sleeping.

**波蒂埃**：你是在借口讥讽我没有教养，还是——天哪，你是认真的。\
**Poitier**: What? You're kidding! You trying to say I'm being rude? Or wait, you're serious, aren't you?

对面一本正经的表情否认了波蒂埃最初的推测。\
她不敢置信地看向坐在桌子对面的少女，就像是在看一个外星人。\
Liáng sits totally still, her expression unchanged.

**波蒂埃**：那是哪门子的鬼扯规矩？我家在吃饭的时候就从来没有安静过。\
**Poitier**: What kind of stupid rule is that?

**波蒂埃**：再说……睡觉的时候怎么说话？说梦话？\
这是能想不说就不说的吗？\
**Poitier**: Besides, why would anyone be talking while they're asleep? What, like you can't sleep talk? How do you even control that?

面对这个问题，坐在她对面的少女似乎认真思索了一番。\
Poitier appears to be giving the question some genuine thought.

**梁月**：您说得对，是我的翻译有纰漏。\
那句话更准确的意思是“在到了该睡觉的时间后，我们就应该保持安静”。\
**Liang Yue**: Sorry, maybe I didn't translate it right. It means "keep quiet before sleep."

**波蒂埃**：…………\
**Poitier**: ...

波蒂埃瞠目结舌了半晌，最终瘫软在了座位上。\
For a long moment, Poitier stares at her, dumbfounded. Then, she slumps back in her seat.

**波蒂埃**：天哪……可怜的家伙，你也太无趣了。\
我都已经能够想象到你的童年是什么样的了。\
**Poitier**: The heck? So many rules. Damn, princess, you must've had a miserable childhood.

**波蒂埃**：每天安排各种课程和训练，家里的管教比监狱还严，不论是什么小说电影动画片统统碰都没碰过，对不对？\
**Poitier**: Let me guess. Every day was courses and training, stuck inside, no books, no movies. Did they even let you watch Saturday morning cartoons? I've heard of kids like you. Sounds worse than jail to me.

**波蒂埃**：这不行，这可不行啊。不论是对你的生活来说，还是对工作来说。\
**Poitier**: A childhood like that is rough, kid. It's bad for your head. Bad for the job, too.

少女似乎完全不能理解波蒂埃的崩溃，她皱起了眉头。\
Liáng furrows her brow a little. She can't follow her thought process at all.

**梁月**：我不明白您在诧异什么……您说的“对工作来说”是什么意思？\
**Liang Yue**: I don't understand why you're upset, Ms. Poitier. How is it bad for the job?

**波蒂埃**：比如你看到那个等待我们处理的“基础神秘学警情”清单了吧？\
其中有一项，是一个在唐人街拍戏的电影导演疑似受到人身威胁的事件。\
**Poitier**: Did you check the list of incidents before we set off? There's a case we're going to after lunch. A director that received some kind of threat. She's shooting a film in Chinatown.

**波蒂埃**：虽然目前还没有出事，但她拍的电影涉及神秘学元素，她本人也是神秘学家，所以这个案子就被划给了我们。\
**Poitier**: Anyways, this director's an arcanist, and her movie is all about arcanum. So, it's in our department.

**波蒂埃**：你要是懂电影，事情就会好办一些，毕竟对工作中涉及到的人员总是了解越多越好，那还是个很有名的导演呢。\
**Poitier**: The point is, knowing's half the battle in this job. It'd be easier if you were a cinephile or at least familiar with films. Maybe then you'd know a thing or two about her.

**波蒂埃**：就是“针人”那个混蛋模仿的、十年前火遍世界各地的那部“第一部将真正的神秘术搬上银幕”的电影，《神秘警探C07》的导演。\
**Poitier**: She's famous for those Detective C07 films, the first movies to really put a focus on arcanum and arcanists. Something about it, though: the detective in those films used a skill a lot like this Nightpiercer crook.

**波蒂埃**：我记得是叫菲林……菲林……\
**Poitier**: What's her name again? Something with an N? Nu ...

波蒂埃努力挖掘记忆中的那个往往只在电影开头或是结尾一闪而过的名字，因此忽略了对面少女脸上一闪而过的惊讶表情。\
Poitier strains to recall the name. She only saw it flash on screen for a moment when she watched the film way back when. In her focus, she fails to notice the flash of surprise on Liáng's face.

**梁月**：菲林士多。\
**Liang Yue**: Noire.

**波蒂埃**：没错，就是这个名字！\
**Poitier**: Yeah. That's it.

**波蒂埃**：等等，所以你……\
**Poitier**: Wait, so you—

**梁月**：我也是会看电影的。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, I've watched her movies, too.

**波蒂埃**：哇哦，这可真是出乎我的意料。\
是那种你拿了满分试卷回家的奖励吗？又或是——\
**Poitier**: I'll be damned. So, was it a special reward for getting straight A's? Or—

**调度中心**：呼叫附近警员，市政大厅发生人质劫持事件。\
**Dispatch Center**: Calling all nearby units. Code 3. We have a hostage situation at City Hall.

忽然响起的通信打断了波蒂埃饶有兴趣的追问。\
The radio announcement cuts their get-to-know-you session short.

**调度中心**：嫌疑犯为登记神秘学家，已使用神秘术造成人身威胁，现场警员请求神秘学人员增援，3级警情。\
**Dispatch Center**: Suspect is a registered arcanist, posing a threat to life. On-scene officers are requesting immediate arcanist support.

**梁月**：市政大厅……我记得地图，那就是这附近。\
**Liang Yue**: City Hall? We're close by, aren't we?

**波蒂埃**：看来我们的午餐时间要结束了。\
**Poitier**: Pack up. Lunchtime's over.

## SC-03 秩序与失衡 / Order and Chaos

**老警察**：嘿，冷静点！即使你那么做也无济于事的！\
**Old Police Officer**: Let go of the hostage, sir. This won't do you any good.

**男子**：滚开！！\
**Enraged Man**: Go away!!

**老警察**：该死！\
**Old Police Officer**: Damn!

**老警察**：好险……那群神秘学犯罪科的还没来吗？！\
**Old Police Officer**: That was close! Where's our backup?

**波蒂埃**：随时为您服务，我们来了。\
**Poitier**: DAA, at your service.

**梁月**：情况怎么样了？\
**Liang Yue**: What's the situation?

**老警察**：你们看就知道了。\
**Old Police Officer**: See for yourself.

本应人来人往的市政大厅如今格外空阔，原因一目了然。\
The City Hall, usually bustling with foot traffic, now stands eerily empty. The reason is immediately clear.

**男子**：别过来！退后，都退后！\
**Enraged Man**: Don't come any closer! Stay back! Stay back!!

**人质**：不要杀我，求你了！\
我可以向你道歉，好吗？我真的很抱歉！\
**Hostage**: Please! Don't kill me! I'm sorry, I really am! Please let me go!

**男子**：闭嘴！事到如今已经太迟了，你再说一句话我就杀了你！\
——都退后！！\
**Enraged Man**: Shut up! It's too late now. Say another word, and you're dead! Stay back!!

挟持了人质的男子晃动着手中的利刃，发出愤怒的咆哮。\
He swings the blade in his hand wildly, his voice a furious, panicked snarl.

远远站在警戒网之外的围观群众中，都有不少人都情不自禁地后退了数步——但身处仅距离男子十步前后的女子，却丝毫不为所动。\
The crowd on the other side of the police barricade instinctively recoils, but the woman standing just ten paces away doesn't move an inch.

**？？？**：不，相信我，先生。\
**???**: Hey, hey. Trust me, pal.

**？？？**：您不会想要那样做的。\
**???**: You really don't want to do this.

**波蒂埃**：那是谁？\
看着不像是我们的人。\
**Poitier**: Who's that? Doesn't look like one of ours.

**老警察**：是个事发时在现场的普通民众。\
在我们赶到之前，她帮忙稳住了犯人的情绪。\
**Old Police Officer**: Just some civvy. She was talking with the suspect before we got here.

**梁月**：那个人……\
**Liang Yue**: That woman ...

**波蒂埃**：你认识？\
**Poitier**: What, you know her? Look familiar or something?

**梁月**：不……我想应该是我记错了。\
**Liang Yue**: No. Just a thought. It's nothing.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

她们关注的对象似乎注意到了此处的交谈，不着痕迹地向梁月与波蒂埃的方向望了一眼。\
The woman glances toward the officers, seeming to notice their conversation.

**？？？**：……有些错误一旦犯下就再也无法挽回，弄脏双手后，你将永远失去站在阳光下的资格。\
**???**: People make mistakes. But some mistakes can't be undone. Don't put that blood on your hands, or it'll never wash off.

**？？？**：在那里的那个男人，真的值得你舍弃这一切吗？\
**???**: Is hurting this guy worth all that pain and guilt?

**？？？**：他迟早会受到应有的惩罚，我向你保证。\
**???**: Sooner or later, he'll get what's coming to him for what he's done. I promise you that.

神秘女子的话语似乎对男子生了效，他逐渐露出痛苦挣扎的神色，手上的刀子有所晃动。\
Her words seem to have an effect. The hostage-taker hesitates, his face contorted in pain, his grip on the knife faltering.

**男子**：我……但是我必须……！\
**Enraged Man**: But, but, I must ...

**波蒂埃**：很好，他的注意力分散了。\
菜鸟，到我们出场的时候了！\
**Poitier**: He's distracted. Rookie, time for us to take him down!

**梁月**：您最好不要乱动，先生！\
**Liang Yue**: Please stand down, sir.

人高马大的劫犯最终被比他矮了一个头的少女警探按在了地上。\
其他警员们一拥而上，很快将劫犯铐了起来。\
Although almost half his size, Liáng manages to pin the suspect to the ground. The other officers swarm in, snapping handcuffs around his wrists before he can put up another fight.

**老警察**：嫌疑犯已被控制，重复，嫌疑犯已被控制，不需要后续支援。\
**Old Police Officer**: Suspect under control. I repeat, suspect under control. No further backup needed.

看来他们的任务告一段落了。\
Looks like this case is wrapped up.

**波蒂埃**：……身手不错。\
但真可惜，我还以为终于能够一睹你那位“密友”的真容呢。\
**Poitier**: Nice moves. I was kinda hoping we'd get to see that familiar of yours, though.

**梁月**：对付这种普通的嫌犯并不需要动用到强梁，在我力所能及的方寸之内，我会靠自己解决。\
**Liang Yue**: A simple threat like this isn't worthy of Qiángliáng. I have to reserve its assistance unless absolutely necessary.

**波蒂埃**：这也是你家里的教诲吗？\
还是说驱使它需要额外的代价？\
**Poitier**: So, is this just another one of those rules? Or, do you mean its help comes with a price tag?

**梁月**：……二者皆是。\
**Liang Yue**: Both.

少女有些惊讶地睁大了眼睛。波蒂埃的敏锐出乎了她的意料。\
Despite the curtness of her response, her eyes widen a little at Poitier's astuteness.

但简短的回答后，梁月却不再做进一步的解释，似乎不愿多说。\
这让波蒂埃感到了不满。\
Poitier scowls.

**波蒂埃**：就这样？\
**Poitier**: That it?

**梁月**：您指什么？\
**Liang Yue**: What do you mean?

**波蒂埃**：我是指当你开口时，讨论的似乎总是我们的职责和你的家族使命之类的。\
不是说这是坏事，但你似乎从来不说你对每件事情的感受。\
**Poitier**: I mean, so far, every time you talk about the job or your family rules, it's just the surface-level stuff. How do you actually feel about any of this?

少女似乎颇为不解。\
Liáng looks genuinely confused.

**梁月**：我的感受？\
抱歉……但我不太明白讨论这个话题的必要性。\
**Liang Yue**: How I feel? I-I don't understand why it would be necessary to mention that.

**波蒂埃**：当然有必要了。我们可是搭档，我可不想和心里不知道在想什么的家伙并排坐在警车里。\
**Poitier**: Cause we're partners, kid. We've got to trust each other. How am I gonna let you watch my six if I don't even know how you tick?

但对方似乎仍然没有理解她的意思。\
这名年轻的见习执夜人眼神中依然写着疑惑。\
But Liáng still doesn't seem to get it.

**梁月**：是的。在我于洛杉矶神秘学犯罪科实习期间，您是我的搭档兼教官。\
**Liang Yue**: I see. You're my partner and instructor during my assignment with the LAPD Division of Arcane Affairs.

**梁月**：我会学习您的经验，牢记您的教诲，完成我的工作并通过最终的考核。\
我不会给您添麻烦或拖后腿的。\
**Liang Yue**: So, I will do my best to learn from you and complete my work as assigned. I won't slow you down.

**波蒂埃**：不，我不是说那个——该死，算了！\
当我没说吧。\
**Poitier**: That's not what I'm—Urgh. Forget it.

**梁月**：……？\
**Liang Yue**: ...?

梁月的潜台词仿佛在说“自己的想法并不重要”，这让波蒂埃心中恼火，但对方油盐不进的模样又让她无处发泄。\
Liáng's tone all but says, "My personal feelings don't matter." Poitier gives up trying to argue with someone with such a stubborn, unreadable demeanor.

围绕着二人的空气变得扎人。\
幸亏在事情变得更糟之前，从一旁凑上来的青年闯入了这令人窒息的空间。\
She simply stares at her, quietly seething to herself. Luckily, before things can spiral further, the hostage cuts through the tension.

**人质**：谢天谢地，以及谢谢你，可爱的小姐！\
那个家伙真是疯了！\
**Hostage**: Oh, thank God you took down that lunatic. I'm really grateful, Miss.

**人质**：看你小小年纪，可真是了不起。你是神秘学犯罪科的警官吗？\
但你的制服看起来似乎有些不同，我想我见过它……是夜巡特遣，对吗？\
**Hostage**: But, ain't you a bit young to be an Arcane Affairs Officer? I think I've seen that uniform somewhere else before. You're a vigil, right?

**梁月**：是的，先生——等等。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, sir. Wait.

梁月忽然咽下了未尽的话语，狐疑地盯着刚刚亲手解救出来的人质的面孔。\
Liáng swallows the rest of her words as she stares at the hostage she just rescued, her expression suddenly wary.

**梁月**：我见过你。\
**Liang Yue**: I know you.

**梁月**：通过电话作案的神秘学家诈骗犯“棍骗约翰”落网，他用专属神秘术“唯命是从”控制受害者向自己的账户汇入大笔金钱。\
**Liang Yue**: The arcanist scammer, Johnny Three-Times, has been apprehended. Using his arcane skill "Omnis Obeisance," he manipulated his victims to do anything he asked, specifically, transferring all their money to him.

**梁月**：你是那个神秘学家诈骗犯“棍骗约翰”！\
**Liang Yue**: You're that scammer, Johnny Three-Times.

**棍骗约翰**：哎呦……看来这就是上过报纸的坏处了。\
**Johnny Three-Times**: Oopsie. Guess that's the downside of getting your name in the papers.

**波蒂埃**：什么？\
等等，可“棍骗约翰”不是被抓了吗，为什么会出现在这里？\
**Poitier**: What? Didn't we already book that guy? What's he doing here?

**老警察**：因为这个家伙骗来的钱一直没有追回来，让他给藏起来了。\
**Old Police Officer**: He got a sweetheart deal. A reduced sentence in exchange for revealing where he stashed all the dough he stole.

**老警察**：他要求以把钱还回来作为条件，申请减刑。\
那也包含政府的一大笔钱，不是个小数目……所以上面的人答应了。\
**Old Police Officer**: And it was a s**tload of money too, apparently from some big donors to the mayor's re-election campaign.

**老警察**：这次放这个人渣出来，就是让他指认藏钱的地方。\
没想到半路有人袭击了押送的警员，把他给绑到了这里。\
**Old Police Officer**: Of course, he demanded he be present for the unveiling of his stash. So, they brought him here. That's when this loony attacked the police escort and took him hostage.

**棍骗约翰**：哎哟！轻点啊，警官。\
只是戴个手铐，抓得那么用力做什么？\
**Johnny Three-Times**: Hey, easy, officer. You've already got me. No need to be so rough with the cuffs.

**老警察**：闭嘴，你这个渣滓！\
**Old Police Officer**: Clam it, Johnny.

**波蒂埃**：……早知道刚才就让这家伙死了算了。\
**Poitier**: We should've just let that guy ice him.

**梁月**：等等，那么刚才那个要杀他的人……难道是？\
**Liang Yue**: May I ask, officer, do we know if the man trying to kill him was—

**老警察**：一个受害者家属。被骗钱的是他妈妈，七十多岁的老太太，发现被骗后承受不住……没救回来。\
**Old Police Officer**: Yeah, he's the son of a victim. This bastard took his mom for all she was worth, and when she found out—boom—heart attack.

老警员叹息着摇了摇头，但一旁的“棍骗约翰”却嗤笑了一声。\
He shakes his head, heaving a weary sigh. Johnny Three-Times snickers.

**棍骗约翰**：那人和他家老太婆一样，不仅脑袋不好使，还没有自己是个傻瓜的自知之明。\
**Johnny Three-Times**: Ha. Like mother, like son. He was just as dumb as his doddering old mom. Worse even, cause he didn't even catch wise to it.

**棍骗约翰**：丛林里弱肉强食靠的是力量，而在钢筋水泥的城市里优胜劣汰靠的是脑子。\
**Johnny Three-Times**: It's a concrete jungle, baby, and it follows jungle rules. Survival of the fittest. Crap for brains here never had a chance.

**棍骗约翰**：没有我，他那老太婆也会叫别人骗了。\
再说只是被骗走几个钱就把自己的命整没了，要我说也真是搞笑得很。\
**Johnny Three-Times**: If it wasn't me, it woulda been someone else. What a joke! Imagine keeling over just cause you lost a bit of cash.

**棍骗约翰**：这种人永远不会学习教训，永远不会用脑子。\
他也不想想，把我弄死了，他老太婆给骗走的钱从哪里找回来——\
**Johnny Three-Times**: Then we've got this dumbass, coming at me with even less of a brain. Think about it. If he killed me, how's he gonna get his money back?

**波蒂埃**：闭嘴吧，你这个混球！\
**Poitier**: Shut the f**k up, asshole!

一记重拳凿进了棍骗约翰的腹部，他抽搐着蜷缩在地。\
She levels a punch to his gut, sending him crumpling to the ground, gasping for air.

**棍骗约翰**：——呃？！\
**Johnny Three-Times**: UGH!

**梁月**：波蒂埃教官？！\
您在做什么？\
**Liang Yue**: Officer Poitier, what are you doing?

**波蒂埃**：你看了还不明白？当然是给这个自命不凡的畜生一点教训。\
**Poitier**: What? I'm teaching this douchebag a lesson.

**梁月**：我们不能这么做，这是违反规定的。\
**Liang Yue**: But we can't do that. It's against the rules.

见习执夜人坚定地挡在了棍骗约翰的身前，波蒂埃因此不得不停下了动作。\
Liáng steps between the two, blocking Poitier from doing any more.

**棍骗约翰**：咳咳……看来执夜人就是比普通的神秘学警察更明白事理。\
你说对吗，警官？\
**Johnny Three-Times**: *cough* Well, I guess the Vigiles are a cut above the trash when it comes to the DAA. Am I right?

少女那副义正辞严的模样，和身后棍骗约翰小人得志的嘴脸，让波蒂埃深吸了一口气才压住了心中的怒火。\
Poitier takes a deep breath as she tries to rein in her frustration.

**波蒂埃**：啧……轮不到你来教我什么是对什么是错，菜鸟。\
**Poitier**: Let's get this straight, rookie. You don't tell me what to do.

**波蒂埃**：我最讨厌的就是像你这样的家伙了。\
只会高高在上地说些冠冕堂皇的大道理，总以为自己是最正确的那个。\
**Poitier**: I should've known. You're just the worst kind of cop—Everything by the book, sticking to your high-and-mighty principles like you know what's best.

她的教官冷哼一声，别过头走开了。\
She lets out a frosty huff and turns away.

**梁月**：…………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

**女孩**：梁月！你为什么要告诉老师？\
**Girl**: Liáng Yuè! How dare you rat us out?

**梁月**：因为……因为你们那么做是不对的。\
**Liang Yue**: Be-Because you did something wrong.

**女孩**：告密精！你不来就算了，为什么要让老师知道？\
**Girl**: Then you're a rat. I didn't really care if you wanted to come along, but now you go and snitch on us?

**男孩**：我早说了，就不应该叫她。\
**Boy**: I told you we shouldn't have invited her.

**梁月**：等等，别走——\
**Liang Yue**: Wait, don't go.

**梁月**：我——\
**Liang Yue**: I—

梁月开口，刚想要说些什么——在她的目光落在波蒂埃身后大厅的另一角时，忽然止住了话头。\
The clamor of fearful voices cuts her off.

**青年警察**：——我的天哪！快来人阻止他！\
**Young Police Officer**: No. Somebody stop him.

## SC-04 降邪 / Exorcism

**棍骗约翰**：不要过来，救命、救命！\
**Johnny Three-Times**: Stay back!! Help me! Help!!!

市政大厅再一次陷入了混乱，棍骗约翰尖叫着仓皇逃命，试图远离身后的煞星。\
The City Hall has been plunged back into chaos. Johnny lets out a shriek, scrambling to get as far away as possible.

**男子**：让开！\
**Enraged Man**: Get away!

**青年警察**：呃……！\
**Young Police Officer**: Urgh!

男子用鲜血淋漓的双手，将试图阻拦他的警员抛到一旁——那是他挣脱手铐时，掰断自己的拇指流下的血。\
He hurls the officer aside. Blood drips down his fingers from the thumb he broke to slip his hand out of his cuffs.

他有如鬼神附体，不知从哪里得来了一股怪力，数个警员一拥而上，竟然也被他轻松撞开。\
He moves with inhuman strength, fighting off the approaching officers with ease.

**男子**：不要挡我的路！那个王八蛋……我要杀了你，我要杀了你！\
**Enraged Man**: Out of my way! I will kill you! I will kill you all!

**波蒂埃**：该死，那老兄是怎么回事？！\
**Poitier**: Damn it! Is this dude high or something?

**梁月**：他的样子看起来明显不对劲！\
那是……\
**Liang Yue**: No, no. I don't think this is drugs.

**梁月**：某种神秘术，和……某种邪祟之物的气息。\
**Liang Yue**: It's an arcane skill. I sense some kind of evil spirit.

**梁月**：——波蒂埃教官，我想我能让那位先生停下来！\
**Liang Yue**: I think I can stop him, ma'am.

方才的不愉快已经被二人抛在了脑后。\
事态紧急，波蒂埃立刻点了头。\
The tension between them has been totally forgotten. The situation is urgent. Poitier gives a sharp nod.

**波蒂埃**：好吧，虽然我不知道你说的“邪祟之物”究竟是个什么——但如果你觉得能做些什么的话，就快做！\
**Poitier**: Fine. Whatever it is, and whatever you think you can do, do it.

**梁月**：明白。\
这正是我的使命所在。\
**Liang Yue**: I will. This is my duty.

梁月郑重点了点头，向大厅中央的男子跑去。\
Liáng gives a firm nod before rushing toward the suspect.

**男子**：我要杀了这个人渣。杀了他，杀了他……\
**Enraged Man**: Kill ... I must kill this bastard.

**男子**：谁？！\
**Enraged Man**: Who are you?!

**梁月**：请您不要紧张，先生。我身上没有武器。\
**Liang Yue**: Please stay calm, sir. I have no weapon.

**梁月**：我只是想要请您听一通电话。\
**Liang Yue**: I'm just here to make a phone call.

**男子**：什么？……电话？\
**Enraged Man**: What? A phone call?

**梁月**：是的。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes.

**梁月**：一通电话。\
**Liang Yue**: And you're going to make it.

**男子**：……电话那边是谁？\
**Enraged Man**: Who are you dialing?

**梁月**：请不要着急，我现在拨通它。\
**Liang Yue**: You'll soon find out.

**梁月**：强梁既出，罔有不韪。斩杀凶咎——枭截不祥！\
**Liang Yue**: Arise Qiángliáng, swift and fierce! Banish all evil and cleanse this place!

**男子**：不！不……！\
我的头……呃啊啊——\
**Enraged Man**: No! No! My head! Ugh!

**男子**：对不起，妈……对不起……\
**Enraged Man**: I'm so sorry, Mama.

男子在留下几句模糊不清的呢喃低语后栽倒在地。\
周围的警员心有余悸，一时仍然不敢靠近。\
With one last garbled whisper, the man collapses. The officers around him remain frozen, still too wary to approach.

**青年警察**：……我们还要给他上手铐吗？\
**Young Police Officer**: Should we cuff him?

**梁月**：我来吧。\
但我想比起警察局，我们应该先送他去医院进行一番彻底的检查。\
**Liang Yue**: Allow me. But I believe we should bring him to the hospital to be checked over immediately.

**老警察**：那么他能交给你们吗？我们还得照看那个家伙。\
**Old Police Officer**: Think you can handle him? We got this conman to take care of.

梁月顺着年长警官所指的方向看去。\
She follows the older officer's gaze.

不久前还不可一世的棍骗约翰此刻瘫软在地，细看还会发现他身着的下装有一片不自然的深色印记。\
Not long ago, Johnny Three-Times was brimming with arrogance. Now, he is a crumpled heap on the floor. A dark stain has formed on the crotch of his pants.

**波蒂埃**：天呐，真是个没胆的窝囊废。\
**Poitier**: God, what a loser.

波蒂埃冷笑一声摇了摇头后，便收回了目光。\
随后她犹豫片刻，最终将视线投向了梁月。\
Poitier sneers, shaking her head as she turns away. She hesitates, then shifts her gaze to Liáng.

**波蒂埃**：你知道我想说什么，就是……那个，你知道的吧？\
**Poitier**: So, uh, y-you know what I'm about to say, right?

**梁月**：……？\
**Liang Yue**: ...?

回应波蒂埃的是一张满是疑问的面孔。\
好吧，这也不能怪对方。\
Liáng looks visibly confused, although more understandably this time.

**波蒂埃**：好了……我很抱歉！\
这就是我想说的。\
**Poitier**: Okay. I'm sorry. Is that what you want? For me to say it? Sorry.

**波蒂埃**：我同情那个伙计，但也没有帮上什么忙。如果不是你，我们就真的只有击毙他了，而这可不是我想看到的。\
**Poitier**: I felt bad for that guy, but there was nothing we could do for him while he was possessed. If it weren't for you, we might've shot him.

**波蒂埃**：我刚才说了点难听的话，你就忘了吧。\
你帮了大忙——做得好。\
**Poitier**: Well done, Vigil Liáng. And please just forget what I said. I was out of line.

她一气呵成地说完了这番话，别过头去不想看对方的表情。\
然而等了许久，波蒂埃却没有等到任何一句回复。\
The moment her apology ends, she turns her head, unwilling to see Liáng's reaction. But after a long pause, there is no response.

**波蒂埃**：……说点什么呀！\
**Poitier**: Say something.

撞进她视野中的是一张写着意外的面孔。\
She looks back to see Liáng frozen in surprise.

**梁月**：哦……当然，我……\
**Liang Yue**: Oh, right, I ...

**梁月**：我并没有在意，波蒂埃教官。\
**Liang Yue**: It's okay. I didn't take it to heart.

**波蒂埃**：……很好。\
**Poitier**: Ahem. Good.

**？？？**：噗……\
**???**: Heh heh.

**波蒂埃**：什……什么人？！\
**Poitier**: Who's there?

一声轻笑从侧旁传来，波蒂埃像是一只被踩了尾巴的猫一样蹦了起来。\
A stifled laugh hits their ears. Poitier springs back like a startled cat.

**？？？**：抱歉，我并不是有意偷听你们的对话，也并没有取笑你们的意思。\
**???**: Sorry, I shouldn't eavesdrop. It's a bad habit.

**？？？**：只是……你们的感情真好，让我想起我从前的朋友们。\
**???**: It's just you remind me of my friends back in the old days.

**梁月**：您是方才的那位小姐。\
是我们疏忽了，我们还没有向您表示过感谢。\
**Liang Yue**: You're the lady that tried to help us soothe him. Thank you for the help.

**梁月**：多亏了您帮忙安抚住犯人的情绪，事态才没有恶化，我们也才能及时制服那位先生。谢谢您。\
**Liang Yue**: It could have turned out much worse if you hadn't been there. Thank you again.

**？？？**：你太客气了，小小的见习执夜人小姐，我只是做了我力所能及的事。\
更何况，最后真正控制住场面的是你和你的伙伴。\
**???**: That's too kind of you, young vigil. I just did what anyone should. Really, it was you and your partner that were the real heroes.

**梁月**：您真是谦虚。您……\
**Liang Yue**: You're too modest, ma'am. Actually, forgive me for asking.

**梁月**：我是不是在哪里见过您？\
**Liang Yue**: Haven't I seen your face before?

梁月盯着女子看了许久，终于忍不住将这个疑问说出了口。\
She studied the woman's face for quite some time before speaking this thought aloud.

也许她们的相会发生在某个“非现实”的地方——但那是哪里？\
徘徊在嘴边的答案，被对方先一步揭晓。\
They haven't met in person, no, it was in some other way, but how? Where? She has barely begun forming the words when the woman gives her the answer.

**？？？**：没想到时隔多年，还能遇到仍然记得那部电影的人。\
**???**: Good to know that someone still remembers those old flicks, even after all these years.

贝雷帽下那人的眉眼，逐渐和记忆中另一张面孔重叠在一起。\
The features of the face beneath the beret overlap with a face from Liáng's memory.

那张记忆中的面孔没有面前女子身上的成熟与稳重，更多的则是意气风发与神采飞扬。\
But the face she remembers lacks the maturity and composure of the woman before her. That face was brimming with youthful confidence, full of fire and energy.

但不变的是那双明亮的眼睛。它们就像是夜空中的星星，总是在银幕或录像厅电视机的小小屏幕上闪闪发光。\
But one thing has remained the same—those bright, shining eyes, like stars twinkling on silver screens and television sets.

**梁月**：我……想起来了，我见过您。\
在电影里见过您。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, from the movies. That's right.

**梁月**：您是……您是那位——\
**Liang Yue**: You—You're ...

**奇星**：是的。\
我是奇星，在《神秘警探C07》里面演C07的那个。\
**Qi Xing**: Oops, you got me. I'm Qí Xīng, or were you hoping I'd say Detective C07?

女子向目瞪口呆的二人眨了眨眼睛。\
She winks at the two dumbfounded officers.

**值班医生**：辛苦了，距离检测结果出来还需要一段时间，请你们稍等。\
**ER Doctor**: Our full report will take some time. You'll need to wait for now.

**梁月**：好的……麻烦您了。\
**Liang Yue**: Thank you, doctor.

**波蒂埃**：那个劫犯随身带着证件，倒是为我们省了不少事。\
艾瑞克·黄，43岁，在唐人街附近经营一家蔬菜店。\
**Poitier**: Our perp had his ID with him. That saves us a lot of digging. Eric Wong, 43, runs a grocery store in Chinatown.

**波蒂埃**：父母均已过世，但有个妻子丽莲·刘，十年前来美，各种证件都没有问题。\
全家上下没有犯罪记录，可以说都是清清白白的优秀市民。\
**Poitier**: Let's see. The only family member we've got is his wife, a Lilian Lau, who immigrated to the States 10 years ago. Both have no criminal record, totally clean.

**波蒂埃**：虽然因血统原因天生能够使用强大的神秘术，但在这件事之前，他一次都没有将这份能力用在过歪处。\
**Poitier**: He's an arcanist, apparently, and a powerful one at that. But no reports of any prior misuse of arcanum.

**波蒂埃**：我们在案发地点附近找到了他的车，里面装满了采购回来的土豆啦，胡萝卜什么的……作为障眼法，这高明得有些多此一举了。\
**Poitier**: His car was found near the crime scene, all filled up with potatoes and carrots from the wholesalers. Either this was just a spur-of-the-moment whacko move or some bizarre attempt at a tuber-based alibi.

**波蒂埃**：无论如何，我们已经联系了他的家属，应该过一会儿就能到，我们也许可以从他们的口中获得一些线索。\
**Poitier**: Anyway. We've contacted his wife, and she should be here soon. Maybe we'll get some more clues from her.

**波蒂埃**：……菜鸟？你在听吗？\
**Poitier**: Yo, Liáng? You listening?

**梁月**：是啊……在……\
**Liang Yue**: Oh. Y-You're right.

**波蒂埃**：…………\
**Poitier**: ...

答案显然是否定的。波蒂埃深吸了一口气——\
The answer is obvious—No. Poitier takes a deep breath.

**波蒂埃**：回神！\
**Poitier**: Earth calling Liáng.

**梁月**：哇？！\
**Liang Yue**: Whoa!

耳边骤然炸开的吼声让神游天外的梁惊得跳了起来。\
The sudden shout snaps Liáng out of her daze.

**梁月**：您……您做什么，波蒂埃教官？\
这里可是医院！\
**Liang Yue**: Officer Poitier, we're in a hospital. We should keep quiet.

**波蒂埃**：我也想要小声，但我看要是声音小了，就根本进不去你的大脑了。\
**Poitier**: Hmph. I would have, but that didn't seem likely to bring you back to earth, space cadet.

**波蒂埃**：你到底要发呆到什么时候，不就是见到C07的演员了吗？\
至于吗？\
**Poitier**: So, what's got you lost in space now?

**梁月**：我没有发呆，您刚才说的话我都听到了，我只是……只是在思考一些问题。\
**Liang Yue**: Um, I-I'm just thinking.

**波蒂埃**：哦？那你在思考什么？\
**Poitier**: About what?

**梁月**：……奇星小姐的事。\
**Liang Yue**: About Ms. Qí Xīng.

**波蒂埃**：你看吧？\
你说起那个导演的名字时那么熟悉，我就觉得奇怪了。\
**Poitier**: Ha, right. I guess you're really into those movies, huh? It's all good, boo.

**波蒂埃**：原来我们的乖乖仔经常会瞒着父母去偷看电影，而且还是《C07》系列的粉丝。你早说嘛！\
**Poitier**: I get the picture now. Our little C07 fan sneaking into the cinema behind her parents' back. You know, you're beginning to almost seem human, princess.

**波蒂埃**：我还一度担心你是个假人，像上次拉普拉斯提供给警局贴罚单的机器人之类的，会偷偷在背地里喝机油。看来我终于可以松一口气了。\
**Poitier**: At first, I thought you might be an android, like those Laplace bots that they've got writing parking tickets for us.

**梁月**：我……\
**Liang Yue**: I ...

梁月起初似乎想要反驳，但话到嘴边，她最终改变了主意。\
Liáng looks as if she wants to argue, but at the last moment, she stops herself.

**梁月**：是的……我的确很喜欢奇星小姐饰演的C07系列电影。\
那个角色对我来说也有很重要的意义。\
**Liang Yue**: In fact, I do like Ms. Qí Xīng's C07 movies very much. Her character means a lot to me.

**波蒂埃**：难不成你是因为那部电影才选择做执夜人的？\
**Poitier**: Oh. Is that the reason why you decided to be a vigil?

**梁月**：……准确地说，是它让我接受了自己只能成为警察。\
**Liang Yue**: Specifically, yes. It's the reason I decided my destiny was to be in the police.

**梁月**：话扯得有些远了，波蒂埃教官。\
我的确在思考关于奇星小姐的事，但那和我个人的喜恶无关。\
**Liang Yue**: But back to the topic. I was thinking about Ms. Qí Xīng, but it wasn't because I like her or anything like that.

少女摇了摇头，眼神变得凌厉，眉头却微微蹙起。\
She shakes her head, her gaze sharpening, her brows furrowed slightly.

**梁月**：制造连续袭击案的“针人”擅长使用飞针型的攻击性神秘术，而奇星小姐当年也正是以亲身上阵实拍的“银针”神秘术闻名。\
**Liang Yue**: It's just that ... her being here made me think about Nightpiercer. Ms. Qí Xīng has a similar arcane skill to the one he appears to use. She called it Silver Needle. She even performed it in her movies.

**梁月**：……这仅仅只是一个巧合吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Could that really just be a coincidence?

**波蒂埃**：哈？\
**Poitier**: Huh?

警官拧紧了眉头，就像听到了一个差劲的脑筋急转弯。\
但若有所思的梁月继续说了下去。\
The officer knits her brow as if she's just been hit with a bad joke. But Liáng, deep in thought, continues.

**梁月**：以及……她刚才的话，我总感觉有些意味深长。\
**Liang Yue**: And what she said felt meaningful, in some way.

**维尔汀**：约一个小时前\
One hour earlier

**梁月**：很荣幸见到您，奇星小姐！\
我……我小的时候是看着您演的电影长大的。\
**Liang Yue**: It's a great pleasure to meet you, Ms. Qí Xīng. I—I grew up watching your films.

**梁月**：您来这里是做什么呢？\
我的意思是说，如果方便问的话？\
**Liang Yue**: But what are you doing here in L.A.? Um, I mean, if it's okay to ask?

**奇星**：没有什么不方便的。我是来见一位老友的。\
**Qi Xing**: Sure, not a problem at all. I'm here to see an old friend.

作为一名曾火遍大江南北的影星，奇星的态度却十分亲和。\
她说话的口吻如同与友人闲谈，没有丝毫的拿腔作调。\
Though she was once a star known across the nation, Qí Xīng speaks warmly and without airs. It's like she's chatting with an old friend.

**梁月**：您是说……菲林士多导演？\
我听说她正在唐人街那边拍戏。\
**Liang Yue**: Is it Ms. Noire? I heard she's planning a new film.

**奇星**：是的，你也知道？\
我们已经很久没见面了，这次因为一些契机，我决定找她聚一聚。\
**Qi Xing**: Oh, so you heard the news? It's been a long time since I last saw her. You're right, though, kid. I've got something I need to talk to her about.

**梁月**：原来是这样，那真是……太好了。\
**Liang Yue**: Um, of course. That's great.

**梁月**：马上就是度朔节了，我听说唐人街那边也会举办社火游行，一定会很热闹的。\
**Liang Yue**: Oh, and the Dùshuò Festival is coming soon. I hope you'll go to the Shèhuǒ Parade in Chinatown. It'd be so much fun to see you there.

**波蒂埃**：……？\
**Poitier**: ...?

波蒂埃疑惑地盯着话忽然多了起来的梁月，感觉自己的搭档仿佛变成了另一个人。\
The quiet, reserved Liáng has suddenly turned chatty. Poitier stares at her. She's like an entirely different person.

**奇星**：今年的社火游行……也是，不知不觉又到这个时候了。\
**Qi Xing**: Shèhuǒ ... Is it really that time of year again?

**梁月**：您不喜欢社火游行吗？\
**Liang Yue**: You don't like the parade?

**奇星**：不，怎么会呢。\
**Qi Xing**: Of course I do.

**奇星**：酬神、消灾、祈福、欢祝……人们在热闹的庆典中迎接新一年的到来，祈祷来年风调雨顺、合境平安。\
**Qi Xing**: I like every bit of it—watching people eat, perform, and come together to celebrate the end of the year and to pray for peace and good luck in the next.

**奇星**：社火游行寄托着人们最朴实的愿望，那样纯粹、又那样美好，没有人会不喜欢它。\
**Qi Xing**: I like the pure and simple wish that the Shèhuǒ Parade carries.

**奇星**：……只是，每年的社火游行总会让我想到那个结局。\
**Qi Xing**: But it always reminds me of the ending.

**波蒂埃**：结局？\
**Poitier**: What ending?

奇星摇了摇头，似乎没有进一步继续这个话题的意思，梁月却忽然福至心灵。\
Qí Xīng falls silent, shaking her head. But no more explanation is needed. Liáng's memories have come back to her.

**梁月**：难道您是说……C07系列电影最后一部的那个结局？\
**Liang Yue**: You mean the ending of the last film in the C07 series?

看起来她猜对了，因为奇星略感意外地睁大了双眼后，点了点头。\
She must have guessed correctly. Qí Xīng's eyes widen a little. Then, she gives a small nod.

**奇星**：是的。\
**Qi Xing**: Yes.

**奇星**：虽然有许多人对那个结局十分追捧，说它“反映现实”“悲剧比喜剧更能让人记住”……\
**Qi Xing**: I know lots of people like that ending. "A reflection of reality," they say, "Tragedy leaves people with a deeper impression than comedy."

**奇星**：但坦白说，我并不喜欢当时的那个结局。\
坏人在最后并没有得到惩罚，正义的英雄失败了……这算什么？\
**Qi Xing**: But as for me, I hated it. The good guys failed, and the bad guys won? Ha. What kind of an ending is that?

**奇星**：我们无法控制现实，但至少能够决定电影里的故事。\
**Qi Xing**: Maybe we don't get a say in how things work in reality, but in stories we can. We should.

**奇星**：现实的世界已经足够模棱两可，荒谬不经。\
善有善报、恶有恶报，这才是大家走进电影院时期待看到的东西。\
**Qi Xing**: Reality itself is tragic enough already. Why should a movie remind us of how absurd things really are? "What goes around comes around." That's what people want to see in the movies.

作为一番由电影衍生出的讨论，这名昔日影星的口吻显然有些过于严肃了。\
但她所言之中仍然有些梁月颇有同感的地方。\
Her tone has turned unusually serious for a discussion about film, but these words strike a chord with Liáng.

**梁月**：我……我有同感。\
我记得小时候的我觉得很奇怪，疑惑为什么会是那种结局。\
**Liang Yue**: I-I agree with you. When I was little, I also didn't like how it ended.

**梁月**：也许现实的确就是这样无法尽如人意，但我想……至少在电影里，我还是想要看到纯粹的“邪不胜正”。\
**Liang Yue**: Maybe it's true that reality can't guarantee us true justice, but I still want to see justice being served, at least in fiction.

梁月的回答似乎博得了奇星的好感，她的眼睛亮了起来。\
This response seems to earn Qí Xīng's approval.

**奇星**：见习执夜人小姐，我想请问您一个也许有些冒昧的问题。\
**Qi Xing**: I feel the same way. Pardon me for asking.

**奇星**：您刚才呼唤出的那位伙伴让人印象深刻，我想我在传说中读到过符合它特征的记载。\
**Qi Xing**: That beast you summoned was something else. It reminded me of a certain creature, a legendary beast from the north of China.

**奇星**：“强梁既出，罔有不韪。斩杀凶咎，枭截不祥”……\
**Qi Xing**: "Arise Qiángliáng, swift and fierce! Banish all evil and cleanse this place!"

**奇星**：您想必就是梁家的后人，并且是那少数受到了眷顾的孩子之一，对吗？\
**Qi Xing**: That must make you a descendant of the Liáng family, right?

奇星眼中的某种东西，让梁月产生了被灼烧般的错觉。\
但梁月仍然诚实地回答了对方的问题。\
Something in Qí Xīng's gaze makes Liáng feel as though she's standing too close to an open flame. But even so, she answers truthfully.

**梁月**：我的确是十二侲子之一的梁家之后，我叫梁月。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes. I'm Liáng Yuè, from the Liáng family of the Twelve Zhènzǐ.

**奇星**：梁月……梁月。\
**Qi Xing**: Liáng Yuè ... Liáng Yuè.

**奇星**：好的，我记住你了。\
**Qi Xing**: It's a good name, little vigil. I'll keep it in mind.

## SC-05 局外人 / Other Side, Same Coin

**梁月**：我记得我在报纸上看到过，关于奇星小姐以及另外两位《神秘警探C07》系列电影主创人员之间的矛盾与纠纷。\
**Liang Yue**: I read an article about the conflicts between Ms. Qí Xīng and the other two producers of the C07 series.

**梁月**：我本以为那不过是八卦杂志捕风捉影编造的谣言，但如果包括奇星小姐与菲林士多的分歧和矛盾在内的那些传闻都是真的的话……\
**Liang Yue**: Before, I thought it was only rumors. But now, thinking over what she said, what if it's true?

**梁月**：不，这太荒谬了。\
**Liang Yue**: What am I saying? It's ridiculous.

**波蒂埃**：别想啦，瞧你那副愁眉苦脸的样子！\
**Poitier**: Then stop pouting over it, princess. We've got work to do.

**梁月**：呃！\
**Liang Yue**: Urgh!

人来人往的拉普拉斯康复中心合作医院走廊中，冥思苦想的见习执夜人少女后背上挨了搭档的一记掌击。\
The hallway of the Laplace Rehabilitation Center Cooperative Hospital is bustling with people. Lost in thought, Liáng is jolted back to reality by a firm clap on the back.

**波蒂埃**：一个用“银针神秘术”的罪犯出没在洛杉矶，而奇星本人也刚好在这个城市，用着同一个神秘术……\
**Poitier**: You wanna bet on how many people in L.A. have similar arcane skills? Come on. It's a total coincidence.

**波蒂埃**：你不会打算单凭这些就说奇星是犯人吧？那也太离谱了。\
**Poitier**: You don't really think they're the same person, do you? That'd be nuts!

**波蒂埃**：拜托，那可是奇星，曾经的超级巨星！\
虽然她现在不再出演电影了，但是当年谁没有看过她演的电影？\
**Poitier**: I mean it's the Detective C07 we're talking about. Sure, she's been retired from acting for a while, but she's like super famous.

**波蒂埃**：如果是演戏走火入魔、觉得自己真是电影里那个行侠仗义的正义英雄，那又为什么现在才开始作案？这讲不通。\
**Poitier**: If she was gonna go all kooky and start taking out crooks like she was the real C07, why wait all this time? It's been years since her last movie, and we're only just dealing with this Nightpiercer guy now.

**波蒂埃**：针型的攻击性神秘术不是什么少见的东西。“针人”也许只是看过那部电影之后模仿了里面的神秘术，又或者这只是巧合……\
**Poitier**: Besides, it's not like it's a crazy, unusual type of arcane skill. Who knows? Maybe this Nightpiercer guy is a fan of Detective C07's films too? Can't rule out anything yet.

**波蒂埃**：……喂，你没事吧？我刚才有那么用力吗？\
**Poitier**: Hey, you okay in there? Did I knock the wind out of you?

**梁月**：咳、咳……请别在意，我没事。\
**Liang Yue**: *cough* It's okay. I'm fine.

梁月摇了摇头，并无追究的意思。\
Liáng shakes her head.

波蒂埃茫然中带着心虚的表情诉说着她并非有意而为之，更何况……\
这突如其来的一击，也的确将梁月带离了方才纷杂的思绪。\
Poitier, still bewildered and perhaps feeling a little guilty, insists that she didn't mean to hit her so hard. Not that it matters. At least the sudden smack did the trick in pulling Liáng out of her spiraling thoughts.

检查结果和嫌犯的家属都还没有到来，带着波蒂埃聊表歉意的几枚硬币，梁月来到医院走廊的一角，和自动贩卖机交换了一瓶橙汁。\
Neither the test results nor the suspect's family has arrived yet. Liáng makes her way to the vending machine at the far end of the hallway with the coins Poitier dropped in her hand as a half-hearted apology and buys herself an orange juice.

但方才那个“荒谬的猜测”仍然盘踞在她的脑海中，不肯离去。\
But that absurd thought, that ridiculous guess from earlier, still refuses to leave her mind.

**梁月**：……快忘了它们吧，那根本不可能，而且也不符合逻辑。\
**Liang Yue**: Forget it. Just like you said, it doesn't make any sense.

忘却的尝试并不成功，直到一个焦急的声音打断梁月纷乱的思绪。\
All attempts to push the thought from her mind are failing. That is, until a frantic voice cuts through the air.

**医生**：但您受伤了！您不能就这样离开。\
**Doctor**: But you're injured, ma'am. You can't just leave.

**？？？**：我没受伤，我没事！这个只是……只是坏了一点而已，我会自己修的！\
**???**: I'm totally fine. It's just a tiny smidge of damage. I can fix it myself.

**医生**：您在说什么呀，您怎么能如此轻视自己的身体？我看得出来，您的手臂绝对是断了，必须要处理一下才行！\
**Doctor**: You call a broken arm a smidge? You need to let us treat it immediately.

**梁月**：发生什么事了？\
**Liang Yue**: What's going on here?

医生通过梁月身上的制服认出了她的身份。\
The doctor recognizes her uniform immediately.

**医生**：您是……一名执夜人？\
您来得正好，也许您能够帮忙劝住这个孩子。\
**Doctor**: Are you a vigil? Could you help me stop this girl? She's trying to leave with a broken arm.

**医生**：她刚才在乘坐出租车的时候遭遇了一场交通事故，失去意识被送到了这里。\
但她醒来之后，居然要求我们不要管她……\
**Doctor**: She was in an accident. But since she's woken up, she's refused to let us examine anything.

**医生**：我看得出这孩子的体质特殊，但无论如何我们是医生，不能就这样坐视伤者带着病痛离开。\
**Doctor**: She might not be our normal kind of patient, but we're doctors. We can't let someone leave when they need immediate medical attention.

**？？？**：执夜人……？！\
**???**: A vigil?

**？？？**：但但但但但我真的赶时间，再不走我就要赶不上车了！\
**???**: I-I-I-I-I-I'm in a hurry now. I'm gonna miss my bus.

细看不难发现少女衣装下裸露的“皮肤”呈冷硬的金属色泽，想必这就是医师口中“体质特殊”的缘由。\
Beneath the girl's clothing, the exposed skin has a cold, metallic sheen. That must be what the doctor meant by "not our normal kind of patient."

梁月当然没有错过少女胸前代表圣洛夫基金会职员身份的徽章。\
但在看清梁月所身着的制服后，对方表现出的惊慌失措却令人生疑。\
Liáng notices the emblem on her chest, marking her as an employee of the St. Pavlov Foundation. How odd that she'd have such a panicked reaction at the sight of a vigil.

**梁月**：……我想不论是什么样的急事，都比不上身体重要。\
这位医生说得没错，您最好接受检查后再离开。\
**Liang Yue**: There'll be another bus, but you only have one body. You should listen to the doctor, sit down, and wait, until you're cleared to leave.

**梁月**：因此请您出示一下您的身份证件吧，这样医生才好为您进行诊疗。\
**Liang Yue**: Please show us your ID so that the doctor can give you treatment.

那颗机械脑袋僵硬了几秒。\
随后，以堪称迅猛的气势仰了起来。\
For a few stiff seconds, the girl's mechanical head freezes in place. Then, in a movement almost too fast to follow, it snaps up.

**？？？**：我的老天爷！有一只仓鼠骑着听诊器在天花板上飞！\
**???**: Look. A hamster riding a stethoscope.

**梁月**：仓鼠骑……什么？\
**Liang Yue**: A hamster what?

实在过于令人匪夷所思的台词让梁月不由得真的转头看了看……\
而理所当然的，并没有仓鼠骑着听诊器在天花板上飞。\
The bizarreness of these words leaves Liáng no choice but to glance in the pointed direction, only to confirm, of course, that there is no hamster nor stethoscope in sight.

**？？？**：就是现在！\
**???**: Now!

**梁月**：你……等等，站住！\
**Liang Yue**: Hey, wait!

**医护人员**：哦，小心！\
**Medical Staff**: Watch out!

**梁月**：抱歉，医生，我急着——\
**Liang Yue**: Sorry, I'm after a—

并不宽敞的医院走廊显然并不适合上演追逐战，梁月被一辆从拐角处出现的手推车挡住了去路，再抬头时已经不见那颗机械脑袋的影子了。\
The hospital's narrow hallways are hardly suitable for a chase, and Liáng quickly finds her path blocked by a supply cart. By the time she's made it past, the mechanical-headed girl has disappeared.

自神秘学犯罪科领取的金属变色龙通信器发出了独有的声响，打消了梁月正欲继续追踪的意图。\
Her metal chameleon communication device, issued by the Division of Arcane Affairs, gives off its distinctive chime.

**波蒂埃**：喂，菜鸟！你买个饮料跑去哪里了？\
尽快回来，检查结果出来了，那位先生的家属也到了。\
**Poitier**: Hey, rookie. Where did you go? Get back here. The medical report is ready, and Mr. Wong's family just arrived.

**梁月**：我……好的。\
检查的结果如何？\
**Liang Yue**: I ... Understood. How's Mr. Wong doing?

通信的另一端沉默了片刻。\
There's a long pause on the other end of the line.

**波蒂埃**：不太乐观。\
**Poitier**: It's not pretty.

**男子**：…………\
**Enraged Man**: ...

病床上沉睡的男人形容枯槁，呼吸间发出犹如拉风箱般的声音，宛如一棵被蛀虫掏空的朽木。\
Mr. Wong is lying unconscious on the hospital bed, looking haggard. His breathing is labored and raspy, like wind rattling through a hollowed-out log.

**女子**：怎么……怎么弄成这样啊！\
他这是怎么了？早上还好好的呀！\
**Woman**: How ... What happened to him? He seems completely normal this morning.

她的四肢软了下去，幸而有随行的男人托撑着，才不至于垮倒。\
Her legs go weak. Were it not for the man supporting her, she might have collapsed entirely.

**？？？**：别着急，听听医生怎么说。\
**???**: Please relax, Ms. Wong. We have to wait and see what the doctor says.

**波蒂埃**：是你？\
**Poitier**: You again?

波蒂埃立刻认出，男子正是隔三岔五就会造访神秘学犯罪科的那位并不受欢迎的常客。\
Poitier instantly recognizes him—one of the Division of Arcane Affairs's least welcome and regular visitors.

**波蒂埃**：哦……我记起来了。\
您是一位持证的神秘学民间侦探。您是接受了这位女士的委托吗？\
**Poitier**: Right, right. You're the local arcane private eye, aren't you, Zhōu? Are you commissioned by the victim?

**民间侦探**：什么？\
**Private Investigator**: What?

他先是诧异地瞪大了眼睛，随后狠狠剐了波蒂埃一眼。\
The man's eyes widen in surprise before shooting Poitier a venomous glare.

**民间侦探**：哈！\
我和某些拿着不菲的薪酬，却无所作为的蛀虫可不同。\
**Private Investigator**: Ha. Unlike some tax leeches out there, I actually help people in need.

**民间侦探**：街坊邻里有难时帮一把手，在我这里是不收钱的。\
**Private Investigator**: And I don't charge a fee when it comes to my neighbors.

**波蒂埃**：……抱歉，是我失言了。\
**Poitier**: Sorry.

男子显然也无意在此时争吵，冷哼一声后不再理睬身着制服的两名警官，而是用询问的眼神望向一旁的医生。\
He clearly has no interest in arguing at a time like this. He lets out a cold snort and turns to the doctor with a questioning look.

**值班医生**：执夜人梁小姐为他清除了身上所中的未知神秘术，但尽管生理上并无大碍，那种未知的术式仍然留下了后遗症。\
**ER Doctor**: Ms. Liáng has cleared the unknown arcane skill that was afflicting him. His physical condition is stable, but I fear there may be some long-term effects on his mind.

**值班医生**：他的精神状态十分糟糕，呈现出了严重的思维混乱和记忆错乱症状。\
我们不得已，只好让他保持睡眠状态了。\
**ER Doctor**: He seems to be suffering from a severe thought and memory disorder. It would be best to keep him asleep.

**女子**：那……那大夫，他什么时候能醒过来？我能和他说话吗？\
**Woman**: Doctor, when will he wake up? Can I speak to him?

**值班医生**：我们不建议您在您丈夫清醒的情况下和他会面。\
他大概率……是无法认出您的。\
**ER Doctor**: For now, we suggest against it. It may cause him additional distress to see someone familiar to him. We fear there might be memory loss.

**女子**：什么？怎么……\
**Woman**: What? How?

**女子**：诶呀，这都是什么事呀！\
先是妈走了，现在你也……这叫我怎么办才好啊？\
**Woman**: What should I do now? With his mother gone, I can't take any more of this.

**梁月**：女士……\
**Liang Yue**: Madam ...

女子像是被抽走了力气，瘫坐在一旁的座椅上。\
梁月张口欲安慰对方，却不知该说些什么。\
The woman looks as though all the strength has been drained from her body as she slumps into a nearby chair. Liáng opens her mouth to offer comfort but can't seem to find the right words.

男人的目光扫过波蒂埃，最终瞪向梁月。\
Zhōu's gaze sweeps past Poitier before settling on Liáng.

**民间侦探**：看来，你们警局专门请来了一个华人小跟班来“对症下药”。\
**Private Investigator**: So, who's the little Chinese kid? Did the DAA give you a sidekick to do your job for you?

**民间侦探**：但如果你们帮不上忙，就不必假惺惺地站在这里碍事了。\
算我拜托你们，给我片刻安宁吧！\
**Private Investigator**: Forget it lah. Listen, if you're not going to do your best to help these people, then it's better you just stay out of my way.

**梁月**：……\
**Liang Yue**: ...

梁月用询问的目光看向波蒂埃，后者无奈地摇摇头，招手让梁月来到身旁后，向她出示了院方的诊断结果。\
Liáng looks to Poitier with a questioning gaze. Poitier shakes her head and sighs, gesturing for her to come closer before handing over the hospital's diagnosis.

**波蒂埃**：这个可怜的家伙身上残留的神秘术痕迹，能够证明当时他无法控制自己的行为。这让他能够免于牢狱之灾。\
**Poitier**: When they first brought him in, there were remnants of the arcanum riddled through his body. It might have gone a long way to proving he wasn't in control of himself.

**波蒂埃**：但坏消息是那股神秘术气息很快消散了，医院没能查出他到底是出了什么毛病。\
**Poitier**: But I guess anything definitive has already faded away. The doctors couldn't isolate a cause.

**波蒂埃**：这样下去，这个可怜的家伙也许后半辈子都要在精神病院里度过了。\
**Poitier**: Worse-case scenario, they might not believe us and have this poor guy shoved off to the funny farm.

梁月握紧了拳头，看向蜷缩在病房的座椅上低声啜泣的女子。\
和宽大的座椅相比，她的身影是那样单薄。\
Liáng clenches her fists and looks toward the woman curled up in the hospital chair, quietly sobbing. She looks so small against the oversized seat.

最终，梁月走上前去，在坐椅旁蹲下了身。\
Finally, Liáng steps forward and crouches beside the chair.

迟疑片刻后，在那名并不友好的男子惊讶的目光中，她伸手覆上女子的手背。\
After a brief hesitation, she reaches out and places a hand over the woman's. Zhōu looks surprised.

**梁月**：阿姨，您别太难过了……这样伤身体。\
**Liang Yue**: Madam, please, you need to stay strong for your husband.

**梁月**：叔叔现在这样的情况也只是暂时的。\
这里有拉普拉斯康复中心外派来的名医，一定能够找到方法治好他的。\
**Liang Yue**: They've brought in some of the best doctors from the Laplace Rehab Center. If there is anyone that can help him, it'll be them.

某种意义上来讲，这番其实并无任何保证的承诺甚至可以被定义为谎言。\
但谎言也有它的价值，有人需要谎言。\
In a way, it is a promise with no real guarantee—a statement that could almost be considered a lie. But even lies have value when a person needs to hear them.

它起效了。\
女子抬手草草擦去面庞上的泪珠，仍然红着眼睛，但至少抬起了头。\
The woman hastily wipes her tear-streaked face and lifts her head.

**女子**：我……我从上午起就联系不上他，说是去进货，人却迟迟不见踪影。\
结果到了下午，我就接到警察的电话，说他……\
**Woman**: He said that he was going to buy produce from the wholesalers, but I couldn't reach him. And then, the police called.

**女子**：我家这口子一向老实、脾气好，街坊邻里都知道。\
他肯定做不出来这种违法的事情的！\
**Woman**: My husband is a good man. Everyone knows that. He would never do something like this.

**女子**：警官，求求你啊！\
你可得帮帮我们，帮我们查清楚啊！\
**Woman**: Please, Miss, you have to help us.

**梁月**：……！\
**Liang Yue**: ...!

女子捉住了梁月的手，紧紧握住，却又在不断颤抖。\
The woman grasps Liáng's hand tightly in hers, her fingers trembling.

那是一双柔软却也粗糙的手，书写着一对平凡的夫妇为更好的生活而勤恳拼搏的日日夜夜。\
Her hands are gentle, yet rough, etched with years of hard work—the kind of hands earned through long days and nights of striving for a better life.

**梁月**：……我……\
**Liang Yue**: I ...

贴合的皮肤处传来带着焦急和绝望的体温。\
那温度滚烫，甚至让人产生了要被灼伤的错觉。\
In her palm, she can feel the woman's desperate, burning warmth. It is so hot. She feels it could scorch her.

——梁月吸了一口气。\
Liáng takes a deep breath.

**梁月**：当然了。\
阿姨，您放心。\
**Liang Yue**: You can rely on us, ma'am.

**梁月**：——我们一定会查清楚真相的。\
**Liang Yue**: We'll find out the truth behind this. I promise you.

梁月用力回握住那双手。\
She gives the woman's hand a firm, reassuring squeeze.

**女子**：好呀……好呀！我先谢谢你们了！\
**Woman**: Thank you. Thank you so much!

**女子**：就全靠你了，姑娘！\
**Woman**: You are our only hope, please!

——谎言也能够成真，有人决心做到这一点。\
Sometimes, a lie can become the truth. All it takes is someone willing to make it so.

**民间侦探**：……\
**Private Investigator**: ...

病房的门在二人的身后合上。\
短暂的相顾无言后，波蒂埃挑起一侧的眉毛，先开了口。\
The door to the ward is shut behind them. After a moment of silence, Poitier tilts her head.

**波蒂埃**：听起来你擅自答应了一些不在我们职务范围内的事情，菜鸟。\
**Poitier**: Rookie mistake, princess. Never make a promise about something you don't get to decide on.

**梁月**：抱歉，波蒂埃教官。\
但请您听我说，我——\
**Liang Yue**: I'm sorry, Ms. Poitier. But I only meant—

**波蒂埃**：停，停。\
**Poitier**: Hold it.

**波蒂埃**：我又没说不行。\
**Poitier**: I didn't say we weren't gonna do our best.

**梁月**：…………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

那些还没能出口的话语失去了它们的用场。\
片刻后，梁月露出了一个在波蒂埃印象中也许是第一次见的笑脸。\
The words she was about to say no longer serve any purpose. Instead, Liáng does something Poitier has never seen her do before. She smiles.

**梁月**：谢谢您，波蒂埃教官。\
**Liang Yue**: Thank you, ma'am.

**波蒂埃**：别着急谢我。\
就算要调查，我们也得有线索才行。\
**Poitier**: Not so fast. We still need some solid evidence if we're gonna crack this case.

**梁月**：目前并没有明显的线索。\
就像那位女士说的一样，她的丈夫一向与人为善，没有任何仇家。\
**Liang Yue**: But where to begin? It seems like there are no obvious clues beyond what we've seen. Mr. Wong had no enemies and was well-loved in his community.

**梁月**：他的交友圈子也十分干净，属于低危人群。\
但当我问到唐人街有没有什么怪事的时候，她身边的那个大叔主动开口了。\
**Liang Yue**: If that's the case, then it can't be a simple motivation. Still, something sticks out to me. When I asked about any recent events or happenings, it wasn't Mrs. Wong that answered. It was ...

这是个足以让波蒂埃惊讶的消息。\
Poitier already knows where this is going.

**波蒂埃**：那个一向讨厌我们的赤脚侦探？\
