**Poitier**: Zhōu. Our private eye with a chip on his shoulder against the DAA.

**梁月**：是的。他提到最近唐人街一带，零零碎碎地发生了许多怪事。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes. He mentioned that there have been strange things going on around L.A.'s Chinatown recently.

**梁月**：像幼儿经常神不守舍，年轻人忽然变得精神恍惚，又或是原本精神抖擞的老者一夜间变得痴呆健忘……\
**Liang Yue**: According to my notes, he mentioned there were children that suddenly became distant and unresponsive, young men that began showing signs of memory loss, and an otherwise healthy elder that rapidly developed signs of dementia.

**梁月**：也有人像是黄先生这样，变得癫狂易怒。\
但他们认为这只是邻里之间的小摩擦，因此大多没有报案。\
**Liang Yue**: Absent-mindedness, empty despondence towards family and friends, memory loss. It all sounds very familiar to Mr. Wong's condition. But no one thought to bring the matter to the police.

**梁月**：我询问了护士，她们也证实说唐人街片区最近收治了不少“因不明原因出现精神异常”的患者。\
**Liang Yue**: I also spoke with the nurses here. They said they've also noticed an increase in patients from Chinatown, complaining of confusion and memory loss.

**梁月**：不过没有一例上报——毕竟事情“不大不小”。\
**Liang Yue**: I guess, once again, no one thought it was serious enough for our attention.

梁月话语间透露的意思让波蒂埃的脸色凝重了起来。\
Poitier's expression darkens.

**波蒂埃**：你怀疑这些“怪事”都是同一种神秘学事件导致的？\
**Poitier**: Well, whatcha thinking, cadet? Are all these cases related?

**波蒂埃**：这可不是一个能随随便便拿出来的结论。\
如果真是这样，那……这件事的严重程度就远超我们的想象了。\
**Poitier**: If it's as widespread as you're making it out to be, we might be in over our heads.

**梁月**：既然存在这个可能性，我想我们就不该忽视。\
**Liang Yue**: Even so, I think we can't overlook it as a possibility.

**梁月**：直接影响高等智慧生命精神层面的神秘术虽然罕见，但并不是不存在。\
在夜巡特遣的档案室中，我阅读过不少这样的案例。\
**Liang Yue**: Arcane skills that directly affect the mind are rare, but they do exist. I've read of similar cases in the Vigiles Archive.

**梁月**：在那些案例中，受害者的症状乍看起来都各不相同——\
这恰好和眼下发生在唐人街的现象一致。\
**Liang Yue**: One of them, as I recall, had very similar symptoms to what we're seeing here.

梁月说到这里，又皱眉露出了思索的神情。\
Liáng's brow furrows.

**梁月**：令我百思不得其解的是，若这一切都是人为，施术者的动机又是什么？\
**Liang Yue**: However, if there were some criminal intention behind all of these symptoms, what could it be?

**梁月**：又难道说，这起事件是个意外？是某个血统强大却还无法掌控神秘术的幼童，抑或是某些未被监管的危险神秘学物件引发的？\
**Liang Yue**: Or could it be an accident? Maybe a child with a powerful arcane skill who can't control it? Or some unregulated and dangerous arcane objects?

**梁月**：现阶段证据太少……我们还无法下定论。\
**Liang Yue**: We can't draw any conclusions without more evidence.

眼下只能得出这个说不上是结论的结论，二人都是愁眉不展。\
片刻后，波蒂埃却像是忽然想起了什么。\
The two officers look troubled. Then, as if something has clicked in her mind, Poitier's face lights up.

**波蒂埃**：不过说起来，我记得你们基金会就有一个专门的部门，负责“关押”那些可能捅出篓子来的小玩意。\
**Poitier**: Arcane objects ... Isn't there a department in the Foundation that stores and records dangerous arcane materials?

**梁月**：是的，就在圣洛夫基金会总部。\
它叫做——\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, at the headquarters of the Foundation. And its official name is ...

**梁月**：神秘学藏品管理部。\
The Arcanum Containment Department.

**玛蒂尔达**：到达，我想就是这里没错了。\
**Matilda**: Ah. Voilà. I believe I am here.

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯……倒是比我想象中的更整洁明亮一些。\
**Matilda**: Hmm, it is much brighter and more spacious than I expected.

## SC-06 秘密通缉令 / Secret Warrant

**玛蒂尔达**：柜子，柜子，柜子……还是柜子。\
**Matilda**: Cabinets, cabinets, and more cabinets.

**玛蒂尔达**：这里的人去哪里了？\
奇怪，这样重要的部门，连个看管的人都没有吗？\
**Matilda**: Who is in charge here? I was under the impression this was an important department, no? Where is the security?

博闻强识的优等生玛蒂尔达小姐穿过一排又一排的档案柜。\
她在介绍基金会历史的书籍中读到过关于这个部门的事。\
The ever-curious Matilda weaves her way through the rows of filing cabinets. She has read about this department in books detailing the Foundation's history.

**玛蒂尔达**：我记得那本书上写着：“从古至今几乎所有的神秘学现象，你都能够在神秘学藏品管理室中找到与之匹配的物件。”\
**Matilda**: "The department contains all known objects which have produced dangerous or mysterious arcane phenomenon."

**玛蒂尔达**：甚至还有人说：“在神秘学藏品管理室的档案柜之外，已经不存在尚未解开的神秘学谜团了……”\
**Matilda**: Some even say it contains "Every arcane mystery—solved and unsolved—that has ever been recorded."

**玛蒂尔达**：但接下来的事大家都知道了，“暴雨”来了。\
**Matilda**: But of course, the biggest mystery of all time, the "Storm," still defies them.

**玛蒂尔达**：几乎所有部门的工作重心都转向破解这个最大的神秘学谜团，没有人再关心神秘学藏品管理室的档案柜里那一个个“小谜团”了。\
**Matilda**: As it does for us all. It seems, with every department turned to the study of the "Storm," there is little time to spare for these more trivial puzzles.

脚步声在空荡荡的楼层中回响。\
玛蒂尔达莫名有一种被注视的感觉，却始终没有看到半个人影。\
Her footsteps echo through the empty department, and the odd sense that she's being watched settles over her.

安静有时令人放松，有时则令人避讳。\
它会传染孤独，将人们压在心底深处的不安翻出水面。\
Silence can be comforting, but it can also be unsettling—a breeding ground for loneliness, dredging up long-buried unease.

**玛蒂尔达**：……\
**Matilda**: ...

**玛蒂尔达**：不知道妈妈怎么样了。\
Z女士说会帮忙关注她的消息，可现在却还是没有音信……\
**Matilda**: I wonder how Mama is doing. Madam Z said she would keep an eye on her, but still no updates.

勇敢的小调查员不知不觉停下了脚步，垂下了头去。\
She finds herself pausing, her gaze lowering to the ground.

——但也只有片刻。\
But only for a moment.

**玛蒂尔达**：不对，你在想什么呢？那可是伟大的玛蒂尔达小姐的伟大的妈妈！\
她不会出什么事的。\
**Matilda**: No, bring yourself together, Matilda Bouanich. This is your mama, the greatest mother of all time. What could possibly have gone wrong?

伴随着她大步迈开的步伐，浅色的单边马尾再次精神抖擞地跃动了起来。\
With renewed confidence, she picks up her pace, her pale ponytail bouncing behind her.

**玛蒂尔达**：倒是那个狡猾的维尔汀，打着什么“复兴乌卢鲁运动会”的名号度假……\
而踏实可靠的优等生玛蒂尔达小姐却在这里跑腿！\
**Matilda**: Now her most outstanding daughter runs an important errand for the Foundation, unlike some others who have dedicated their valuable time to a vacation in the name of "reviving the Uluru Games."

**玛蒂尔达**：她最好祈祷真的能够举办一场像是历史书里面写的那样的、盛大而恢宏的运动会，不然我就要——\
**Matilda**: Still, one must hope they will succeed in making the games as grand and sublime as they say they were in the distant past, or else ...

**玛蒂尔达**：嗯？\
**Matilda**: Hmm?

在穿过某排档案柜时，划过视野边缘的一抹异色让她停下了脚步。\
Just as she passes another set of shelves, something catches her eye.

**？？？**：看来这边没有什么问题。那么下一列就是……\
**???**: Everything's fine here. Now, on to the next row.

**？？？**：哦！\
是它，我最喜欢的神秘学管理品之一！\
**???**: Oh. This is one of my favorites.

**玛蒂尔达**：那是什么？\
**Matilda**: What is it?

**？？？**：好问题！\
这可是件了不起的东西，看看上面的编号你就明白了。\
**???**: An excellent question, Miss. See that serial number on it?

**？？？**：——神秘学管理品编号AN-003，沛霖川的河水。\
003号耶！\
**???**: AN-003, a water sample from the Pèilín River. Number 003.

**？？？**：尽管我们神秘学藏品管理部里收藏着无数珍奇有趣的东西，但不论让谁来选出自己最喜欢的前一百名，它都百分百会上榜。\
**???**: There are hundreds of thousands of samples, collections, and records here, but no matter who you ask, this particular one will always make their top list.

**？？？**：它来自中国内陆一个与世隔绝的古城，当调查员来到那座城池的时候，他们发现城里的人们居然依旧维持着中国晚唐时期的着装与风俗。\
**???**: Collected in a remote city in China. When the investigators arrived, they found that it had been isolated in time. All its inhabitants dressed and lived as if they were from the late Táng Dynasty.

**？？？**：他们对时代的变迁一无所知，就像是被世界遗忘了一样。\
**???**: They were completely unaware of the state of the world beyond their lands, as if trapped in a time capsule from the forgotten past.

**玛蒂尔达**：哦……\
**Matilda**: Oh ...

试管中的液体清澈而晶莹，与其说是河水，不如说更接近液化的某种透亮的宝石，玛蒂尔达不禁看得有些入神。\
The liquid inside the vial is clear and pristine—less like river water and more like a perfectly liquefied gemstone. Matilda can't help but stare in fascination.

**玛蒂尔达**：但这怎么可能呢？\
又不是原始部落，他们总要和外面往来的。\
**Matilda**: But how is that possible? Did no one ever leave the city? Not even to travel or do business?

**？？？**：问得好！调查员们也为此感到疑惑，他们最终发现问题出在环绕那座城市的护城河“沛霖川”上。那条河里蕴藏着不可思议的神秘术。\
**???**: You're a clever one, Miss. Yes, it seems the investigators were confused, too. In the end, they realized that an arcane skill was affecting the Pèilín River.

**？？？**：然而……那份力量却在不断消散。没等调查员们弄清其中的奥秘，河水中就已经再也无法检测出任何神秘术残留了。\
**???**: Sadly, it seems the arcane energy was dissipating by the time they arrived, and they weren't able to figure out its cause.

**？？？**：只有这一份样本幸运地被保存了下来。拉普拉斯的人对它很有兴趣，他们一直在寻找方法，试图搞明白其中的奥秘。\
**???**: This is the only sample they were able to recover. Laplace has been begging for access to it. They're eager to unravel the mystery.

**玛蒂尔达**：哇哦……原来是这样。\
我承认这个故事还是挺有趣的。\
**Matilda**: Wow. That is indeed a most intriguing claim.

**？？？**：这可不是故事，这是真……的……\
**???**: It's not just a claim, Miss. It's real. Wait.

**？？？**：你是……玛蒂尔达·布翁尼小姐？！\
**???**: Ms. Matilda Bouanich?

这个粗心大意的年轻职员似乎刚刚才真正意识到玛蒂尔达的出现。\
The careless young staff member only now seems to have fully recognized Matilda's presence.

**玛蒂尔达**：你认识我？\
**Matilda**: You've heard of me?

**？？？**：当然。您的父亲和母亲都颇负盛名，当年您一家人加入基金会的时候可是引起了不小的轰动。\
**???**: Yeah, of course. Who hasn't heard of the Bouaniches and their star investigator daughter. Didn't you know that everyone's been talking about you since you joined the Foundation?

**？？？**：也许您已经忘了，那时我母亲还曾带着我上门拜访……哦！抱歉，我还没有自我介绍呢。\
**???**: Actually, my mother and I went to visit you. Oh. But I haven't introduced myself.

**斯考特**：我是康斯坦丝·斯考特，和您一样，也是第一防线学校毕业的。\
但……\
**Scott**: Constance Scott, I'm a fellow graduate from SPDM.

**斯考特**：惭愧的是如您所见，我毕业后只不过是个小小的神秘学藏品管理部的仓库管理员罢了。\
**Scott**: Of course, now, I'm just a record keeper here.

这应当并非谦辞。历届第一防线学校的优等生都会获得将名字装点在校史馆里的荣耀，但玛蒂尔达对斯考特的名字毫无印象。\
It doesn't seem like false modesty. Every top student of the SPDM was granted the honor of having their name inscribed in the school's hall of fame, but Matilda has never once come across the name Scott.

**玛蒂尔达**：好吧，斯考特小姐——实际上，正好，我正在找你。\
佩德拉委员让我将这个交给你。\
**Matilda**: Actually, I've been looking for you as well, Ms. Scott. Commissioner Pedra asked me to give this to you.

**斯考特**：一封信？是什么事？\
**Scott**: A letter? What's it about?

**玛蒂尔达**：我也不知道。那个大块头刚才阴沉着脸将我喊过去，让我把几个月前在旧金山遇到的事又讲了一遍，然后就……\
**Matilda**: I couldn't say. But he had a most unpleasant look about him as he gave it to me. Then he asked me to review my report on the events in San Francisco.

**玛蒂尔达**：怎么了？你的脸色好难看。\
**Matilda**: Are you alright? Your face has grown quite pale.

**斯考特**：我没事，只是……我想我猜到是什么事了。\
**Scott**: I'm fine. I just have a bad feeling I know what I'm about to read.

送别年轻的信使，斯考特捏着这封她并不愿意收到的信件来到了一间管理部内鲜有人踏足的偏僻房间。\
Having bid farewell to Matilda, Scott makes her way to a secluded room within the department, the letter clutched in her hand.

房门在她的身后关上。\
她拆开信封，信纸轻盈地飘了出来，带给了她一个沉重的消息。\
She carefully closes the door behind her, and, with one last glance around the room, opens the envelope. A single sheet of paper floats out from within, one carrying a heavy message.

**佩德拉**：调查结果出来了，是个坏消息。\
不论是对你，还是对基金会来说，都是。\
**Pedra**: The investigation has been concluded. Unfortunately, their findings were exactly as we feared.

**佩德拉**：我们必须尽快逮住她，在那些东西引发难以收拾的麻烦之前，回收那些流出基金会的神秘学管理品。\
**Pedra**: The suspect must be apprehended ASAP, and all efforts must be made to retrieve this arcane object before either cause further trouble.

**佩德拉**：我们已经锁定了她最后出现的地点，你需要立刻启程——地点是洛杉矶，唐人街。\
**Pedra**: You must leave immediately. Her last reported sighting was in Chinatown, Los Angeles.

**商贩**：新鲜的橘子啊，看一看啊。\
**Vendor**: Oranges! Fresh oranges!

**游客**：抱歉，能再告诉我一遍这个叫什么吗？\
“纸马舞”“纸马舞”……好，记住了。\
**Tourist**: Sorry, could you say that again? Zhǐ Mǎ Wǔ? And that means paper horse dance? Okay. I got it.

**唐人街居民**：老板，今天还有烧肉吗？\
……没了？那切一块叉烧吧，再拿半只白切鸡。\
**Chinatown Resident**: Hey, shopkeeper! Got any Siu Yuk left? No? Then give me a piece of Char Siu and some Bak Chit Gai, please.

**孩童**：哇哦……爸，快看！\
那个屋顶上有龙，这也太酷了！\
**Child**: Wow! Daddy, look! There's a dragon on the floor. That's totally cool!

操着不同语言的人们来来往往络绎不绝。\
而梁月在宽敞的大道上走走停停，几乎目不暇接。\
People speaking many languages meet and weave around each other on the crowded avenue. Liáng wanders among them, stopping every now and then to take it all in.

**波蒂埃**：欢迎来到唐人街，怎么样，有什么感想吗？\
**Poitier**: Welcome to Chinatown. How do you like it?

**梁月**：这里的确让我感到十分亲切。\
您经常来唐人街吗，波蒂埃教官？\
**Liang Yue**: Yes. It does give me a certain sense of nostalgia. Do you come here often, Ms. Poitier?

**波蒂埃**：算是吧，我记得上次来是大概……唔，三年前？\
**Poitier**: Yeah, I guess so. I mean, outside of work, it's been a while. Three years or so.

**梁月**：……我想这应该不能叫“经常来”。\
**Liang Yue**: Only once in three years? I don't think you can consider that "often."

波蒂埃摆了摆手，看向两侧的熙熙攘攘的街道。\
Poitier waves a hand, glancing down the lively streets on either side.

**波蒂埃**：要是想来一场一日旅行的话，这里的确是个好去处。\
但如果作为穿着这身制服的人来到这里……事情就不一样了。\
**Poitier**: Yeah, well, it's a fun place for a day trip, sure, but things are different when you put on the uniform.

**波蒂埃**：正如你之前所见到的那个民间侦探，他就是警局与唐人街之间关系的缩影。\
**Poitier**: Remember that private eye back at the hospital, Zhōu? You can get an impression about how people see the police around here from him.

**梁月**：您的意思是说……唐人街里面的人不配合我们的工作吗？\
**Liang Yue**: You mean that the residents here don't cooperate with the Arcane Affairs division?

**波蒂埃**：倒也不是。应该说因为语言和文化上的差异，他们有时并不倾向于寻求我们的帮助，而有时即使我们想要帮忙，也可能无从下手。\
**Poitier**: Well, it's complicated. There's a lot of language and cultural barriers. Folks here just don't turn to the police to solve their problems. Even when they do, we feel like we have no idea where to start.

**波蒂埃**：我听说在你们那里，许多超自然者也会和人们生活在一起。\
唐人街这里也是一样，第一次来的时候我吓了一跳。\
**Poitier**: The thing that surprised me the most was how arcanists of all kinds and humans live so closely together here. I guess it's the same in China, isn't it?

**波蒂埃**：那次我们接到报警说这边的一家中药铺子遭了贼，过去一看，店主居然是只一人高的大白鸟。\
**Poitier**: I remember this one time, we had a call about a break-in. When we got there, it turned out the shopkeeper was a big white bird as tall as I am.

**波蒂埃**：还有一次有个三流傀儡师让他的洋娃娃走丢了，我一路追到了这里，向路过的一个大婶问路……结果你知道她说什么吗？\
**Poitier**: And this other time, we're chasing down a lost puppet for some lame-ass puppeteer. Anyways, so I ask an old lady if she'd seen a doll nearby. You know what she said?

**波蒂埃**：她居然和旁边的人说“尼们敲，介个老外好香肘丢了……”\
**Poitier**: Well, I don't know what she said, but she started going off about me being a Lǎowài.

**波蒂埃**：我不知道其他的话是什么意思，但我听得懂“老外”！\
就是“外国人”的意思！可拜托，我是在这个国家出生的耶！\
**Poitier**: Now, give me some credit. I might not speak Chinese, but I do know Lǎowài means foreigner. So, excuse me? Like I'm American, baby—born and raised.

**梁月**：噗……抱歉。\
**Liang Yue**: Heh heh. Sorry.

梁月知道自己应该保持严肃，无奈波蒂埃愤愤不平的控诉，让她最终还是没忍住笑出了声。\
Liáng knows she should remain serious, but she can't help but be tickled by Poitier's indignation.

她的教官瞪了她一眼，却也没有说什么，反而是轻声叹了一口气。\
Poitier shoots her a glare, but then heaves a quiet sigh.

**波蒂埃**：当然，还有些更糟糕的例子，我就不说了。\
**Poitier**: That's not even the half of it.

**波蒂埃**：我并不讨厌这里，但也称不上喜欢。\
最准确的说法是——我和其他警员们都不了解这里。\
**Poitier**: The thing is, I don't hate it here, although I can't say I love Chinatown very much either. To be honest, most of us on the force haven't found a way to make inroads with the people here.

**梁月**：那么就让我们从现在开始试着了解这里吧。\
毕竟我们已经进来了。\
**Liang Yue**: If that's the problem, why don't we try to understand things step by step? Maybe then we can start fresh? We're here anyway.

梁月回过头，用目光向波蒂埃示意道路尽头的那座牌坊。\
距离她们穿过那扇“另一个世界”的入口，已经过去了片刻。\
Liáng turns back and examines the archway at the beginning of the road. They have already been in this "other world" for a while.

**波蒂埃**：……你说得对。\
**Poitier**: Yeah, it's worth a shot.

**波蒂埃**：这一系列被隐瞒的“怪事”背后的真相，至少离我们已不远了……\
**Poitier**: If we're gonna get anywhere, then we'll have to start here.

**波蒂埃**：不过在那之前，我们得先把另一件“正事”办了。\
**Poitier**: But we need to check another task off our list first.

二人穿过大街，拐入一条唐人街内的小巷。\
They cross the street and turn into a narrow alleyway.

**波蒂埃**：穿过这条巷子应该就到了。\
是不是很开心，菜鸟？\
**Poitier**: Should be right there, down the alley. Feeling excited, rookie?

**波蒂埃**：我们马上就要去见你最喜欢的菲林士多导演了。\
**Poitier**: We're about to pay a visit to your favorite director, Noire.

**梁月**：我只是喜欢那部电影，对它的导演并没有什么特别的感情——\
**Liang Yue**: Favorite? What? No. I just like the movies, that's all. I've got no specific feelings for the director.

梁月忍不住反驳，但在波蒂埃揶揄的目光下，最终止住了话语。\
Liáng can't hold back her rebuttal, but under Poitier's teasing gaze, she stops herself.

**梁月**：……好吧，还是有那么一点期待的。\
我的确很想看看拍摄出我最喜欢的电影的导演究竟是什么人。\
**Liang Yue**: Maybe just a little. I am curious about the mind of the director behind such great movies.

**梁月**：但这是工作，我会将它和我个人的感情与喜好分开。\
**Liang Yue**: But this is strictly a police matter, so I will act with professional self-restraint.

**梁月**：我已经联系夜巡特遣的情报部门，请求他们帮忙整理关于菲林士多导演的个人信息，以及可能和事件有关的情报，相信一会儿就会有结果了。\
**Liang Yue**: Actually, I've made a request with the Vigiles Intelligence branch for a file on Director Noire and any related events. We should get it soon.

**波蒂埃**：这么上心？\
**Poitier**: You've got a file on her already? Feels like you're going a bit overboard, rookie.

**波蒂埃**：虽然说那位大导演受到了人身威胁，但记录显示当时是她的助理报的警，后续菲林士多本人联系了警方，说一切都是误会……\
**Poitier**: It wasn't actually the director that called us. Her assistant did. Later on, Noire herself contacted us and said the so-called threat was just a misunderstanding.

**波蒂埃**：近些年大环境好了不少，那些针对神秘学家的激进行为已经很少见了。\
按理来讲，那次报警应当被作为误报处理。\
**Poitier**: Normally, we'd leave it at that. There's too much real crime out there to bother with a case where the victim doesn't think anything happened.

**波蒂埃**：只是报警时那个助理说得煞有其事，接警员担心有什么隐情，才把这件事排进了我们的待处理事项里。\
**Poitier**: Still, according to Dispatch, the assistant was real spooked over it. The operator got the feeling we should give it a second look, so they kept the file open.

**波蒂埃**：咱们优先了这个紧急程度并不高的案子，只是因为咱们需要有个借口进来唐人街，你没有忘记吧？\
**Poitier**: But look, this is just a follow-up and an excuse to come down here. So, keep your mind on the real mission.

**梁月**：当然没有。\
**Liang Yue**: Got it, ma'am.

昨日神秘学犯罪科中的情景浮现在梁月的眼前。\
The scene from the Division of Arcane Affairs yesterday flashes across Liáng's mind.

离开医院后，二人立刻返回神秘学犯罪科汇报了她们的发现，并指出了唐人街“怪事”背后所存在的隐患。\
After leaving the hospital, they immediately returned to report their findings and highlight the dangers lurking behind Chinatown's strange events.

——但上头显然有另一番判断。\
But the higher-ups had a different take on things.

**波蒂埃**：说是已经转交给负责那一带的人了，他们会继续调查这件事。\
但……\
**Poitier**: It's been reassigned to the local precinct.

从警长办公室中走出的波蒂埃对梁月摇了摇头，敏锐的少女立刻从自己教官的神情中察觉到了端倪。\
Poitier stands in the doorway to the Deputy Chief's Office and shakes her head. Liáng immediately catches the subtle shift in her expression.

**梁月**：有哪里不妥吗？\
**Liang Yue**: What's wrong? What does that mean?

**波蒂埃**：神秘学警察一直是紧俏货。我认识负责跟进的人，人品和能力都说得过去，但他们并没有接受过调查神秘学事件的培训。\
**Poitier**: Nothing, kid. It's just most of the force aren't trained to deal with arcane crimes. Don't get me wrong. They're good, capable officers, but I'm worried.

**波蒂埃**：如果要查的是普通案子，也许没有什么可担心的。\
可显然，我们面对的是神秘学案件。\
**Poitier**: If this was any other case, I'd keep my mouth shut, but come on, this is clearly our department. This case has arcanum all over it.

**波蒂埃**：说实话，我不认为他们能够查出什么有价值的东西。\
**Poitier**: I don't think they know what they're getting into.

**梁月**：……\
**Liang Yue**: ...

二人相对无言了片刻。\
但忽然，梁月眼前一亮。\
For a brief moment, neither speaks. Then, Liáng's eyes light up.

**梁月**：等等，我有了一个想法。\
或许我们可以这样做——\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Poitier, I have an idea. What if we ...

**波蒂埃**：借调查那位大导演受到人身威胁一事的机会进入唐人街，由我们亲自查清唐人街的“怪事”……\
**Poitier**: We prioritize Noire's case, which just happens to put us in Chinatown. So, there's no harm in asking a few questions about our other investigation.

**波蒂埃**：真有你的！老实交代，你是不是经常披着一张老实孩子的绵羊皮，干这种钻规则空子的事情？\
**Poitier**: I knew there was a little rebel in you, Liáng. You like to bend the rules, just not break 'em, am I right?

**梁月**：咳……也不是经常。\
**Liang Yue**: Um, not too often.

**梁月**：而且虽说菲林士多导演的案子只是我们为了应对报告拉来的幌子，我认为我们也应当认真对待……\
**Liang Yue**: Actually, I think we're obliged to take Ms. Noire's case seriously, even if it wouldn't help us with the other case.

**梁月**：嗯？稍等，我的联络装置响了。\
**Liang Yue**: Please wait a minute. It's my communication device.

梁月将那个总被基金会内部人士诟病过于笨重的通信器拿了出来。\
波蒂埃凑了过来，趴在她胸口的变色龙通信器也好奇地伸长了脑袋。\
Liáng pulls out the communication device often criticized by Foundation employees for being too bulky. Poitier leans in to get a better look. Her chameleon comm perched on her chest stretches its neck in curiosity.

**系统音**：SPF-I型便携联络装置已开启。\
检测到您有一封新的邮件，正在为您下载附件……\
**Notification**: SPF-I Portable Contact Device activated. You've received a new message. Downloading attachment.

**系统音**：下载完成，请于收件箱中查收。\
**Notification**: Download complete. Please check your mailbox.

**波蒂埃**：邮件？\
是关于什么的？\
**Poitier**: Message? What's it about?

**梁月**：应该是我申请调阅的与菲林士多导演有关的情报，情报科那边给了我回复。\
**Liang Yue**: It's from the Intelligence Department. They've found her records.

**梁月**：菲林士多导演是在基金会登记过的神秘学家，因此基金会那边应该有不少关于她的资料，也许我们可以从中获得一些线索……\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Noire is registered with the Foundation. There might be something in her files that can provide us some clues.

梁月点开被置顶的那一封邮件，一目三行地扫过附件中的信息，声音逐渐低了下去，脸色也凝重了起来。\
She opens the pinned email and scans through the attached files. Her expression turns serious.

**梁月**：等等，这是……八年前发生在香港的……“映像事件”？\
**Liang Yue**: Wait. Is this ...

## SC-07 参演须知 / Rookie Actor's Guide

**工作人员**：这是谁的东西？别放在这里，挡路了，一会儿摄像机要从这里过，快拿走！\
**Crew Member**: Whose is this? It's blocking the camera's sightlines. Get it out of the way!

**龙套演员**：什么时候轮到我们上场？早知道这么久，我也应该带个板凳过来。\
**Extra**: When are we coming in? We've been waiting forever. I wish I brought a chair.

**围观群众**：这是干什么，拍戏？有大明星吗？……\
**Crowd**: What's going on? Are they filming another movie? Do you see anyone famous?

小巷尽头，一处原已空置许久的旧屋内摆满了各式摄影器材，剧组工作人员与演员们穿梭其间，引来过路人好奇的目光。\
At the end of the alley, in an old abandoned house filled with camera equipment, crew members and actors go about their business, drawing curious glances from passersby.

其中一个有些眼熟的身影引起了梁月的注意。\
One particular figure catches Liáng's attention—someone strangely familiar.

**？？？**：哇！这就是今天的盒饭？大叔，我可以打开看看吗？\
**???**: Oh! Is that today's lunch? Mind if I take a look?

**？？？**：还没到放饭时间？好吧……\
**???**: Not now? Fine.

**梁月**：那是……医院里那个形迹可疑的基金会职员。\
**Liang Yue**: That's that odd person I saw at the hospital. She works for the Foundation.

**波蒂埃**：摄像头脑袋的那一个？\
可疑是什么意思，假冒的？\
**Poitier**: Who? You mean camera-head over there? What do you mean by odd? You think she could be a fake?

**梁月**：不……我在向情报科申请调阅资料的时候，也查了关于她的事情。\
**Liang Yue**: No, she's a real Foundation member. I checked her information as well when I inquired about Ms. Noire's file.

**梁月**：她名叫莱瑟姆，是一名意识唤醒者，供职于圣洛夫基金会神秘学藏品管理部。\
**Liang Yue**: Her name is Latham, an Awakened arcanist, currently working in the Arcanum Containment Department.

**梁月**：以我目前的权限还无法随意调阅她的详细个人信息，不过莱瑟姆小姐的身份看起来并没有什么问题。\
**Liang Yue**: I wasn't given any access to her details. But based on our encounter, we should have no problem with her.

**波蒂埃**：那就暂时别管了。\
意识唤醒者，或多或少有些怪癖。\
**Poitier**: Good, fine. I'm happy enough leaving the Awakened to their quirkiness.

这的确不是她们眼下最应先关注的事，梁月暂时放下了心里那份怪异的感觉，和波蒂埃一起穿过围观的人群，踏入片场之中。\
She isn't their top priority—Liáng knows that. She pushes aside that odd feeling for now, following Poitier through the crowd and onto the set.

**助理**：导演还没有吃饭？\
她又这样，也不管自己的身体，之前医生都那样提醒她……\
**Assistant**: What do you mean she hasn't eaten yet? Director Noire's doctor was explicit that she is not allowed to skip any meals.

**助理**：嗯？\
……两位警官，请问有什么事吗？\
**Assistant**: Oh, hello, officers. How can I help you?

一位打扮入时的女子注意到了二人，走上前来。\
The well-dressed woman walks over to them.

**波蒂埃**：我们之前接到了来自琳·王女士的电话，称菲林士多导演遭遇了不知名人士的跟踪和威胁。\
**Poitier**: We received a call from a Lin Wang. Did you make a report about some unknown person making physical threats and stalking Ms. Noire?

**助理**：哦……您是说那件事。\
我就是王琳，但……\
**Assistant**: Yes. That's right. I'm Lin, but ...

听说梁月二人的来意后，女子的面上露出了迟疑的神情。\
她犹豫地看向片场的一侧。\
Upon hearing their purpose, Lin hesitates, glancing uncertainly over at one end of the set.

**演员Ⅰ**：干得好，伙计们！\
**Actor I**: We did it!

**演员Ⅱ**：哦，艾比！你在这里——\
**Actor II**: Abby?! You're here!

**菲林士多**：停。\
**Noire**: Cut.

角落坐在轮椅上的那人一声令下，场上所有的士兵都停下了手中的动作。\
At this single command, the actors freeze in place.

**菲林士多**：不行。刚才你的情绪不对。\
**Noire**: No. I'm afraid we'll have to roll that again.

**演员Ⅱ**：不、不好意思！\
导演……\
**Actor II**: I-I'm sorry, director.

被点到的那个年轻人立刻手足无措了起来。\
他淹没在一众演员之中，显然只是这一幕中的一个小角色。\
The young actor's body stiffens instantly. Based on where he's standing, it's clear that he is only a background character in this scene.

但显然，端坐于她的专属王座之上，纵览全局的菲林士多并没有遗漏这名普通士兵略有瑕疵的表现。\
But Noire, seated on her throne-like wheelchair—the overseer of everything—didn't miss his mistake, no matter how minor it was.

**菲林士多**：她的确是你的恋人，但现在你处在一个长时间单方面和她断了联系的状态。\
**Noire**: Not at all. I just want more emotion this time. She's your true love, but you have been apart for a long time. Things are different now. She is, you are.

**菲林士多**：现在你们重逢了，你当然应该欢喜，但不能是纯粹的欢喜，还需要带上一些担忧、一些心虚。\
**Noire**: Your reunion must be more complex. It isn't simply happiness you feel. You must mix that emotion with worry and guilt.

**菲林士多**：她并不知道你这边的特殊情况。你会想，她会不会误会你？会不会有怨言？又会不会在这期间遇到什么其他的麻烦事？\
**Noire**: She doesn't know anything about what happened to you. You can't help but worry that she will never be able to understand you. You wonder if she has got herself into any troubles.

**菲林士多**：这个镜头只是一闪而过，可还是会呈现给观众。\
你们也是这场戏的一份子，我希望你能做得更好。\
**Noire**: I know this is a short scene, but the audience must see your full range of emotions. You are capable of more, so be more.

**菲林士多**：我记得你是戏剧学院出身的……我想这应该难不倒你？\
**Noire**: I know you attended drama school, so let's see that training shine. I know you can do it.

**演员Ⅱ**：当然……当然，导演！\
我会做到的！\
**Actor II**: Yes, director. I'll try my best.

自己被大名鼎鼎的导演记住了，青年的受宠若惊一目了然。\
他立刻直起了腰杆，一扫方才战战兢兢的畏缩模样。\
Simply being noticed by the famous director is enough to leave him visibly flustered. He immediately straightens up, shedding his nervous stance from moments before.

**菲林士多**：很好，那我们再来一次。\
**Noire**: Good. Let's roll it again.

**助理**：咳……导演，打扰一下。\
**Assistant**: Ahem, excuse me, Director Noire?

助理看准机会，在又一次的拍摄开始前三步并作两步走上前去，在菲林士多的身边耳语了一番。\
Seizing this moment before the next take, the assistant swoops in and whispers something to Noire.

**菲林士多**：……\
**Noire**: ...

其间，菲林士多向梁月她们的方向看了一眼。她神色平静，并不见丝毫意外之色，看不出究竟在想什么。\
Noire glances toward the two officers, her face betraying no emotion. It's impossible to tell what she's thinking.

**波蒂埃**：我只知道菲林士多拍了很多有名的电影，倒还是第一次知道她是坐轮椅的。\
**Poitier**: Huh, for someone that famous, you'd think I'd have known she uses a wheelchair.

**波蒂埃**：喂，怎么样？\
终于见到你心心念的菲林士多大导演了，是不是很激动？\
**Poitier**: How you feeling? Finally getting a chance to meet your favorite director. Thrilled?

波蒂埃趁机用手肘捅了梁月一下，微微俯下身来拿她打趣。\
但看到梁月的表情，她却是一愣。\
Poitier nudges Liáng with her elbow, tilting forward a little as she teases her. But when she sees Liáng's face, she pauses.

**波蒂埃**：怎么愁眉苦脸的？\
刚才在路上的时候，你不是还挺兴奋的吗？\
**Poitier**: What's with the long face, kid? Where'd all your excitement go?

**波蒂埃**：……是那封邮件？\
**Poitier**: Oh. Is it about the message you got?

**梁月**：是的。\
……里面有些事情，很让人在意。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes. It's just something that's bothering me.

但没等梁月来得及向波蒂埃详细解释，她们讨论的对象就已经操控着轮椅来到了她们的面前。\
Before Liáng can explain, the subject of their discussion rolls toward them in her wheelchair.

**菲林士多**：感谢你们的到来，两位尊敬的警官小姐。\
但我想我应该已经致电说明过了，这一切实际上是一场误会。\
**Noire**: Thanks for coming, officers. But I believe I've already explained that this was all just a misunderstanding.

**菲林士多**：如两位所见，我现在安然无恙——当然，除了这老毛病之外。\
**Noire**: As you can see, I'm in perfect health, well, ignoring these two.

她拍了拍自己的双腿，笑得清朗。看来这位著名导演并不介意自己身体上的残缺，但显然这种玩笑外人很难捧场。\
She pats her legs with a cheerful laugh. It seems the director has no qualms about her physical condition, though it's hardly the kind of joke anyone else can comfortably laugh along to.

**波蒂埃**：但您的助理王女士报警时曾声称，近几个月来有不明人士始终在对您进行跟踪行为，您还收到了一封“威胁信”。\
**Poitier**: But according to your assistant, there's been someone stalking you for months, and they've recently sent you a threatening letter.

**波蒂埃**：这些都是误会吗？\
**Poitier**: So what—that all just "misunderstandings" too?

**菲林士多**：对此我真的很抱歉。\
阿琳跟了我有段时间了，她很关心我，有的时候会有些反应过度。\
**Noire**: I'm terribly sorry for inconveniencing you, officers. Lin is a very dedicated assistant, always looking out for me. She may have just overreacted to my situation.

**菲林士多**：无意自吹自擂，警官，但我姑且小有名气，无论走到哪里，都可能会有一些狂热的影迷做出一些稍微越界的行为。\
**Noire**: I don't mean to brag, but I've been in the limelight for long enough that I've seen my share of crazy fans.

**菲林士多**：对此，我已经习惯了。\
**Noire**: I'm used to it.

**波蒂埃**：但那封信的确存在，对吗？\
可以给我看看吗？\
**Poitier**: Sure, I get that. But about that letter you received, do you still have it?

菲林士多苦笑着摇了摇头。\
Noire lets out a wry chuckle and shakes her head.

**菲林士多**：我恐怕现在我们已经很难找到它了。\
**Noire**: I'm afraid I don't have it anymore.

**菲林士多**：每到一个新地方，我都会收到许多封来信。\
有些较为友善，有些则并非如此。\
**Noire**: I receive so many letters, most of them friendly, some of them not-so-much friendly.

**菲林士多**：在这个圈子里多年，我帮助了不少人，但显然也有意无意得罪过一些人。\
您所提到的那一封就来自后者，我没有特意保留它们的习惯。\
**Noire**: I've made a name in this industry, and a few enemies too. If I paid any attention to the negativity, it'd only drag me down. I tend not to keep the bad ones around.

**菲林士多**：总有人期待着在我身上，发生些比再也站不起来更糟糕的事情。\
如果能有两位英姿飒爽的警官小姐护卫左右，我自然也会安心不少。\
**Noire**: While I'm sure you would do a fine job keeping me safe, officers, I can't let myself worry over it. Besides, what are they going to do? Break my kneecaps?

**菲林士多**：令人为难的是……对于剧组来说，二位的存在可能会让大家产生一些不必要的忧虑。\
**Noire**: Frankly, the only thing I am worried about is that your presence is another distraction for my crew.

她投来一个带着感激与歉意的眼神。\
She casts a grateful, and perhaps apologetic, look around the set.

**菲林士多**：非常感谢二位警官的关心，但我必须为电影的质量负责。\
我希望保证每一次搬上银幕的作品都是最好的。\
**Noire**: So, it's very much appreciated that you went out of your way to check in on me, but I have a movie to make. I can't disappoint my fans.

**菲林士多**：现在，警官们。\
如果没有别的事，就请原谅我先失陪了。\
**Noire**: Now, if you'll excuse me, we're burning daylight, and I still have four more scenes to film.

**菲林士多**：今天还有四五场戏等着我们去拍。我在荷里活这边的制片人许可了不少我就拍摄提出的任性请求，相对地也给我出了不少难题。\
**Noire**: These Hollywood producers may have opened doors for me, but they also give me so many problems lately.

她向梁月与波蒂埃二人笑了笑，似乎打算以此为这场对话的终止符。\
She smiles at the officers, as if to signal the conversation's end.

**梁月**：——只是因为电影吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Is this really just because of your movie?

已经调转了轮椅方向的菲林士多，因梁月的话停下了动作。\
Noire has already begun to turn her wheelchair away, but Liáng stops her in her tracks.

**菲林士多**：您是指？\
**Noire**: Pardon me?

**梁月**：您拒绝了我们的帮助和调查，理由是您认为那些威胁不过是常见的恶作剧和并不会被付诸于行动的诳言，并不值得以引起过度的重视。\
**Liang Yue**: You seem to be refusing our assistance because you've decided this threat is only a harmless prank.

**梁月**：您认为它们并不值得付出让警方进入剧组、带来例如媒体的过度关注等麻烦的代价去解决。\
**Liang Yue**: You've decided that it's worth the risk to focus on your film.

**梁月**：这是您的选择，我无意妄加评论，它也的确在某种程度上说的通——\
**Liang Yue**: I don't mean to judge your decision. It may be understandable in some cases.

梁月在菲林士多审视的目光中走到她的近前，俯身在菲林士多的耳边轻轻落下最后一句话。\
She moves closer, lowering her voice as she leans in to deliver the next sentence in a hushed voice.

**梁月**：——在“没有任何迹象表示您的周围存在实质危险”的情况下。\
**Liang Yue**: But if this threat is not just a prank, if it is serious ...

**菲林士多**：……听起来警官小姐并不这么认为？\
**Noire**: Am I sensing disapproval?

菲林士多微微眯起双眼，抬手制止了正欲靠近的助理。\
Noire narrows her eyes a little and raises a hand to halt her approaching assistant.

这是成功的标志，对话得以延续，梁月获得了追问的机会。\
她收起心底复杂的情绪，继续用只有二人能够听到的音量说了下去。\
This is a good sign. Liáng has earned the chance to talk for at least a little longer. She pushes aside her conflicting emotions and carries on in a voice only the two of them can hear.

**梁月**：从数日前开始，唐人街附近的医院就不断收到因不明原因导致精神状态异常的患者。\
**Liang Yue**: There has been an increase in patients coming from Chinatown showing signs of mental instability.

**梁月**：暴躁易怒、颓废嗜睡、思维混乱、记忆缺失……尽管症状各不相同，但他们此前都并无相关病史，原因至今不明。\
**Liang Yue**: Their symptoms include confusion, amnesia, drowsiness, and volatile anger. None of the patients seem to have anything in common. No prior history, all without clear cause.

**梁月**：这番描述会让您感到熟悉吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Does that sound familiar?

**菲林士多**：抱歉，也许警官小姐能够给我一些提示？\
**Noire**: Sorry, is this leading somewhere?

略作思索后，菲林士多摇了摇头，平静的表情中带着少许恰到好处的茫然。\
After a moment of thought, Noire shakes her head, her calm face carrying a perfectly measured hint of confusion.

**梁月**：……八年前，在您的身边应当也发生过极其类似的事件。\
**Liang Yue**: A case, eight years ago.

**梁月**：与您一起打造了您的成名作《神秘警探C07》系列电影的编剧何日君，在八年前于自家燃起的熊熊大火中身亡。\
**Liang Yue**: Hé Rìjūn, the scriptwriter for your first big hit, Detective C07. She burned to death in her own house.

**梁月**：但在化为一片废墟的火灾现场，负责现场清理的工作人员却发现了一盘完好无缺的胶片。\
**Liang Yue**: However, the cleaners found a film reel in the debris, surprisingly intact after the fire.

**菲林士多**：……\
**Noire**: ...

梁月一直紧紧盯着菲林士多的表情，因此她并没有错过菲林士多在听到“胶片”一词时，一瞬间眼神的变化。\
Liáng has been watching Noire's every expression. She doesn't miss the fleeting shift in her eyes at the mention of the film reel.

**梁月**：很奇怪，对吧？明明现场的其他物品都变成了看不出原型的焦炭，但只有那盘超8毫米胶片完好如初。\
**Liang Yue**: Strange, isn't it? Every other item was burned to ash, yet this one 8mm reel was as good as new.

**梁月**：当时的那些工作人员也是百思不得其解，所以他们放映了那部影片。\
**Liang Yue**: The cleaners felt the same way, so, being curious, they played the reel.

**梁月**：——结果五个人中三人被送进了精神病院，一人坠楼身亡，最后一人虽无大碍，但也是性情大变，成了一副行尸走肉般的模样。\
**Liang Yue**: Three of the five who watched it ended up in an asylum, one jumped from a building, and the last, according to the reports, became like an empty shell of a person.

**菲林士多**：你认为那件事和如今唐人街的“怪事”很相似。\
**Noire**: And what's happening here reminds you of that?

**梁月**：鉴于二者之间的相似性，我认为不能排除这两起事件有关联的可能。\
**Liang Yue**: There are some commonalities between the cases. I can't ignore the possibility that they're related.

**梁月**：毕竟受害者表现出的症状十分相似，而这两起事件中……也都有您的身影出现。\
**Liang Yue**: Two in particular stand out to me, the similar symptoms of those affected, and you.

**梁月**：若说是偶然，我想有些太过于巧合了。\
**Liang Yue**: Hard to shake the thought that these are not coincidences.

片场中的其他人听不到二人谈话的具体内容，但拍摄暂缓的时间远比他们想象中的更久，这引发了一阵阵的窃窃私语。\
Whispers spark among the crew as they eye this secret conversation.

**群众演员**：那两个警察找菲林士多导演做什么？\
还要多久啊？\
**Extra**: What are the police still here for? Are we gonna get back to filming?

**工作人员**：总感觉不是什么好事。\
我们只是想要拍电影，怎么总是有人来找麻烦？\
**Crew Member**: Who knows, but it doesn't seem good. We're losing light here. Can these guys wrap it up already?

那些声音自然也落入了菲林士多与梁月的耳中。\
再开口时，菲林士多的态度干脆了许多。\
These murmurs, of course, don't escape Noire's and Liáng's notice. When she speaks again, Noire's tone is far more direct.

**菲林士多**：这是一则指控吗？\
**Noire**: Is that an accusation?

**梁月**：不，当然不。\
我只是在考虑假如这两起案件相关，也许您能够提供一些线索。\
**Liang Yue**: No, not at all. I'm just hoping you might be able to shed some light on our case.

**梁月**：八年前的事件经夜巡特遣的调查，被正式认定为恶性神秘学事件，罪魁祸首就是编剧何日君留下的那盘胶片——《三燕归巢》。\
**Liang Yue**: After our initial investigation, we officially recorded it as an ominous arcanum incident, and determined that the cause was that 8mm film reel, which contained a film titled Reunion of the Three Swallows.

**梁月**：可尽管已经结案，案件仍然残留了部分疑点。\
最关键的……便是那盘胶片侵蚀无辜者精神的原因，至今未能查清。\
**Liang Yue**: To this day, however, the exact nature of the arcanum hasn't been conclusively determined. We still aren't sure why it has this strange effect on people's minds, nor why the damage appears to be irreversible.

**梁月**：所有的神秘学存在都有其起源，像是“胶片”这类原本并不具有神秘学属性的物品更是如此。一定有什么契机让它发生了转变。\
**Liang Yue**: Perhaps more importantly, we still don't know the origin behind the arcanum on the reel. There are many possible causes that might create such an effect.

**梁月**：……而吸收了来自神秘学家的某种强烈感情，是普通物品非预期性地转化为神秘学物品最常见的原因。\
**Liang Yue**: One of the most common thoughts is from absorbing powerful emotions from an arcanist.

**梁月**：其中，憎恶、愤怒、仇恨……这些来自人心黑暗面的情感，拥有着超乎想象的强大力量。\
**Liang Yue**: The darkest emotions possess the strongest power, anger, hatred ...

**梁月**：即使孕育出它们的人已经死去，它们仍然能够以“诅咒”的形式留存在世间，完成主人未尽的执念。\
**Liang Yue**: Emotions so strong that they can outlast their bearer's death, like a curse from beyond the grave carrying out their last will as an obsession.

**梁月**：——这通常意味着一场灾难。\
**Liang Yue**: And in such cases, these objects are sure to lead to disaster.

**梁月**：《三燕归巢》表现出的性质就符合这一特征，毫无疑问，它是一张“被诅咒的胶片”。\
**Liang Yue**: I believe that this film is, undoubtedly, one such cursed item.

**梁月**：如果这次的事件也是那部胶片造成的，我们需要弄清楚它的目的，才能够拿出对策。\
**Liang Yue**: If it is the case that this film was involved in these new incidents, then we must find out what obsession it's carrying out, and find a countermeasure.

**菲林士多**：而听起来警官小姐已经有调查的方向了。\
**Noire**: I assume you're already on the case.

**梁月**：……当年负责调查那起案件的神秘学警察，在档案中留下了自己的调查报告和推测。\
**Liang Yue**: Indeed, I am, Ms. Noire. I've been studying the report on the original case, including some of the theories of the original investigator.

**梁月**：种种迹象指出，作为共同缔造了《神秘警探C07》系列电影的伙伴，您与编剧何日君在背地里却存在着许多嫌隙。\
**Liang Yue**: One of those theories suggests that despite your collaboration on the C07 series, there were many points of conflict between you and Ms. Hé.

**梁月**：在何日君葬身火海的当天，您与她曾经爆发过激烈的冲突，而在何日君死后，更是有传闻称她的死与您脱不了干系……\
**Liang Yue**: In fact, the reports mention you had a violent quarrel with her on the day of the fire. There was even a question about whether you might have been responsible for her death.

**梁月**：您愿意谈谈这件事吗？因为如果造成眼下唐人街怪事频发的罪魁祸首，真的是八年前的那张“被诅咒的胶片”……\
**Liang Yue**: So, as you can see, I have more than a strong reason to believe you are connected. And if this cursed reel is behind these recent incidents ...

**梁月**：那么我恐怕，它最有可能瞄准的目标，就是您。\
**Liang Yue**: I'm afraid that you may be the intended target of this curse.

## SC-08 餐后审问室 / Post-lunch Questioning

**波蒂埃**：真是可恶！\
我必须得说，那位导演的电影很有趣，可她本人就完全不同了。\
**Poitier**: Hot damn, rookie. Who coulda guessed the famous director would be a part of her own real-life thriller.

**波蒂埃**：费了九牛二虎之力，却根本没得到什么有用的信息……\
我最讨厌那种整天面上挂着笑脸，却根本看不懂她在想什么的人了。\
**Poitier**: After talking to her, we still got nothing useful to go on. I can't read anything behind that smiling face of hers.

**波蒂埃**：如果在唐人街作乱的真的是那张“被诅咒的胶片”，危险的可是她耶！\
居然一点也不着急。\
**Poitier**: But if your little theory has got any truth to it, then Noire is in real danger. So, why not talk? Isn't she worried about her own life?

波蒂埃化愤怒为食欲，眨眼间桌上的餐点就消失了大半。\
咽下最后一只虾饺，她回头看向不远处正和老板娘攀谈的搭档。\
Poitier channels her frustration into her food, devouring most of the meal in the blink of an eye. As she swallows the last shrimp dumpling, she turns to look at Liáng, who is busy chatting with the restaurant owner.

**梁月**：是吗？原来对面杂货店那家的女儿也……\
**Liang Yue**: You mean the grocer's daughter has also ...

**老板娘**：就是咯！最近都不知道搞什么，好多街坊家里都出了事。\
**Female Storekeeper**: Yes. So many, many things happening around the neighborhood. Crazy!

**老板娘**：老林家还算好啦。他带个女儿去看了中医，抓了药，吃了一段时间就好了不少。\
**Female Storekeeper**: But the Lu's are lucky. They took their daughter to a good local doctor, and she got better.

**老板娘**：但是对面街口马仔他阿嫲就麻烦了。那个阿婆原本就身体不好，忽然间又变到疯疯癫癫……他们两公婆都要担心死了！\
**Female Storekeeper**: But the other family down the road aren't so lucky. Their grandma was already so weak from arthritis, and now she's gone crazy. She's probably gonna drive them crazy too.

**老板娘**：之前都有个靓妹来问这件事，说什么事情不太对路……唉，我说啊，就是临近年关，那些污糟的东西都出来了。\
**Female Storekeeper**: You know what? Another girl, she asked around about this too. *sigh* If I had to guess, it's because of those evil spirits. Things are never easy before the Dùshuò Festival.

**梁月**：您说还有人打听过这件事，那是什么人？\
**Liang Yue**: Another girl? Do you know who she is?

**老板娘**：她说自己是什么新科学……新科学什么鬼事务所的，好像是个神婆，刚来到唐人街这一带的。\
**Female Storekeeper**: She said she's an exorcist from the neo-science ... neo-science something ... exorcism office ... and is new here in Chinatown.

**老板娘**：她还给了一张卡片，印到鬼五马六的，不过不知道被我放到哪里了。\
**Female Storekeeper**: She gave me a fancy business card. But I don't know where it is now.

**梁月**：……原来如此，多谢您。\
**Liang Yue**: I see. Thank you very much.

向老板娘道过谢后，梁月返回座位，波蒂埃立刻投去疑问的眼神。\
As Liáng returns to her seat, Poitier shoots her a questioning look.

**波蒂埃**：怎么样？\
**Poitier**: So, any progress?

**梁月**：有两个坏消息。受害者的数目比我们之前认为的还要多，并且……\
我们并不是唯一察觉到这一事件的人。\
**Liang Yue**: I have some bad news. First, there are more victims than we expected; second, we're not the only ones who've noticed.

**梁月**：如果想要在引起恐慌和不必要的骚动前解决事件，我们就需要抓紧了。\
**Liang Yue**: We need to hurry if we don't want this case to attract wider attention.

**波蒂埃**：那个菲林士多导演不能成为突破口吗？\
**Poitier**: Why don't we start with the director, then? She seems like our best lead.

解决掉了眼前一圈的餐点，波蒂埃将摆在桌边的叉烧包拉到了自己的面前。\
Having cleared the dishes closest to her, Poitier pulls the char siu buns from the other side of the table.

**波蒂埃**：没想到原本只是我们用来作为进入唐人街的借口的事件，居然和我们在调查的事有关系。\
**Poitier**: I've got a hunch her case is connected with this one.

**波蒂埃**：你也说了，发生在那个菲林士多导演过去的事件和现在发生在唐人街的事非常相似，这未免有些过于巧合了。\
**Poitier**: Just like you said, there are too many coincidences to not dig deeper.

**波蒂埃**：那个编剧何日君也是神秘学家。在被烈火焚身的弥留之际，她的怨恨被自己的作品吸收……这样的案件在神秘学犯罪科中并不罕见。\
**Poitier**: That writer, what was it, Hé Rìjūn? She's an arcanist, right? No surprise that she'd imbue that film with all of her final bits of hatred. I've seen a dozen cases like it.

**波蒂埃**：那种含有诅咒的物件往往邪乎的很，搞不好就是追着菲林士多来了唐人街，其他受害者都只是被殃及池鱼而已。\
**Poitier**: Cursed objects are weird as heck. It's definitely possible that it could've chased Noire all the way here.

**梁月**：“菲林士多导演与何日君之死有关”只是一个传闻而已，并没有任何证据能够证明何日君临死时对菲林士多怀有怨恨。\
**Liang Yue**: But there isn't any evidence that corroborates the rivalry between Ms. Noire and Ms. Hé.

**波蒂埃**：但就连你们夜巡特遣管理局都把这件事写进了情报里，不就说明了这件事并不全是空穴来风吗？\
**Poitier**: Hold on. Didn't you read that in a report by another vigil? Maybe it's only hearsay, but that's something.

**波蒂埃**：在那个看了胶片之后精神失常，最终跑到建设中的高楼一跃而下的家伙摔成一块肉饼的同一晚，菲林士多遭遇车祸，双腿残疾……\
**Poitier**: Not only that. Get this—I did some digging of my own. The night that cleaner leaped off that roof was the exact same night that Noire was in the car accident that left her legs paralyzed.

**波蒂埃**：这两件事发生的时间只相隔不到五分钟，发生的地点只相距一条街。\
难道你要说这是巧合？\
**Poitier**: It gets freakier. According to the reports, they happened within minutes of each other, and the building was less than a block away from the scene of the accident. How's that for evidence?

**波蒂埃**：我告诉你，做神秘学警察最忌讳的一个词，就是“巧合”。\
**Poitier**: We've got a saying in the DAA, cadet. "When it comes to arcanum, there's no such thing as coincidences."

伴随着这句斩钉截铁的结论，最后一只叉烧包被波蒂埃吞进了腹中。\
With this declaration, Poitier pops the last char siu bun into her mouth.

**梁月**：……但这始终是推测，并未得到证实。\
**Liang Yue**: Whether coincidence or not, it isn't much to go on. We need evidence.

**波蒂埃**：是这样没错啦，但我的意思是说，当我们察觉到某些诡异的“偶然”时，彻查到底就是我们神秘学警察的工作……\
**Poitier**: Of course. We can't just leap to accusations without proof. But when it comes to arcane crime, you've gotta follow your hunches. So, keep your nose to the ground.

话说到一半，波蒂埃终于察觉到对面少女的低落，讪讪放下手中攥着的筷子。\
Poitier notices the dejection on Liáng's face and sheepishly sets down her chopsticks.

**波蒂埃**：我明白你的心情，喜欢的电影背后居然有这么多乌烟瘴气的事，多少会有些幻灭。\
**Poitier**: I get you. This isn't just about evidence. You don't wanna point the finger at someone you admire.

**波蒂埃**：有时候我们被告知要远离那些作品背后的人是有道理的。\
**Poitier**: But you've gotta pursue this, even if that means you have to separate the artist from their work.

梁月沉默片刻，拿起桌上的冰镇柠檬汽水喝了一口，重新振作了起来。\
Liáng remains silent for a moment, picks up the chilled lemon soda from the table, and takes a sip.

**梁月**：我不敢确定菲林士多导演以及八年前的“映像事件”和现在的唐人街发生的怪事有关联，其实还有另外一个原因。\
**Liang Yue**: Actually, there is another reason that I'm not entirely convinced that Ms. Noire, the "film incident," and the events in Chinatown are connected.

**梁月**：当年引发事件的那张“被诅咒的胶片”《三燕归巢》，其实早在事件过后约半年就被圣洛夫基金会回收了。\
**Liang Yue**: In fact, it's quite a substantial reason. If our records are correct, the cursed reel was found and contained by the Foundation six months after the initial incident.

**梁月**：现在它应该处在神秘学藏品管理部的监管之下，除非由于什么特殊原因，它从基金会内被流出到了外界，否则是不可能——\
**Liang Yue**: Which means, unless something has gone horribly wrong, it should still be safely stored within the Arcanum Containment Depart—

尖锐的破碎声打断了梁月的话，二人循声向一旁的座位上看去。\
A sharp crash interrupts her words. The two turn toward the sound.

**斯考特**：呃，抱歉抱歉，真是对不起……\
**Scott**: Oops! I'm sorry. I'm so sorry.

一个戴眼镜的少女正手忙脚乱地捏起桌上的纸巾，试图收拾不小心打翻在地的餐盘碎片。\
A bespectacled girl fumbles with a napkin as she hurriedly tries to clean up the shattered dish she just knocked over.

——但她时不时瞥向梁月与波蒂埃这桌的眼神，和胸前令人眼熟的徽章，当然并没有逃过两名年轻警员的目光。\
But her sneaking glances toward the two officers don't escape their attention, and the shiny emblem on her chest tells them exactly where she's from.

**梁月**：…………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

**波蒂埃**：呃…………\
**Poitier**: Well ...

她们交换了一个怪异的眼神。\
They exchange a puzzled look.

**波蒂埃**：说起来，你是不是说你昨天也遇到了一个形迹可疑的基金会成员？\
**Poitier**: If I remember it right, you mentioned earlier that you saw someone from the Foundation acting suspicious yesterday.

**梁月**：是的，而……根据资料，那个人正好是供职于神秘学藏品管理部的。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, like the lady over there, she also works for the ACD.

**波蒂埃**：看起来我们有必要找这位小姐聊聊。\
**Poitier**: Guess we'll have a talk with her.

**梁月**：我同意。\
**Liang Yue**: I agree, Ms. Poitier.

她们从桌边站起身，向那名少女走去。\
They rise from the table and approach the girl.

在梁月和波蒂埃不依不饶的逼问下，形迹可疑的基金会成员最终选择了举手投降。\
Under Liáng and Poitier's relentless questioning, the suspicious Foundation member ultimately surrenders.

**斯考特**：好了好了，我说还不行吗！\
**Scott**: Alright, alright. I'll tell.

**斯考特**：但只能和你说。你是执夜人，对吧？\
这是基金会内部的事务，所以……\
**Scott**: But only to you, since you're a vigil, but she isn't, right? Sorry, I should really only disclose this info to other Foundation members.

她小心翼翼地瞥向一旁的波蒂埃。\
She shoots a cautious glance at Poitier.

**波蒂埃**：啧。\
**Poitier**: Hmph.

她并未多说什么，扬了扬下巴表示了许可。\
Poitier says nothing, simply raising her chin at Liáng in approval.

梁月跟着少女从后门离开。四下无人，少女在用便携联络装置确认了梁月的身份后，踌躇片刻，凑到梁月的耳边。\
Liáng follows the girl out into the empty alley. After verifying Liáng's identity with her communication device, the girl gives a final glance up and down the alley before talking.

**斯考特**：见习执夜人梁小姐，既然您被选入了夜巡特遣管理局，就说明您是值得信赖的人。\
**Scott**: There's no one I would trust more than a vigil, Ms. Liáng.

**斯考特**：其实我是为了一项基金会的任务而来，也许……您能够提供一些帮助。\
**Scott**: I'm here on a mission for the Foundation, and you might be able to help me with it.

**佩德拉**：1990年9月，出现在重塑之手下属组织启明会违法集会的未知女性神秘学家制造了严重的人身伤害事件。\
**Pedra**: September 1990, a female arcanist committed a serious assault and caused a number of casualties. She appeared at an illegal gathering held by the Order of Enlightenment, a subordinate organization of Manus Vindictae.

**佩德拉**：司辰在该事件后与此女性神秘学家发生了接触，经调查，确认其身份为超自然者——天使娜娜。\
**Pedra**: The Timekeeper encountered her and confirmed her identity: Anjo Nala, a Beyond arcanist.

**佩德拉**：她诞生自19世纪，推测于1968年被封印进外形如同发条玩具的封印物中，成为了必须听从封印物持有者命令的致命武器。\
**Pedra**: Born sometime in the 19th century, she was sealed inside a wind-up toy in the year 1968. Since then, she has become a lethal weapon that must obey whoever possesses her toy.

**佩德拉**：但早在1985年，我是说“真正的”1985年——\
**Pedra**: But back in 1985, I mean, the real 1985 ...

**佩德拉**：这一封印物本应已被圣洛夫基金会作为“危险神秘学物品”回收，保管于神秘学藏品管理部。\
**Pedra**: That toy had been safely stored in our Arcanum Containment Department as a "dangerous item."

**斯考特**：……有人从基金会偷走了它，将它流出到了外界。\
**Scott**: Until it was stolen.

**佩德拉**：你也参加了那次清点工作。除了编号NO.066“发条玩具”之外，另有四件神秘学管理品被发现失窃。\
**Pedra**: You were involved in that particular inventory check. There are four additional items that are now lost aside from No. 066.

**佩德拉**：“暴雨”的来袭和此前从未出现过的“规避‘暴雨’的咒语”……那场骚乱让我们无暇顾及其他。但毫无疑问，我们的工作出现了疏漏。\
**Pedra**: The circumstances of the last "Storm" and that devastating "spell" threw our whole organization into chaos. However, there's no excuse for failing to uphold our department's most crucial mission.

**佩德拉**：幸运的是，我们很快发现所有线索都指向了同一个嫌犯。\
**Pedra**: Fortunately, it appears that our "break-in" was committed by a single culprit.

**斯考特**：我听到你和你的搭档在餐厅中的对话了，唐人街中发生了许多怪事，对吗？\
**Scott**: I heard what you and your partner just said. It's about all the weird things happening in Chinatown, right?

**斯考特**：最理想的情况，是在莱瑟姆还没有借助那些神秘学物品的力量搞出太大的动静前，将她抓获并回收那些神秘学管理品……\
**Scott**: It was my mission to catch Latham and retrieve all the arcane objects she'd stolen before they caused more damage.

**斯考特**：但显然，事情已经有些迟了。\
**Scott**: But I guess it's already too late for that.

这番话中的意思很明确了，不容得梁月假装听不懂。\
The meaning behind these words is crystal clear. There is no room for Liáng to feign ignorance.

**梁月**：难道说，在那些同样被发现失窃的神秘学管理品中……\
**Liang Yue**: Then you're saying that ...

**斯考特**：你刚才提到的那张“被诅咒的胶片”正是其中之一。\
似乎你们发现了它去向的线索？\
**Scott**: Yes, the cursed reel from the incident you mentioned was among the stolen items. And you said that you have some clue about its current whereabouts?

——“被诅咒的胶片”《三燕归巢》，就在唐人街。\
这个消息和它背后代表的含义让梁月心里一沉。\
The cursed film reel, Reunion of the Three Swallows, is in Chinatown—The weight of this revelation sinks heavily in Liáng's chest.

**斯考特**：也许我们可以合作。我接到的任务，原本是让我隐秘行事……\
但事到如今，我想比起保密，更重要的是尽快回收那些神秘学危险品。\
**Scott**: I was told to operate under strict secrecy, but at this point, the faster they're retrieved, the better. So, shall we work together?

斯考特从怀中掏出了一本笔记本，抽出了夹在里面的一张照片。\
Scott takes a notebook from her pocket and pulls out a photo tucked inside.

**斯考特**：嫌犯叫做莱瑟姆，是一名意识唤醒者。\
**Scott**: Our main suspect is Latham, an Awakened arcanist.

尽管早有心理准备，但在看清照片中除斯考特外的另一名少女时，梁月还是不禁露出了惊讶的表情。\
Liáng can't help but look surprised when she recognizes the other girl in the photograph.

但她的惊讶似乎被斯考特误解为了另一个意思。\
But Scott seems to misinterpret her reaction.

**斯考特**：是啊……她是我的同僚，和我的关系也很好。\
我通常都是叫她“空脑袋”的，因为她平时笨笨的，又经常忘东西……\
**Scott**: It's hard for me to believe she'd do this. We were colleagues and close friends. I used to call her Loggerhead, because she's the most forgetful person I know.

**斯考特**：说实话，我不愿意相信她居然做了这样的事，她看起来并不像是会为了钱而做出这种事的人，但……\
**Scott**: At first, I refused to believe she could do such a thing. I still don't understand why. She's not the kind to be greedy.

**斯考特**：当时负责调查这件事的也是一名执夜人女士，夜巡特遣总不会出错。\
**Scott**: But the Vigiles investigated the theft thoroughly, and the Vigiles are not the kind to make mistakes.

**斯考特**：你刚才说近期你刚好在洛杉矶实习，也许你知道些关于莱瑟姆下落的线索？\
**Scott**: You've been here a few days already, right? Have you had any word about where she might be?

斯考特的眉头紧蹙，眼神满是挣扎，像是既期待听到一个肯定的回复，却又畏惧着那样一个答案。\
Scott's brow furrows, her expression torn between hope and fear. It's as if she wants confirmation while equally dreading to hear the truth.

**梁月**：……\
**Liang Yue**: ...

**梁月**：不，我没有。\
**Liang Yue**: Sorry, I haven't.

梁月摇了摇头。\
She shakes her head.

随即，斯考特的表情肉眼可见地放松了下来。\
Scott's expression visibly relaxes.

**斯考特**：哦……那真是太遗憾了。\
**Scott**: Oh. What a pity.

## SC-09 没头脑嘉宾 / A Name Deserved

**老板娘**：欢迎下次光临——\
**Female Storekeeper**: Have a good day!

老板娘最后的几个音节被拦在了餐馆内，梁月拉着波蒂埃三步并作两步跃出店门。\
Before the owner can even say goodbye, Liáng has yanked Poitier out the front door.

**波蒂埃**：等等，这么着急做什么？我还没有吃饱呢！\
**Poitier**: What's the rush? I haven't even finished my noodles.

**梁月**：您可以留些肚子晚上再吃，现在我们必须立刻找到那名神秘学藏品管理部的职员莱瑟姆！\
**Liang Yue**: We can eat later, but we need to find Ms. Latham, now!

**波蒂埃**：等等，等等！我明白要趁着那个基金会追捕的嫌犯逃到其他地方之前逮住她，但我不明白的是为什么你不直接告诉那个基金会职员？\
**Poitier**: Wait, wait. Hold on. I'm all for chasing down a crook. But why do I get the feeling you didn't tell your Foundation friend about your run-in with Latham?

**波蒂埃**：为什么要瞒着她，在她离开之后偷偷去找那个摄像头脑袋？\
**Poitier**: What's up? Why you keeping her in the dark?

**梁月**：只是以防万一，这件事情让我觉得有些奇怪。\
**Liang Yue**: I think that something isn't right about her.

**梁月**：我们在培训时去过基金会的神秘学藏品管理部，那里看起来满是破绽，但实际上各处都安置了监控的术式。\
**Liang Yue**: I've been to the ACD before. To most, it might seem defenseless, but it's actually heavily protected by arcane rituals.

**梁月**：根据斯考特小姐的说法，那名叫作莱瑟姆的职员是单独作案……\
**Liang Yue**: According to Ms. Scott, Latham acted alone.

**梁月**：但我查询了她的档案，除了是一名意识唤醒者外，她并没有什么特殊之处，在神秘术上的造诣也不过平平。\
**Liang Yue**: But there's nothing in her file that would suggest she's capable of that. Her arcane skill level is frankly far from remarkable.

**梁月**：我并不认为那个叫做莱瑟姆的职员能够仅凭运气，突破神秘学藏品管理部的警戒系统。\
**Liang Yue**: Even with insider knowledge, I don't believe it's possible she could have bypassed the security system and escaped on her own.

**梁月**：显然嫌犯莱瑟姆也许隐藏了实力，又或是有其他同伙……无论如何，这种量级的事，都不应该由一个普通职员负责追捕工作。\
**Liang Yue**: Either Ms. Latham has playing the Foundation for fools, or she has more powerful accomplices. That leads me to another thing. This mission is not something a typical Foundation staff member would be assigned to—as Ms. Scott claimed to be.

**梁月**：——这件事的背后一定有隐情。\
**Liang Yue**: There's something we don't know.

**波蒂埃**：你的意思是说……那个眼镜妹骗了你？\
**Poitier**: You're saying that girl with glasses lied to you?

**梁月**：又或许……她也被蒙在鼓里。\
**Liang Yue**: Maybe, or that she was being lied to herself.

梁月从披风下掏出自己的SPF-Ⅰ型便携联络装置，简单操作两下后，将上面的界面展示给波蒂埃。\
Liáng pulls her SPF-I contact device from beneath her cloak. After a few simple taps, she turns it around for Poitier to see.

**梁月**：我之前在基金会的系统中搜索过关于莱瑟姆的情报，上面并没有出现任何异常提示。\
**Liang Yue**: There was another thing I found while searching through Ms. Latham's files, or rather, what I didn't find—there were no warnings or notices on her employee records.

**波蒂埃**：什么意思，她并没有被通缉？\
**Poitier**: You mean, she's not actually wanted?

**梁月**：不……如果那是个谎言，也未免太容易被戳破了。\
**Liang Yue**: No, I don't think so.

**梁月**：依照斯考特小姐所说，神秘学藏品管理部希望隐秘处理这件事。\
我最初认为也许是因此，抓捕莱瑟姆小姐的消息才没有被公开。\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Scott said that their department wanted to solve this problem in secret, so I thought that might explain the reason Ms. Latham's warrant wasn't on her file.

**梁月**：但随后我又在夜巡特遣管理局的子系统中，搜索了有关神秘学藏品管理部失窃事件，以及莱瑟姆、斯考特小姐的信息……\
**Liang Yue**: However, when I tried to access more of their records to double-check my findings, I ran into a block on Ms. Scott's records.

**系统音**：非常抱歉，您没有权限查看相关信息。如需要查阅，请联系您的上级管理者。\
**Notification**: Access denied. You do not have permission to view this information. If you need access, please contact your supervisor.

显示屏上弹出刺眼的警示符号。\
A warning symbol flashes on the screen.

**梁月**：意味着这里有一些还只是“见习”执夜人的我不被允许获知的信息。\
我联系了我的导师，但并没有收到回复。\
**Liang Yue**: It could just be because I'm only a cadet. There are some files that I don't have access to yet. I contacted my supervisor, but I haven't heard anything back.

**梁月**：我也并不想要怀疑斯考特小姐，但怀疑就是我的工作。\
**Liang Yue**: I don't mean to distrust her, but I can't hold anyone above suspicion.

波蒂埃收回了望向那面拒绝给予她们任何信息的屏幕的目光，看向身旁的少女。\
Poitier shifts her gaze from the device's screen back to Liáng.

**波蒂埃**：……我说，那你就不怀疑我吗？\
和我说这些真的没问题吗？\
**Poitier**: And what about me? You're putting a lot of trust in me, Liáng. Is it really alright that you're telling me all this?

**波蒂埃**：惹出事端来的是从基金会流出的危险神秘学管理品，而罪魁祸首是监守自盗的自家职员……这可是个不小的丑闻。\
**Poitier**: A dangerous item stolen from the Foundation and possibly an inside job at that. That's a scandal in the making.

**波蒂埃**：我现在已经知道你这家伙心眼子绝不少，扯出一个让我挑不出漏洞的谎糊弄过去，对你来说应该也不是难事。\
**Poitier**: You could've just lied to me, make up some kind of story. It's not hard for a smart kid like you.

梁月用怪异的眼神看向了波蒂埃。\
Liáng gives Poitier a puzzled look.

**梁月**：因为我们是搭档。这不是您告诉我的吗？\
我并不认为对自己的搭档隐瞒重要的线索是什么明智之举。\
**Liang Yue**: Why would I? We're partners, Ms. Poitier. Hiding information from you wouldn't be right. You told me that yourself, didn't you?

**波蒂埃**：我？\
**Poitier**: Me?

**梁月**：是的，在我们共同执勤的第一天，在那间餐馆里享用午餐的时候。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, the first day we were on duty together, you said you "need to know what makes me tick."

**波蒂埃**：哦……好像是有那么一回事。\
**Poitier**: Hmm, I did, didn't I?

波蒂埃的反应慢了半拍，看起来有些发愣。\
这让梁月不由得疑惑地看了自己的教官两眼。\
Poitier seems a little dazed. Liáng looks at her, sincerity behind her eyes.

**梁月**：我事后又思考了您说的话……您是对的。\
**Liang Yue**: I've reconsidered it, and you're right.

**梁月**：在夜巡特遣的培训中，我的导师也无数次强调过搭档的重要性。\
没有人能永远孤军作战。\
**Liang Yue**: During my training as a vigil, our instructor emphasized many times that trusting in our partner was of vital importance.

**梁月**：您有着出色的行动力、果决的判断力、敏锐的直觉和极高的同理心，是一位可靠且值得信赖的警官。\
**Liang Yue**: And you, Ms. Poitier, have proven to be capable, decisive, and compassionate. I have developed a deep respect for your work.

**梁月**：我们都赞同要亲自将唐人街发生的怪事彻查到底，目的是一致的，因此我们当然应该通力合作……\
**Liang Yue**: We share the same goal: to discover the truth behind the incidents happening in Chinatown. I can't think of any reason why I shouldn't cooperate with you.

**波蒂埃**：行了行了行了，我明白了！\
**Poitier**: Alright, alright, alright. Enough. I'm blushing already.

波蒂埃几乎是有些狼狈地打断了梁月。\
Poitier cuts Liáng off, almost flustered.

**波蒂埃**：为什么你平常有什么事情总是闷在心里，说起这种话的时候却又……又一点也不觉得害臊？\
**Poitier**: Damn, girl! I didn't expect my meek little mouse to turn into this.

**梁月**：这种话是指……？\
**Liang Yue**: This what?

**波蒂埃**：……没什么！\
总之，我明白你的意思了。\
**Poitier**: Forget it. You've made your point. Now, stop it.

波蒂埃挥手示意这个话题到此为止。\
Poitier waves a hand, signaling the conversation's end.

**波蒂埃**：不过，基金会那边不会追究你的责任吗？例如说你“擅自把机密信息泄露给地方神秘学犯罪科”之类的。\
**Poitier**: But you kinda missed my point. I'm worrying that the Foundation is gonna punish you for leaking classified information. Won't you get in trouble?

**梁月**：我的确隶属于基金会，但在这层身份之前……我更是十二侲子之一的梁家之后。\
**Liang Yue**: Though I may be a vigil of the Foundation, before that, I am a descendant of the Liáng family. I'm obliged to do all that is necessary to fulfill my destiny.

**梁月**：规矩并不是镣铐。我想追回危险神秘学管理品、逮捕监守自盗的犯人才是眼下最优先的事项。\
**Liang Yue**: And given the circumstances, I think providing all relevant information that might assist us in catching the thief and retrieving these threatening arcane objects is worth bending the rules ... just a little.

梁月顿了顿。\
Despite her conviction, Liáng can't help but hesitate a little.

**梁月**：再说，我又没有真的接到来自上面的保密命令。\
**Liang Yue**: Besides, I'm not under any orders to keep this a secret. So ...

**波蒂埃**：……哈哈！\
你这个坏家伙，真是不能对你放松一点警戒。\
**Poitier**: Haha. Cheeky, and you say you don't like bending the rules. I see you, boo.

**波蒂埃**：好吧，就让我们一起去弄清楚这件事背后究竟藏着什么名堂吧。\
**Poitier**: And I like it. Come on. Let's work this out together, partner.

**空脑袋**：我的房间是哪个来着？对了，我写在这里了……\
啊！是这个，差点走过了。\
**Loggerhead**: Which one is my room again? Oh, right, I wrote it down. Let me see. There it is. I almost went too far again.

**空脑袋**：房卡……房卡……在这里。\
**Loggerhead**: Now, the key card. Where did I put it—oh, here.

**空脑袋**：回来了！累死我……了…………\
**Loggerhead**: Home, sweet home. Oh, I'm exhaust—

旅店房间的主人在推门入内后，僵在了原地。\
The camera-headed girl freezes in place.

原因显而易见，本应当独属于她的小窝中一目了然地多了两个不速之客的身影。\
Two officers are standing in her sweet home.

**波蒂埃**：莱瑟姆，对吧？等你半天了。\
**Poitier**: Latham, right? It's been a while.

**梁月**：我们有些话需要问你。\
**Liang Yue**: We have some questions for you. Please try to cooperate.

梁月走上前去，代替房间的主人关上了房门。\
Liáng steps forward and closes the door on her behalf.

当可怜的猎物毫无防备地踏入早已布置好的陷阱中时，结局就已经注定。\
When an unsuspecting prey steps into a carefully laid trap, the outcome is already decided.

**空脑袋**：好啦好啦！我说，我说还不行吗！\
**Loggerhead**: Alright. Fine. I'll tell you everything.

**空脑袋**：是我干的，他们说那些东西是我偷的，然后偷偷卖掉换了钱，都是我！\
大概——诶哟！\
**Loggerhead**: It was me, okay? They said I stole those arcane objects and sold them for money, well, maybe I did—Ouch!

她可怜兮兮地把自己的身体缩进了房间的角落，相较于她娇小的少女体型显得格外笨重的头部，还因此磕到了窗户的边沿。\
As she speaks, she backs closer and closer to the wall behind her, until she smacks her oversized head into the window ledge.

这番供词中的某个字眼让梁月疑惑地歪了歪头。\
A particular word in her statement makes Liáng tilt her head.

**梁月**：你说的“大概”是什么意思？\
**Liang Yue**: What do you mean "maybe"?

**空脑袋**：因为……其实我也不知道……\
**Loggerhead**: Because, actually, I can't remember it.

**空脑袋**：我也不知道我究竟有没有做那些事，因为我找不到那段时间的记忆胶片了。\
**Loggerhead**: I can't find my memory film for that time, so really, I just don't know.

**梁月**：……记忆胶片？\
**Liang Yue**: Memory film?

这名被称作“空脑袋”的意识唤醒者少女并不是什么硬骨头，约半小时后，她就已经将自己的所有底细倒了个干净。\
This so-called Loggerhead girl, an Awakened, isn't exactly a tough one. Within thirty minutes, she has spilled everything.

然而面对这个本该十分喜人的成果，两名年轻的执法者却丝毫不见欣喜之色。\
Yet, despite this seemingly ideal result, neither of the officers looks pleased.

**波蒂埃**：唉……好吧。\
让我总结一下，莱瑟姆。\
**Poitier**: *sigh* So, to summarize what you just said, Latham:

**波蒂埃**：你是一个意识唤醒者，你的本体是组成莱瑟姆环路的一枚零件。\
**Poitier**: You're an Awakened piece of a movie projector, which forms a Latham loop.

**波蒂埃**：你诞生的意义是“放映”而不是“记忆”，所以尽管你成为了一名意识唤醒者，你却有严重的健忘症。\
**Poitier**: You were designed to play movies, not record them, and that's why you suffer from severe amnesia.

**波蒂埃**：你的记忆大概只能维持三天，三天过后，你的脑袋就会变得空无一物……是这个意思吗？\
**Poitier**: You can only recall things that happened within the last three days, and after that, you'll forget almost everything, do I got that right?

**空脑袋**：是呀……哈哈。\
**Loggerhead**: I guess so.

**波蒂埃**：哈哈什么哈哈！\
**Poitier**: You guess so?

**空脑袋**：咿！\
**Loggerhead**: Eek!

突然暴起的波蒂埃显然把莱瑟姆吓了一跳——她再次缩回了那个似乎能够提供给她少许安全感的角落，把自己塞进了窗边墙壁和椅子的中间。\
Poitier's sudden questioning startles the girl. She shrinks further into the corner, wedging herself between the window and a nearby chair.

**波蒂埃**：你在开玩笑吗？怪不得那个眼镜妹叫你空脑袋，你的脑袋根本空空如也啊！\
怎么会有这种事？！\
**Poitier**: I can see why that friend of yours calls you Loggerhead. You deserve the name. What is going on here?

**梁月**：虽说意识唤醒者由于其特殊的起源，原本就可能存在各种各样的体质问题，但……我实在是没有预料到会有这样的情况。\
**Liang Yue**: It's understandable. Awakened arcanists often suffer side effects related to their origins and materials, but still, this is quite unusual, to say the least.

**梁月**：无法确保三天以前记忆的准确性……这就意味着她的证言完全不具备可信性，即使目击或是被卷入什么案件，她也可能完全不记得……\
**Liang Yue**: So, she has no memory of what happened three days ago, or even any of the cases she was involved in. So then, she's basically useless to our investigation.

**梁月**：如果这是一部悬疑推理电影，出现这种角色简直就是一场灾难。\
**Liang Yue**: I can only imagine what a disaster it would be if you showed up in a Detective C07 movie.

**空脑袋**：……也不用说得这么过分吧！我怎么就变成灾难了？\
**Loggerhead**: Hey! That's rude! How come I'm a disaster?

缩在角落的空脑袋挥舞着金属制造的拳头，鼓起勇气表达了她的不满。\
The girl, mustering what little courage she has left, waves her metal fists in defiance.

但莱瑟姆的努力没有对梁月和波蒂埃起到任何威慑作用。\
她们在不约而同地叹出一口气后，看向彼此。\
But her feeble resistance has no effect on the officers. After sighing in unison, they exchange a glance.

**波蒂埃**：……你怎么认为？\
**Poitier**: What do you think?

**梁月**：我已经发送了申请，等情报科传回莱瑟姆小姐的详细信息后，我们就可以确认了。但……我不认为这是一个谎言。\
**Liang Yue**: I've made a request for Ms. Latham's detailed records. But, I don't think she's lying.

**梁月**：一个能说出“仓鼠骑着听诊器在天花板上飞”的嫌疑人……想必还欠缺一点谎言需要的智慧。\
**Liang Yue**: Back at the hospital, the best lie she could come up with was "a hamster riding a stethoscope." I kind of doubt she's a master manipulator.

## SC-10 抽丝剥茧论 / Unraveling the Mystery

**梁月**：请让我重新整理一下吧，两位。\
**Liang Yue**: Let me sort things out.

**梁月**：空脑袋小姐，你提到你能够使用拉普拉斯科算中心开发的特制胶片，以“拍摄”的方法记录你的记忆并备份。\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Loggerhead, you said you could record and save your memories using a special type of film developed by Laplace.

**梁月**：所以虽然你本人并不记得自己是否曾经将神秘学藏品管理部的危险神秘学管理品流出到外界，但按理来说，你的记忆胶片中应当记录了一切。\
**Liang Yue**: Which means that, even if you don't recall taking anything from the Arcanum Containment Department, your film should show whether you did or not.

**梁月**：——然而，那些胶片却不见了。\
是这样吗？\
**Liang Yue**: But the fact is, the films are gone. Isn't that right?

**空脑袋**：是呀……通常我会把重要的“记忆”随身携带，将其他记忆放在自己的房间里。\
**Loggerhead**: Yeah. I usually carry my most important memories with me and leave the others in my room.

**空脑袋**：基金会发现失窃当天出入管理部的只有我后，派人前往我的房间进行了搜查。可他们却没有发现能够证明我清白的、失窃当天的胶片。\
**Loggerhead**: The Foundation staff checked the visitor log after the stuff was stolen. Turns out I was the only one who visited the office that day, so they sent people to my room and checked all my film, but they didn't find anything.

**空脑袋**：再加上说是有什么其他的证据……\
**Loggerhead**: Then they said they already had other evidence, so ...

空脑袋的声音低了下去，在场的另一个人义愤填膺地补完了她未说完的话。\
Loggerhead's voice trails off, and someone else completes her words.

**斯考特**：——所以他们就断定空脑袋是犯人。\
**Scott**: So they just declared Loggerhead guilty.

**斯考特**：但在我看来这根本不可能，一定是哪里出了错！\
**Scott**: But that doesn't make any sense to me. Something must be wrong.

这名自称为追捕莱瑟姆而来的基金会职员，在十分钟前接到了梁月的一通电话。\
The Foundation employee, who claimed to be hunting Loggerhead, received a call from Liáng just ten minutes ago.

当她进入梁月称“找到了线索”的房间，见到空脑袋时脱口而出“你怎还没走”后……空脑袋的另一部分证言也得到了印证。\
But the moment she stepped into the "clue-filled" hotel room and laid eyes on Loggerhead, she blurted out, "You're still here?" And just like that, the final piece of Loggerhead's testimony was confirmed.

**梁月**：……唉。\
**Liang Yue**: *sigh*

梁月的叹息声，让端坐在床上的两名少女默契地低下了头。\
The two girls sitting on the bed lower their heads in silent understanding.

**梁月**：所以在找到莱瑟姆小姐后，你并没有对她实施抓捕，而是为莱瑟姆小姐安排了逃亡的车票。\
**Liang Yue**: So, when you found Ms. Latham, you bought her a train ticket instead of putting her under arrest.

**斯考特**：我知道这不合规矩，但空脑袋不可能是犯人，一定是哪里搞错了。\
作为朋友，我不能就这样将她绑回基金会，坐视她被草草定罪。\
**Scott**: I know I've gone against orders, but I'm sure Loggerhead didn't do this. She's my friend. I can't just arrest her and have the Foundation lock her up.

**斯考特**：刚才我向你隐瞒了这一切……我感到非常抱歉。\
但因为你是夜巡特遣管理局的人，所以我想我必须不能露出破绽……\
**Scott**: I'm sorry for keeping all this from you, but you're a vigil. I had to be careful.

**斯考特**：如果可以的话，梁小姐，波蒂埃小姐，我希望你们能够替我与空脑袋保密。\
等我们查出犯人究竟是谁，再向上面汇报也不迟。\
**Scott**: So, if it's not crossing a line, Ms. Liáng, Ms. Poitier, can I ask you to keep this between us? You can report it after we find out who's really done this.

**空脑袋**：可以吗？求求你们了？\
**Loggerhead**: Could you? Please?

斯考特的眼神中透出恳求，而一旁的空脑袋也同样用晶莹剔透的摄像头期待地盯着梁月与波蒂埃二人。\
Scott's eyes gleam pleadingly, and Loggerhead's lens gleams as she stares at the officers in expectation.

两名少女可怜兮兮的模样让人心生怜悯，甚至让梁月产生了一种自己似乎正在虐待某种无害小动物的错觉……但这场非正式的审讯还没有结束。\
The pitiful expressions on both their faces would tug at anyone's heartstrings. Liáng almost feels as though she's tormenting some kind of harmless creature. But this unofficial interrogation isn't over yet.

**波蒂埃**：这件事等我们把事情弄清楚后再讨论也不迟。\
**Poitier**: We'll talk about that once we figure out what the hell's going on.

**波蒂埃**：刚才说到这个眼镜妹给了你去其他城市的车票，但你为什么还在这里？\
**Poitier**: Back to the case. You said she gave you a train ticket. What're you still doing here?

空脑袋尴尬地笑了笑。\
Loggerhead lets out an awkward laugh.

**空脑袋**：谁能想到呢？在我乘坐出租车去车站的路上，对面的司机好像突然发了疯，直接越过实线和我们撞在了一起。\
**Loggerhead**: Actually, while I was on my way to the train station, a car on the other side of the street lost control and hit my cab.

**空脑袋**：幸亏撞到的是我坐的副驾驶席这侧。\
我的身体结实，但那个司机可是肉体凡胎。\
**Loggerhead**: Thankfully, it crashed into the passenger seat where I was sitting. My metal's much stronger than human flesh.

一旁的梁月略作思索，挖掘出储备在记忆中的某条信息。\
Liáng searches her memory for a moment.

**梁月**：昨天上午的交通事故……我看过记录，那名肇事司机身上也出现了原因不明的精神异常，说不定他也是事件的受害人。\
**Liang Yue**: That's right. There was a car accident yesterday morning. The driver suffered some kind of unknown mental abnormality while he was on the road. Maybe he's fallen victim, too.

**梁月**：在那之后呢？\
**Liang Yue**: What happened next?

**空脑袋**：我被送到了医院，然后就遇到了你嘛。\
那个时候我还以为你就是来抓我的人，所以连忙跑了。\
**Loggerhead**: I was sent to the hospital, and you showed up. I thought you were gonna arrest me, so I ran as fast as I could.

**空脑袋**：斯考特说带着手机和便携联络装置会被定位，所以我早早就把它们丢掉了，可这下我也联系不上她，不知道该如何是好。\
**Loggerhead**: I threw away my cell phone and contact device as soon as I left the Foundation. Scott said they could use them to track me down. I couldn't get ahold of anyone and didn't know what to do.

**空脑袋**：而且……说实话，虽然没有记忆，但我总觉得自己并没有干那些坏事。\
就这样离开总觉得怪怪的。\
**Loggerhead**: And, even though I don't know for sure, I really don't think I'm guilty. It's super weird to be on the run when you feel like you're innocent.

**空脑袋**：所以我就又回到了唐人街，去找菲林士多导演帮忙了。\
毕竟她在这里拍电影，就算没有手机，我也能找到她。\
**Loggerhead**: So, I went back to Chinatown to ask Director Noire for help. She was the only one I could contact directly.

空脑袋提到的那个名字十分关键。\
A crucial name.

**梁月**：……你提到你和菲林士多相识，能讲讲当时的经过吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Noire ... Could you tell me how you got to know her?

**空脑袋**：当然啦！\
**Loggerhead**: Of course.

**空脑袋**：让我看看，星光大道……星光大道……\
有了！在这里，它在左边！\
**Loggerhead**: Let me see. Walk of Fame ... Walk of Fame ... Okay. Now I just need to turn left.

**空脑袋**：……但左边是哪里？当我转身，我的左边就会变一个方向……不是吗？\
大家都是怎么使用地图的？\
**Loggerhead**: Wait, which way is left again? It changes every time I turn, right? Gosh, how the heck do people read maps?

**菲林士多**：发生什么了？你看起来需要帮助。\
**Noire**: Are you alright? It seems you could use some help.

**空脑袋**：——是菲林士多女士帮助了迷路的我，她说她对我的脑袋很感兴趣。\
而聊了几句后，我发现她居然是一名导演！\
**Loggerhead**: Noire stopped to help me. She was really interested in my head, so we had a little chat, and I found out she was a director.

**空脑袋**：在送我去星光大道的路上，我们聊了很多关于电影的话题。在听说我是一个人来旅游、没有什么特别的安排后，她就邀请我一起来唐人街这边拍电影。\
**Loggerhead**: She offered to take me to the Walk of Fame. We talked a lot about movies on our way there. Then, I told her I was traveling alone, so she invited me to join her movie shoot in Chinatown.

**空脑袋**：这我怎么能拒绝呢？\
这可是大导演亲自指导拍摄的片场，我绝对不会错过的。\
**Loggerhead**: How could I say no? I mean, she's a famous director. There's no way I'd miss a chance like that.

**梁月**：但菲林士多女士带领你和剧组成员来到唐人街的那一天，正好是唐人街一带开始出现异常神秘学事件的时间。\
**Liang Yue**: Interesting. That was the same day that odd things started happening in Chinatown.

那颗激动得晃来晃去的脑袋迟疑地停住了。\
The head that was bobbing excitedly comes to a hesitant stop.

**空脑袋**：这……这我就不知道了。\
**Loggerhead**: Hmm. Well, I'm not sure about that.

**梁月**：那一天有发生什么奇怪的事吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Did anything strange happen that day?

摄像头闪了闪。“空脑袋”的脑袋里似乎浮现出了什么东西。\
Loggerhead's lens flickers. It seems something has surfaced in her mind.

**空脑袋**：说起来，那天晚上在来到唐人街后，我住进这个房间收拾行李，发现了一张奇怪的胶片。\
**Loggerhead**: Let me see. I did find a strange film reel when I was unpacking that night.

**梁月**：奇怪的……胶片？\
**Liang Yue**: A strange film reel?

**波蒂埃**：等等，难道说那个就是……？\
**Poitier**: Wait. Could that be ...?

胶片二字让在场的另外三人都提起了注意力。\
All three of the others immediately perk up at the mention of those words.

但不知道是否因为摄像头的视野范围不够宽，瞬间成为视线焦点的那名意识唤醒者少女并没有察觉到众人紧张的凝视。\
But perhaps due to the limited field of vision of her camera lens, Loggerhead remains oblivious to their gazes.

只见她放下自己沉甸甸的背包，一边在口中念叨着，一边悠哉游哉地翻找起来。\
Instead, she pulls her backpack toward her, muttering to herself as she leisurely rummages through it.

**空脑袋**：是呀，我会给记忆胶片们贴上标记，“每天都要看的”“要经常看看的”……经常复习，才不会忘记重要的事。\
**Loggerhead**: Yeah, a strange film reel. I've gotten into the habit of labeling my films, like "Check every day" or "Check from time to time," so that I know what to watch to keep important things in my mind.

**空脑袋**：在住进这间房间后，我也打算来一次“定期复习”，却发现我的胶片里有一张没有贴任何标记。\
**Loggerhead**: I was gonna do a review that night, but when I looked through my film, there was a roll without a label on it.

**空脑袋**：仔细一看，那盘胶片的材质也不对，它不是我的记忆胶片。\
我觉得很奇怪，就用自己放映了它。\
**Loggerhead**: It couldn't have been mine, cause it was made of a different material. I was so curious about it, you know? So I played it.

**梁月**：胶片中的内容是什么？\
**Liang Yue**: What did you see?

**空脑袋**：那好像是一部电影，但是很短，像是片花。\
**Loggerhead**: It was a movie, I guess. But it was pretty short, more like a demo or a trailer or something.

**空脑袋**：奇怪的是里面的内容根本不知所云，有很多莫名其妙的画面和声音，我猜可能是谁的恶作剧……奇怪。\
**Loggerhead**: But it was so weird. Like a jumble of pictures and sounds. It didn't make any sense to me. I dunno. Maybe it was a prank or something. Hm?

她停下了手上翻动背包的动作，茫然地抬起头来。\
She halts her search and looks up blankly.

**斯考特**：怎么了吗？\
**Scott**: What's wrong?

**空脑袋**：那盘胶片……不见了。\
**Loggerhead**: The film. It's gone.

**波蒂埃**：——你说什么？\
**Poitier**: What?

诧异令波蒂埃抬高了嗓门，空脑袋被吓了一跳，心虚地缩了缩身子。\
Loggerhead shrinks nervously once again.

**空脑袋**：反正我没有找到……之前我就是放在包里的。\
**Loggerhead**: I can't find it. It was right here, in my bag.

**波蒂埃**：给我，我来找！\
**Poitier**: Give it to me.

波蒂埃抓过空脑袋的那只鼓鼓囊囊的背包，将里面的东西一口气都倾倒在了床上。\
In one swift motion, Poitier snatches Loggerhead's backpack and upends its contents onto the bed.

**波蒂埃**：你的包怎么比我妹妹的还乱？你都不整理的吗？\
**Poitier**: Damn, first time I've seen a bag messier than my sister's. Do you ever organize your stuff?

如龙卷风般，波蒂埃在空脑袋诸如“我只是忘记扔了”“那个还有用”的尖叫声中，将她的背包连同整个房间都搜刮了一个遍。\
Like a whirlwind, Poitier tears through Loggerhead's things, ignoring her shrieks of "I just forgot to throw that away!" and "I still need that!" as she ransacks not only the backpack but the entire room.

最终，她不得不得出那个令人绝望的结论。\
Finally, she has no choice but to accept a rather disheartening conclusion.

**波蒂埃**：——没有！哪里都没有。\
**Poitier**: Nope. Nothing.

**波蒂埃**：你这个空脑袋，不会是不小心把它带出门弄丢了，或者和交给披萨外卖员的小费弄混了之类的吧？\
**Poitier**: You didn't take it out and lose it somewhere, did you? Mistake it for a tip for your pizza guy or something?

**空脑袋**：就算是我也不会把胶片和钱弄混啦！\
我这几天的记忆胶片可以证明，我没有把它弄丢，它就是这样自己消失了！\
**Loggerhead**: I forget things, but I'm not an idiot. I didn't lose it. Check my film if you wanna prove it. It just disappeared into thin air.

**梁月**：记忆胶片只能记录到你所见到的场景，也许是有人在你的摄像头所照不到的地方拿走了它。\
**Liang Yue**: But your film only records what you saw. Someone might have taken it when you weren't looking.

**梁月**：还有任何人知道这张胶片的事吗？在你播放那盘胶片后，有谁曾经造访，或是发现过什么可疑的事吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Does anyone else know about this film reel? Did you have any visitors or notice anything suspicious after you played it?

**空脑袋**：可疑的迹象？我想应该没有……至少我没有发现。\
**Loggerhead**: Suspicious? I don't think so. At least I didn't see anything.

**空脑袋**：在我播放完那盘胶片之后，除了斯考特来通知我被基金会当作犯人的消息之外，也没有什么可疑的人来过。\
**Loggerhead**: The only person who visited me afterwards was Scott. She came to tell me I was wanted by the Foundation.

**空脑袋**：哦！不过在放映的时候，菲林士多导演也和我在一起。\
因为她说对我的记忆胶片很感兴趣，所以就来了我的房间……\
**Loggerhead**: Oh. But actually, I wasn't alone when I played it. Noire was with me. She said she was interested in my memories, so she came and ...

另外三个人见了鬼一样的目光，让空脑袋怯生生地咽下了剩下的话语。\
The others stare at Loggerhead as if she's grown a second head. She nervously swallows the rest of her sentence.

**空脑袋**：……怎么了吗？\
**Loggerhead**: What's wrong?

**斯考特**：所以……是那个菲林士多导演偷偷拿走了胶片？\
**Scott**: So, it was Noire who took the film?

**演员**：你做什么——呃啊！\
**Actor**: What are you—Ugh!

一记重拳，男子被狠狠打飞。\
A solid punch sends the man flying.

——本该是这样的。\
At least, that's what was supposed to happen.

**演员**：对不起导演，我再来一次。\
**Actor**: Sorry, director. I'll try again.

**菲林士多**：你没有武术的功底，倒地的时候容易磕到头部，叫你做那个动作还是太危险了。\
**Noire**: Don't bother. Clearly, your martial arts skills are severely lacking. I don't want you to hit your head when you fall to the ground.

**菲林士多**：去休息吧。\
**Noire**: Go. Take a break.

一身狼狈的演员本还想继续争取，但所有人都知道这名看似温和的导演一旦做出决定，就不会轻易改变主意。\
The disheveled actor still wants to argue his case, but everyone knows that once this director makes a decision, she won't change her mind easily.

他张了张嘴，最终还是满脸歉意地依言走到了一旁。\
In the end, he simply sighs and steps aside.

**助理**：这就是最后一个人了，导演。\
**Assistant**: That was the last one, director.

**助理**：这里不像香港，没有那么多现成的龙虎武师可供我们选择。\
刘老师和他的弟子们再过几天就会到了，要不这场戏稍微等一下？\
**Assistant**: There are far fewer stunt performers with martial arts experience here than in Hong Kong. Master Lau and his men will arrive in a few days. Perhaps we could shoot this scene then?

**菲林士多**：凯斯那边没有档期。\
让我想想，还有什么其他的方法……\
**Noire**: Nicolas is on a tight schedule. I doubt he'll change it. Let me see what I can do.

短短一句话，自然道不尽这位香港名导远渡重洋后面临的诸多难题。\
A single sentence is far from enough to capture the many difficulties the famous Hong Kong director has faced since working overseas.

她放松身体，让后背靠在轮椅的椅背上，用微微垂下的双眸不着痕迹地扫过整个片场，寻找破局的一子。\
Leaning back in her wheelchair, she discreetly scans the set, searching for the missing piece of the puzzle.

**菲林士多**：……嗯？是她？\
**Noire**: Hm? Her again?

阿琳顺着菲林士多的目光看去。\
Lin follows Noire's gaze.

**助理**：那是……白天的那名小女警？\
**Assistant**: Oh, that young officer?

**龙套演员**：你又来做什么？听着，我不知道你们警察找菲林士多导演究竟是为了什么，但可以不要再打扰我们拍摄了吗？\
**Extra**: What do you want? Listen, I don't know what you're trying to do, but can't you just leave us alone?

**工作人员**：我们这里并不允许外人参观，如果您没有搜查令的话就请回吧。\
**Crew Member**: Sorry, ma'am, this is a closed set. If you don't have a warrant, please leave.

**空脑袋**：大家不要这么凶嘛！\
梁并不是坏人，只是偶尔看起来有些可怕而已……\
**Loggerhead**: Guys, guys, relax. Liáng isn't as mean as she seems.

显然，某位见习执夜人少女的到来并不受欢迎，连带着走在她身旁的摄像头脑袋也遭到了一些质疑。\
Clearly, the arrival of a certain vigil cadet is unwelcome. So much so, that even Loggerhead is being eyed with suspicion.

但梁月没有理会旁人。在进入片场环顾一周后，她便已经锁定了她的目标，径直向那个方向走去。\
But Liáng ignores them. She locked onto her target the moment she scanned the set and is already striding straight toward her.

梁月在目标人物的面前站定。\
She stops a few paces in front of the person in question.

**菲林士多**：没想到我们这么快就又见面了，警官小姐。\
您是还有什么其他的疑惑吗？\
**Noire**: I must say I didn't expect to see you so soon, officer. Is there something else you wanted to ask me?

**菲林士多**：我想我白天应当已经说得很清楚了，我对您目前正在调查的案件一无所知。\
**Noire**: I think I made myself perfectly clear this morning. I know nothing about your case.

**梁月**：您误会了，菲林士多导演。这次我是来帮忙的。\
**Liang Yue**: No, madam. I'm here to help.

**菲林士多**：……帮忙？\
**Noire**: Help with what?

**梁月**：我听莱瑟姆小姐说，您正在为缺少身手出众的龙套演员而发愁。\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Latham mentioned that you're looking for a qualified stunt performer for your movie.

**梁月**：如果您不介意，我想也许我能够帮上您的忙。\
**Liang Yue**: I'd like to help with that, if you don't mind, as an apology.

菲林士多错愕地眨了眨眼睛。\
Noire blinks.

**菲林士多**：……这我倒是没有想到。\
**Noire**: Hmm. You surprise me again.

## SC-11 喂，跑龙套！ / Hey, Kelefe!

**菲林士多**：做我的演员？你吗？\
**Noire**: You mean to say that you're a stuntwoman? Seriously?

菲林士多摇头笑了笑，随即便像是并无太多兴趣般调转了轮椅的朝向。\
Noire chuckles and shakes her head before turning her wheelchair in disinterest.

**菲林士多**：多谢您的好意，警官小姐——不，看您的制服，我想也许我该称呼您为执夜人小姐？\
**Noire**: Thank you, officer. Well, judging by your uniform, you're from the Vigiles Bureau, aren't you?

**菲林士多**：您的提案令我受宠若惊，若是能有夜巡特遣管理局的人参与这部电影的拍摄，想必我们也能够吸引到更多的观众进入影院。\
**Noire**: I appreciate the gesture. It's true that we may be able to attract more viewers if we have a vigil on the cast list.

**菲林士多**：但也许您对拍摄电影有些误解，它并不是一件容易的事，您的好意我心领了。\
**Noire**: But filmmaking isn't as easy as you think. Maybe I can fit you in next time.

这意味着拒绝。但显然作战中并不包含“被拒绝”这一环。\
Rejection. But refusal is not an option in this operation.

**梁月**：我对电影略知一二，也十分喜欢和熟悉您的作品。\
**Liang Yue**: I'm familiar with movies, especially yours. I'm actually a big fan.

**梁月**：我看了刚才您手下其他人的表现，无意冒犯，但——对于那些武戏的部分，也许我可以试一试。\
**Liang Yue**: And I saw the performance just now. Not to be rude or anything, but I think I can handle the stunt.

**梁月**：“做更好的电影”——莱瑟姆小姐告诉我，这就是您所追求的东西，不是吗？\
**Liang Yue**: "For the betterment of the movie." That's what Ms. Latham said you were after. Is that right?

这番话再次掀起一番惊涛骇浪。\
Her words stir up a storm.

**演员**：什么？她在说些什么？\
**Actor**: What? Does she even know what she's talking about?

**工作人员**：口气倒是不小……\
**Crew Member**: Hmph. That's some pretty big talk.

菲林士多似乎也因梁月的这番话哑然失笑，但至少——那架原本逐渐驶离的轮椅，此刻停了下来。\
Even Noire can't help but let out an amused chuckle at Liáng's words. Even so, her wheelchair comes to a stop.

**菲林士多**：这话倒是没错，但……你就这么确定，你就是能够让我的电影变得“更好”的那剂调味料？\
**Noire**: That's true, but are you certain that you'll make my movie better?

**梁月**：是的。\
**Liang Yue**: Yes.

说实话，不。\
To be honest, no.

梁月知道电影的拍摄绝不像是看上去的那样简单，这绝非她的真心话。\
Liáng knows that filmmaking is far more complex than it appears. Her answer is far from the truth.

但为了查清真相……她必须成为一个好演员，正如此刻这般。\
But if she's going to uncover the truth, she has to act the part.

**菲林士多**：……有趣。\
**Noire**: Hmm. Interesting.

**菲林士多**：既然你都说到这个份上了，那么就让我们试试吧，执夜人小姐。\
**Noire**: Since you insist, let's give it a try. Show me what a vigil can do.

这并不是一个多么高明的计谋，值得庆幸的是莱瑟姆所言不虚。\
It isn't a particularly clever trick, but fortunately, Latham's words weren't false.

菲林士多永远不会拒绝让她的电影变得“更好”的任何一个可能性。\
Noire would never turn down an opportunity to improve her films.

**菲林士多**：——很好，很好！\
**Noire**: Excellent! Bravo!

**菲林士多**：你真的做到了你所声称的事，这一条的确更好——堪称完美！\
**Noire**: Exactly as you claimed, no, even better. Really spectacular work, a perfect take.

**梁月**：……您过奖了，菲林士多导演……\
**Liang Yue**: I'm flattered, director.

菲林士多看着摄像机中的回放赞不绝口。\
而NG了将近二十次，一旁梁月的临时戏服已经被汗水浸湿。\
Noire's eyes glisten as she watches the playback of the shot. Meanwhile, after nearly twenty failed takes, Liáng returns to the dressing room, her costume drenched in sweat.

她从片场临时搭建的更衣间走出，换回了平日所穿的执夜人制服。\
正感到口干舌燥之时，一瓶矿泉水被贴心地递到了她的面前。\
When she emerges back in her Vigiles uniform, a bottle of water is handed to her.

**演员Ⅰ**：喝这个吧，没打开过的。\
**Actor I**: Here. It's not open.

**梁月**：……谢谢。\
**Liang Yue**: Thank you.

**演员Ⅰ**：没想到你表现得还挺不错的。那个动作那么危险，真亏你敢做，看着我都害怕。\
**Actor I**: Didn't expect you to pull it off. That was a dangerous stunt. Scared the crap outta me.

**演员Ⅰ**：不过我得提醒你，如果你觉得每次都只是不要命，就能获得菲林士多导演的认可，那就大错特错了！\
**Actor I**: Alright, alright, so you did a good job one time. But let me tell you, it takes a lot more than that to win recognition in this industry.

**演员Ⅱ**：文戏才是考验一个演员的最重要的指标。你的外形不错，看你刚才拍戏也很认真，是不是真的对这一行有兴趣？\
**Actor II**: You've really gotta hone in on the dramatic scenes if you wanna move out of the stuntwoman box. You're good-looking, and you took that scene pretty seriously. You interested in doing that?

**演员Ⅱ**：如果是的话，年轻人，我劝你最好更虚心一些，这样才能有机会真的让更多人看到。\
