**Actor II**: If you are, then I'll suggest you be a little more humble. There's always room for improvement, you know.

**梁月**：我……您说得对，我很抱歉。\
**Liang Yue**: I ... You're right. I'm sorry.

**梁月**：不过我的本职并不是演员，未来也没有在这一行发展的打算，电影只是……我的爱好。\
**Liang Yue**: But I'm not even a stuntwoman, let alone an actress. This is all just a bit of fun for me.

**菲林士多**：哦？那可就太可惜了。\
**Noire**: Is that so? Oh, what a shame.

片场的女王乘着她的座驾来到了梁月的身边。\
The queen of the set rolls over in her chariot, stopping beside Liáng.

**菲林士多**：你的歉意我感受到了，它非常诚恳，我很满意。\
但如果你愿意提供更多，我会更高兴的。\
**Noire**: I appreciate your sincerity, but I'd be even more appreciative if you were willing to do a few more scenes.

**梁月**：如果只是短时间的话……我愿意尽我所能提供帮助。\
**Liang Yue**: If it's just for a short time, I'd like to help in any way I can.

**菲林士多**：这是我今天听过的最好的消息了！\
跟我来，差不多到晚饭时间了，正好带你看看剧本——顺便改改剧本。\
**Noire**: Fantastic! Follow me. We can have dinner and look at the script together. I have a few changes I want to make to the story.

**菲林士多**：相信我，我们的观众一定会期待听到至少一句你的台词的。\
**Noire**: Trust me, the audience will be more than happy to hear a line or two from you.

**梁月**：台词……是吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Lines? Okay.

——但事情的发展似乎开始超出预计的范围了。\
Things seem to be taking an unexpected turn.

**菲林士多**：——就这些吧，怎么样，记住了吗？\
**Noire**: That's all. Well? Have you memorized them?

**梁月**：是的，我都背下来了。但……\
**Liang Yue**: Yes, every word. But ...

**梁月**：这不止一句台词吧？\
**Liang Yue**: Aren't there too many?

桌上摊开的剧本中已经多了几道写写画画的痕迹，潇洒飘逸的字迹在空白处笔走龙蛇。\
The blank spaces in the script spread out on the table are filled with Noire's flamboyant pen strokes.

**助理**：投资人要是知道了，可不一定会同意。\
他们之前不就说过，咱们在香港那一套不能照搬，不可以边拍边改剧本吗？\
**Assistant**: She's got a point, director. The investors might not approve them. They already told us not to change the script like we did in Hong Kong.

**菲林士多**：放心吧，我都改了多少了。\
他都不看剧本，不会知道的。\
**Noire**: Relax. We've done this before. They never read the script anyway.

**菲林士多**：而且这样角色塑造才完整。一句话虽然也可以，但这样的效果更好。\
也不多，只有三句而已嘛！\
**Noire**: Besides, I'm not exactly asking for a monologue here. It's only three lines. Just what's needed to make the character complete.

助理阿琳无奈地摇了摇头，像是知道劝不动菲林士多，不再言语。\
Lin gives a helpless sigh. She knows all too well how pointless it is to try and change Noire's mind.

**梁月**：我会在开拍之前将它们练习好的。\
**Liang Yue**: I'll keep practicing until filming starts.

**菲林士多**：我期待着你的表现。\
**Noire**: I look forward to your performance.

**梁月**：说起来我刚才在片场见到了一些神偶和神轿，我记得应当马上就到度朔节了，剧组的人也要参加社火游行吗？\
**Liang Yue**: By the way, I saw some deity dolls and sedan chairs on the set. The Dùshuò Festival is coming up, right? Is the crew joining the Shèhuǒ Parade?

**菲林士多**：那些是拍戏用的。\
**Noire**: Those are our props.

**菲林士多**：这次电影里的结局，会是一场在社火游行中的戏。\
我和这边的组织者们打了招呼，直接让剧组参与进去，借景拍摄。\
**Noire**: Our final scene is set at the Shèhuǒ Parade. I already spoke with the organizers in Chinatown. They've allowed us to shoot during it.

**梁月**：在社火游行里的戏？我记得C07的最后一部的结局，也是在社火游行中。\
**Liang Yue**: Really? The last C07 movie ended with a Shèhuǒ Parade, too.

菲林士多的双眼一亮，向她露出一个笑容。\
Noire's eyes light up. She smiles.

**菲林士多**：记忆力不错嘛，看来你说你熟悉我的片子并不是在吹牛。\
**Noire**: Good memory. Looks like you meant it when you said you were a big fan.

老板娘端上了她们的餐食，剧本会议暂时告一段落。\
The restaurant owner serves their meal, pausing their script discussion for the time being.

菲林士多和助理小姐都拿起了筷子，但这张四人餐桌上原本最贪吃的那个人却并没有立刻对桌上的美食做出什么反应。\
Noire and her assistant pick up their chopsticks, but Loggerhead remains still.

**空脑袋**：所以……你发现什么了吗？\
**Loggerhead**: So, did you find anything?

**空脑袋**：你说你的“险道兽强梁”有很大概率能够识别出有邪恶气息的物品是否在附近。\
在菲林士多导演的身上你有什么发现吗？\
**Loggerhead**: You said that your beastie friend could detect things tainted with evil, right? So did it sense anything wrong with the director?

虽然空脑袋将自己的扬声器调低了音量……但说实话，她那颗颇引人注目的脑袋很难完成“凑到别人的耳边说悄悄话”这种行为。\
While Loggerhead speaks in a hushed tone, the conspicuousness of her head makes talking in secret a near impossible task.

感受着菲林士多和助理王琳有意无意瞟过来的目光，梁月如坐针毡。\
Feeling Noire and Lin's subtle glances, Liáng squirms in her seat.

**梁月**：……没有。但这并不代表——\
**Liang Yue**: No, but that doesn't mean—

**空脑袋**：太好了！\
我就说吧，菲林士多导演是不会那么做的！\
**Loggerhead**: Yes! I told you she'd never do that.

**梁月**：喂……别那么大声啊！\
**Liang Yue**: Hey! She can hear you, you know.

现在亡羊补牢显然已经晚了。\
The situation is already beyond repair.

**菲林士多**：我不会怎么做？\
**Noire**: I'd never do what?

**梁月**：………………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

有那么一瞬间，梁月产生了一种头疼欲裂的感觉……她忍不住略带责怪地看了身旁的空脑袋一眼，对方明显瑟缩了一下。\
For a brief moment, Liáng feels a splitting headache. She shoots a mildly accusatory glance at Loggerhead, causing her to visibly shrink.

**空脑袋**：抱歉……但，我就是不喜欢遮遮掩掩的嘛。\
**Loggerhead**: Sorry, I don't like skirting around things.

**空脑袋**：有什么事我们不能当面问清楚吗？\
**Loggerhead**: Can't we just ask her straight up?

**梁月**：如果每个犯人都会把自己干的所有坏事全部老实交代，这个世界上就不需要我们这个职业了。\
**Liang Yue**: Not really. If every criminal just confessed to their crimes, the Vigiles wouldn't exist.

但事已至此，梁月不认为蹩脚的掩饰能够将坐在对面的女子糊弄过去，打开天窗说亮话似乎是仅剩的选择了。\
No clumsy cover-up will fool the director now. There is nothing for it but to be upfront.

而这也许并不是最坏的选择。\
Perhaps this is for the best anyway.

**梁月**：……除了向您表示歉意之外，实际上我这一次来找您还有一些其他的目的。\
**Liang Yue**: Actually, I didn't just come here to apologize. There's something I want to ask you about.

**菲林士多**：是什么呢？\
**Noire**: What is it?

恰到好处的疑惑与好奇，却并无意外之色。\
A perfectly measured balance of curiosity and confusion, yet no real surprise.

一位著名的导演在演技方面颇有造诣，也并不是什么令人意外的事情。\
外行人的班门弄斧无法取得预期的成效，也应当在预料之中。\
A renowned director having a knack for acting isn't exactly shocking. In fact, it's about as surprising as an amateur failing miserably to do the same thing.

**梁月**：是关于最近唐人街发生的那些怪事。\
**Liang Yue**: It's about the strange things happening in Chinatown these days.

**助理**：等等……警官小姐。\
难道你刻意接近菲林士多导演，实际上还是为了之前那件事?\
**Assistant**: Wait, so all this was just to butter us up so you could investigate your case?

方才还对她们有说有笑的助理小姐收起了嘴边的笑意。\
尽管早有心理准备，但这并不会让梁月更加好受。\
The assistant, who was all smiles moments ago, suddenly falls silent. Despite her careful preparation, the situation is difficult for Liáng.

**梁月**：请原谅。这是我的工作。\
**Liang Yue**: Sorry, madam, but it's my job.

**梁月**：正如我此前所说，唐人街一带发生了许多怪事，而这与数年前在菲林士多导演身边发生过的“映像事件”极其相似。\
**Liang Yue**: As I said, strange things have been happening in Chinatown—things that bear a striking resemblance to the "film incident" that you were involved in eight years ago, Ms. Noire.

**梁月**：当年的调查显示，引发事件的罪魁祸首是菲林士多导演的好友——编剧何日君生前拍摄的一部暂定名为《三燕归巢》的电影片花。\
**Liang Yue**: The case document stated that the origin of these events is a film reel titled Reunion of the Three Swallows—a movie created by your friend, Hé Rìjūn.

**梁月**：——而在数日前，您应该和莱瑟姆小姐一起在她的房间观看过一部影片。\
您对当时放映的那部胶片的去向有什么头绪吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Latham said you watched a film with her in her room a few days ago. Do you have any idea where that film reel is now?

**菲林士多**：……你是说当时的那盘胶片？\
**Noire**: That film reel?

**梁月**：您不知道？\
**Liang Yue**: Did you not know what it was?

**菲林士多**：我不知道。\
**Noire**: I had no idea.

菲林士多的表情沉了下来。\
显然她已经意识到了梁月提起“那盘胶片”的原因。\
Noire's expression darkens. Clearly, she's realized why Liáng has brought up that film reel.

**菲林士多**：那天晚上我们观看的影片……就算用最委婉的说法，也绝称不上是一部有趣的片花，甚至连“故事”都称不上。\
**Noire**: That film we watched together ... Well, to put it mildly, it had nothing of interest. It didn't seem to have any semblance of a story, even.

**菲林士多**：那就是泰瑞莎拍摄的东西？绝不可能。\
**Noire**: It couldn't have been one of Teresa's.

从记忆中的某个角落，梁月记起《三燕归巢》的档案中曾提到“泰瑞莎”正是其创作者何日君的英文名。\
Liáng recalls that the archive on Reunion of the Three Swallows cited "Teresa" as the English name of its creator, Hé Rìjūn.

菲林士多与何日君是留学时结识的好友，而听起来菲林士多至今仍在用当时的名字称呼对方。\
Noire and Hé Rìjūn had been friends since their days studying abroad, and it seems Noire still uses that name even now.

那些真真假假的传闻与调查报告中未经证实的猜测闪过梁月的脑海……但面前女子愁眉不展的模样，让梁月决定暂时将它们丢到脑后。\
Rumors, investigation reports, and speculations flicker through Liáng's mind. But seeing the somber look on the woman before her, she decides to set them aside for now.

**梁月**：……也许是它原本的内容遭到了污染。基金会的档案中记载，神秘学管理品《三燕归巢》拥有“放映”与“重摄”两种能力。\
**Liang Yue**: Maybe the original content has been contaminated. According to the Foundation's records, the film reel has two abilities: play and record.

**梁月**：“放映”能力让它能够将胶片中的内容，用类似电影映像般的形式在现实世界中再现，我猜测这正是受害者们提到的“幻觉”“鬼影”的真身。\
**Liang Yue**: The play ability allows it to conjure its contents into reality in a form similar to a movie image, which accounts for the hallucinations and phantoms the victims mentioned.

**梁月**：在“放映”生效的范围内，受害者会被“重摄”现象捕获，损失一部分神智和记忆。\
**Liang Yue**: The record ability captures the souls of those in the same effective range as play, and the victims lose a part of themselves, like their sanity or their memories.

**梁月**：档案中虽然没有明确记载，但我猜测正是那部分被“重摄”进入胶片的精神能量，干扰了胶片中的原有内容。\
**Liang Yue**: The case document doesn't mention anything about contamination, but my guess is that the souls recorded by the film have polluted the original content of the film.

**菲林士多**：不管到底是谁或是什么东西导致了这一切——真是没品味。\
**Noire**: Shame on them—whoever's behind this.

低声咒骂了一句后，菲林士多和梁月默契地陷入了沉默，但显然一旁的空脑袋和助理小姐却是满头雾水。\
Noire mutters a curse, and both she and Liáng fall into silence. Meanwhile, Lin and Loggerhead look utterly lost.

**空脑袋**：等一下，等一下……你们在聊什么？知道什么？\
你们不要打哑谜呀！\
**Loggerhead**: Wait, wait. What are you talking about? Can you explain it to me simply, please?

**梁月**：菲林士多导演并不知道那盘胶片很可能就是《三燕归巢》……\
她也并没有将它拿走。\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Noire didn't know that that film was Reunion of the Three Swallows, so naturally, she didn't take it.

**梁月**：我想……她说的是真的。\
**Liang Yue**: I think she's telling the truth.

**空脑袋**：真的？那这真是个好消息！\
**Loggerhead**: Really? That's great news.

没有人附和她。空脑袋迟疑地放下了为庆贺而高举的手臂，后知后觉。\
No one responds. Loggerhead looks around and slowly lowers the arm she raised in premature celebration.

**空脑袋**：哦，对了，胶片还下落不明，所以这称不上是好消息……\
**Loggerhead**: Oh, right. The film's still missing, so it's not great news.

**空脑袋**：但至少菲林士多导演接近我并不是别有目的之类的，对吧？\
对我来说，这就是好消息了。\
**Loggerhead**: But, at least, Noire wasn't up to something when she made friends with me, right? That's definitely good news for me.

她看向菲林士多。\
She turns to Noire.

**空脑袋**：这意味着我们还是朋友！是朋友就可以互帮互助。\
我听梁说，那盘胶片可能会对你造成威胁，那么也许我们可以一起去寻找它。\
**Loggerhead**: That means we're still friends. And friends help each other. Liáng said that the film reel could cause some problems for you. Let me help you find it.

**空脑袋**：等找到后，我们就将它送回神秘学藏品管理部去，顺便再抓住那个偷偷将胶片从神秘学藏品管理部偷出来的坏蛋。\
**Loggerhead**: I'll catch that thief and take the film back to the ACD.

**空脑袋**：这样你也可以放心，我也可以洗清嫌疑，唐人街的麻烦也解决了……一举三得！怎么样，是不是个好主意？\
**Loggerhead**: Then you'll be safe, I'll clear my name, and the problems in Chinatown will be solved. That's three birds with one stone. Genius, right?

**菲林士多**：……你知道吗，莱瑟姆小姐？\
这就是我最喜欢你的一点。\
**Noire**: You know, Ms. Latham, this is what I like about you. You always speak your mind.

菲林士多眯起眼睛笑了笑，没有给予空脑袋肯定的答复，但嘴角的弧度却十分柔和。\
Her eyes squint a little as she curves her mouth into an unexpectedly gentle smile.

**菲林士多**：人与人之间的事总是很复杂，这让它们足够有趣，总能够为我提供源源不断的素材和灵感，令我着迷。\
**Noire**: Our relationships are so complex, aren't they? That's what makes them so intriguing, captivating, really. A constant source of inspiration.

**菲林士多**：但有的时候……我也会想，也许简单些更好。\
你觉得呢，执夜人小姐？\
**Noire**: But sometimes I feel that life is better kept simple. Wouldn't you agree, Ms. Vigil?

**梁月**：……我也有同感。\
**Liang Yue**: Agreed.

“我怀疑你”和“我并不打算与你们合作”的确都各自拥有更加简单的表达方式。\
There are certainly simpler ways to say "I'm suspicious of you" and "I have no intention of cooperating."

**梁月**：……我还能再问您一个问题吗？\
**Liang Yue**: May I ask you another question?

**菲林士多**：请。\
**Noire**: Please.

**梁月**：关于C07的那些传闻……它们哪些是真的，哪些是假的？\
**Liang Yue**: The rumors about C07, which ones are true?

**菲林士多**：我并不认为这些陈年旧事，是破获你手头的案件所必须的。\
**Noire**: I don't think a few old stories will help you solve the case.

**梁月**：……不仅仅是为了调查案件，也因为我想要知道。\
**Liang Yue**: It's not only for the case, but for my own curiosity.

**梁月**：我之前说我很熟悉您的作品……也很喜欢它们，那并不是在说谎。\
**Liang Yue**: I wasn't lying when I said I was familiar with your works. I really like them.

**梁月**：作为一个曾经的观众，这些事情的真伪对我而言很重要。\
**Liang Yue**: And this question matters a lot to me as a fan.

**菲林士多**：……原来是这样。\
**Noire**: Oh. I see.

菲林士多迟疑了片刻。\
Noire ponders for a moment.

**菲林士多**：那么我想你还是不知道为好。\
**Noire**: In that case, I really don't think you should know the truth, for your own good.

**菲林士多**：我很感谢你对我们的电影的喜爱，但……也许过于接近银幕后的人并不是一个好主意。\
**Noire**: I appreciate your love for my works, but it's not a good idea to dig too deep into what went on behind the scenes.

**菲林士多**：只享受故事，才不至于消磨了乐趣。\
**Noire**: Just enjoy the stories for what they are. Otherwise, the magic will be ruined.

她轻微摇了摇头，垂下的眼眸中却闪过几分思索。\
She gives a slight shake of her head, but a flicker of contemplation passes through her downcast eyes.

**菲林士多**：不过作为补偿，也许我可以提供另一条你应当会感兴趣的消息。\
**Noire**: Well, I can tell you one thing that might interest you, though.

## SC-12 捕鼠器 / Mousetrap

夜色渐浓，唐人街外转角处的餐厅中，顾客已寥寥无几。\
但此时店门拴着的铃声响起，又有二人推门而入。\
Night has deepened, and the little restaurant on the corner outside of Chinatown is almost empty. The doorbell chimes, and two people walk in.

**空脑袋**：斯考特！还有……高个子警官，这边！\
**Loggerhead**: Scott, and Tall Officer, over here.

**波蒂埃**：是波蒂埃。\
只过去了三个小时，你就已经忘记了吗？\
**Poitier**: Again, it's Poitier. Have you seriously already forgotten my name? It's only been three hours.

在空脑袋的招呼下，新进门的那两人来到梁月与空脑袋的这一席上落座。\
At Loggerhead's call, the two newcomers take a seat at her and Liáng's table.

**梁月**：怎么样？\
**Liang Yue**: What's your status?

**斯考特**：抱歉……我这边没有什么收获。\
**Scott**: Couldn't find anything useful. Sorry.

**斯考特**：为了不暴露空脑袋的事，我打发一起跟来的职员去追查其他神秘学管理品的线索了，但除了那件“发条玩具”之外，另外几件至今都下落不明。\
**Scott**: I already asked the investigators who came with me to track down the other missing items, you know, to cover up for Loggerhead, but so far, they haven't found anything.

**斯考特**：至于真正将这些神秘学管理品从神秘学藏品管理部流出的犯人……更是毫无头绪。\
**Scott**: As for the person who stole the item, I haven't a clue.

**空脑袋**：是吗……\
**Loggerhead**: Well ...

**空脑袋**：不过也许没有消息就是最好的消息，至少其他那些丢失的神秘学管理品还没有把哪座城市炸出一个大洞来之类的。\
**Loggerhead**: At least there haven't been any reports of arcane explosions or earthquakes. No news is good news, right?

**波蒂埃**：你们怎么样？\
**Poitier**: What about you? Any leads?

**梁月**：菲林士多并没有拿走胶片。但她拒绝向我们透露更多有关那张“被诅咒的胶片”《三燕归巢》和它的创作者何日君的事。\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Noire didn't take the film, but she refused to tell us anything about its curse or the former owner, Hé Rìjūn.

她故作低落地叹了一口气，并未说出菲林士多最后附赠的那条消息。\
She lets out a deliberately dejected sigh, withholding the final message Noire gave her.

**波蒂埃**：那看起来只有我这边有好消息了。\
**Poitier**: Looks like I'm the only one who has good news.

**梁月**：真的？……哪一边？\
**Liang Yue**: You do? What about?

波蒂埃扬了扬下巴，越过桌对面的斯考特，指向窗外漆黑的街道。\
Poitier tilts her head, gesturing past Scott to the darkened street outside the window.

**波蒂埃**：你让我关注的神秘学物品非法交易这条线。\
**Poitier**: The illegal trade of arcane items. You told me to keep an eye on it.

**波蒂埃**：我联系了科里负责这方面的家伙，他告诉我说一个绰号叫“癞皮狗”的黑市中间人行迹古怪。\
**Poitier**: I contacted my guy who tracks all that stuff. Told me about this trader called Pug Dog, a middleman in the black market.

**波蒂埃**：早上那家伙因为超速被拦下来了，但他居然老老实实地交了罚单——放在平时，那可是会当街开枪的主。\
**Poitier**: He was pulled over for speeding this morning, but he actually paid the ticket right away. Can you believe that? I wouldn't be surprised if he shot the police car and ran away there.

**梁月**：一个无法无天的犯罪分子忽然表现得很老实？\
**Liang Yue**: An outlaw suddenly behaving himself ...

**梁月**：这代表……他很可能有些更重要的“预定”，所以不能让那些“小麻烦”阻碍了计划。\
**Liang Yue**: He must be up to something important. Something big enough to make him avoid getting into trouble over a speeding ticket.

**波蒂埃**：我们的人也这么想，于是就标记了那个家伙，结果发现就在刚才，他开了一辆报告为失窃车辆的雪佛兰到了这里——唐人街。\
**Poitier**: The officers thought the same, so they tracked him to this stolen car, right? Well, guess where it's headed—here, Chinatown.

**癞皮狗**：……\
**Pug Dog**: ...

眉间一道狰狞疤痕的男人踏过皎洁的月光，最终在钻入一条漆黑的小巷后停下了脚步。\
A man with a deep, jagged scar across his brow saunters under the moonlight.

——他并没有发现缀在自己身后、藏身在见习执夜人施展的“静谧无声”神秘术下的四条小尾巴。\
At last, he stops, slipping into a darkened alleyway. He has no idea that four silent pursuers are lurking nearby, hidden under a rookie vigil's Silent Shadow arcane skill.

**空脑袋**：他要做什么？\
**Loggerhead**: What's he doing?

**波蒂埃**：看起来是在等待什么人。\
**Poitier**: Waiting for someone's my guess.

**斯考特**：一个从事非法神秘学物品交易的黑市中间人……意思是那张“被诅咒的胶片”很可能在他的手上，而他正要和什么人做交易？\
**Scott**: A middleman for the arcane black market. So, he probably has the cursed film, and now he's planning to sell it to someone.

**斯考特**：我们应该立即抓住他，防止东西再次丢失！这是唯一的机会了——\
**Scott**: We should get him now, before the film's sold off. Come on, this is our chance.

**斯考特**：唔……唔？！\
**Scott**: Hm? Mmm.

好在敏锐的少女及时堵住了她的嘴巴，让声音再透不出半点儿。\
Liáng clamps a hand over her mouth just in time, muffling her outburst.

**梁月**：嘘！别动，有什么人来了。\
**Liang Yue**: Shh. Someone's coming.

从更加浓重的黑暗之中逐渐浮现出一个身影。\
From the depths of the shadows, a figure emerges.

她并非向癞皮狗走去，而是乘着什么东西，例如——轮椅。\
Not walking toward Pug Dog, but riding something. Perhaps—a wheelchair.

**菲林士多**：晚上好，尊敬的先生。\
我希望您没有等待太久。\
**Noire**: Good evening, sir. I hope I didn't keep you too long.

**癞皮狗**：钱带来了吗？\
**Pug Dog**: You got the dough?

**菲林士多**：当然。\
**Noire**: Of course.

菲林士多从怀里掏出一件长方形的物品。\
Noire pulls a rectangular object from her coat.

**波蒂埃**：是个信封……看着可不薄。\
**Poitier**: It's an envelope. Looks pretty thick.

波蒂埃所言无误，因为癞皮狗接过信封后数清了钱，满意地点了点头。\
Poitier is right. Pug Dog takes the envelope and pulls a handful of bills from it before nodding in satisfaction.

**癞皮狗**：数量没错。\
不用担心，我癞皮狗的信誉放眼全城都是有口皆碑的。\
**Pug Dog**: All here. Dontcha worry, alright? You can trust me. Everyone in L.A. knows Pug Dog.

癞皮狗将那一个鼓鼓囊囊的信封放进口袋，转而从夹克的内袋中取出了另一个物件。\
He stuffs the bulging envelope into his pocket before pulling an item from his jacket.

**癞皮狗**：你的东西在这里。\
**Pug Dog**: Here's your stuff.

那东西在黑暗中划过一道并不明晰的弧线，被菲林士多准确无误地接住。\
The item cuts an arc through the darkness, landing precisely in Noire's waiting hands.

**癞皮狗**：行了，交易已经完成，那我就撤了。\
您出手阔绰，人也爽快，是那种我还会愿意再合作的客户。\
**Pug Dog**: Heh. I like customers like you, generous and to the point. Alright, I'm outta here. Pleasure doin' business with ya. And hey, feel free to call me again.

他四下望了望，随后再次望向菲林士多，压低了声音。\
He scans the area before turning back to Noire, lowering his voice.

**癞皮狗**：看在这个份上……我给您个忠告，回去的时候您最好注意些。\
**Pug Dog**: Seein' as you're a good customer o' mine, here's a bit of advice: Watch your back on the way outta here.

**菲林士多**：您这是什么意思——\
**Noire**: What do you mean?

癞皮狗话语中暗含的警示之意让菲林士多不由得追问，但她的话并没能说完。\
But Noire doesn't get the chance to press further.

时机已到，从暗处大步走出的梁月打断了这场见不得光的谈话。\
The moment has come. Liáng strides out from the shadows.

**梁月**：请原谅我冒昧打断你们的谈话，但——我想不论是菲林士多导演还是这位先生，都暂时不需要考虑“回去”的问题了。\
**Liang Yue**: Sorry to interrupt, but neither one of you will be making your own way home. Ms. Noire, Pug Dog.

**梁月**：因为我恐怕二位需要跟我们一起去神秘学犯罪科走一趟。\
**Liang Yue**: I'm afraid you'll be coming to the Arcane Affairs office with me.

**癞皮狗**：该死，是条子！\
**Pug Dog**: F**kin' cop!

**癞皮狗**：疼疼疼！轻一点！\
**Pug Dog**: Ow! Easy, easy.

**波蒂埃**：别废话，老实点！\
**Poitier**: Shut up and stay down!

尽管癞皮狗意欲反抗，但不消片刻便被按在了地上。\
Pug Dog's attempts to fight back have been utterly useless.

**梁月**：……菲林士多导演，我能请您让我看看他交给您的那件东西吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Ms. Noire, could you show me what he gave you?

**菲林士多**：请。\
**Noire**: Go ahead.

那只灰扑扑的小盒子被递到了梁月的面前。\
She hands a dusty gray box to Liáng.

盒子中装的是一盘看似平平无奇的胶片，但梁月却意识到怀中寄宿着险道兽强梁的祭器在隐隐发烫。\
Inside is an ordinary-looking film reel. But Liáng can feel the vessel containing Qiángliáng growing warm against her skin.

**梁月**：……我想就是它。尺寸也没有错，超8毫米。\
这就是编剧何日君的遗作，“被诅咒的胶片”《三燕归巢》。\
**Liang Yue**: Super 8 mm. This must be it. Reunion of the Three Swallows. Hé Rìjūn's final work.

**梁月**：也是唐人街一系列怪事的罪魁祸首。\
**Liang Yue**: The culprit behind the strange happenings in Chinatown.

但此时它却只是安静地躺在梁月的手中，乖顺而无害。\
Yet for now, it lies quietly in her grasp, docile and unthreatening.

**波蒂埃**：很好，虽然多了许多波折，但事情的进展比我想象中的要顺利很多嘛！\
我们只花了一天，就找到了罪魁祸首。\
**Poitier**: Well, that was easier than expected. Half a day, and we've already tracked it down.

**波蒂埃**：接下来就只剩下让这盘胶片收起它的神通了。\
要怎么做？例如……把它掰了？\
**Poitier**: Now all we gotta do is stop it from doing its arcanum-y thing. But how? Smash it?

在梁月回复之前，有人率先对这个提案表示了委婉的反对。\
Before Liáng can respond, Noire voices a polite opposition.

**菲林士多**：我并不认为这是最好的办法。\
**Noire**: I don't think that's a good idea.

**梁月**：关于这一点，必须承认菲林士多导演说的是对的。\
**Liang Yue**: I have to admit, Ms. Noire's right.

**梁月**：面对危险神秘学管理品，应当更加谨慎地处理，目前谁也不知道如果破坏它，是会让事情好转……还是恶化。\
**Liang Yue**: Arcane items need to be handled with the utmost care. No one knows what will happen once it's broken. We could make things worse.

**波蒂埃**：好吧……看来我们只能带着这张胶片回去从长计议了。\
**Poitier**: Fine. Let's take these two back to the office first.

**波蒂埃**：站起来吧老兄！我们该走了。\
**Poitier**: On your feet, tough guy! We gotta go.

**癞皮狗**：呃……该死，事情是怎么暴露的？难道是哪个混球告了密？\
**Pug Dog**: Ugh. Damn it. How'd ya find me? Some asshole sell me out?

癞皮狗从地上被波蒂埃一把拽了起来，他一边骂骂咧咧，一边不情愿地向外走去。\
Pug Dog is yanked up from the ground. He reluctantly follows Poitier, grumbling and cursing under his breath.

——但在走过梁月的时候，他忽然停住了脚步。\
But as he passes Liáng, he stops.

**癞皮狗**：等等……你？\
**Pug Dog**: Wait. You!

他用充满不可思议的眼神瞪向梁月——不。\
He stares.

准确来说，他瞪着的是梁月身后的那个躲躲闪闪的身影。\
Not at her, precisely, but at the figure cowering behind her.

**癞皮狗**：——是你，是你！该死的，是你出卖了我！\
原来你和警察原本就是一伙儿的！\
**Pug Dog**: It was you! You f**kin' traitor! I shoulda known you were workin' with the cops.

空脑袋疑惑地看向那个人。\
Loggerhead tilts her head in confusion.

**空脑袋**：……嗯？你这话是什么意思？\
**Loggerhead**: Huh? What are you talking about?

**斯考特**：呃……不，听我解释，这是个误会……\
**Scott**: Uh, wait, let me explain. This is just a misunderstanding.

**梁月**：请不要担心，斯考特小姐。\
这位先生的确误会了，我会向大家解释的。\
**Liang Yue**: Don't worry, Ms. Scott. You're right. There has been a misunderstanding between you and him. Allow me to explain.

斯考特闻言刚松了一口气，但梁月的下一句话却直接让她如遭雷殛，呆立在了原地。\
Scott heaves a sigh of relief, only for Liáng's next words to hit her like a thunderclap.

**梁月**：你的确并没有出卖这位先生的意思，也并没有与我们合谋。\
**Liang Yue**: You never had the intention of betraying him, nor were you working with us.

**梁月**：你只是诚实地将要出售的物品交给了他——仅此而已。\
**Liang Yue**: You simply gave him the item you wanted to sell. That's it.

## SC-13 A计划外 / A Project Gone Awry

**空脑袋**：我……不明白。\
**Loggerhead**: What? What do you mean?

空脑袋看向自己的好友，又看向义愤填膺的黑市中间人，最后茫然地望向眼前面色平静的梁月。\
Loggerhead turns to her friend, then to Pug Dog, then back to Liáng. She remains totally expressionless.

**梁月**：谜底其实并不复杂，虽然我们遭遇了许多干扰项……但只要排除它们，就不难看清真相。\
**Liang Yue**: The truth was always there—hidden beneath the lies and distractions. All you have to do is whittle them down, one by one.

**梁月**：导致唐人街怪事频发的直接原因是神秘学管理品《三燕归巢》，它的确和菲林士多导演有着极深的渊源……\
**Liang Yue**: The probable cause of the events in Chinatown is the Reunion of the Three Swallows film reel, and apparently, Ms. Noire has a history with it.

而这份“渊源”的具体情况暂时还并不明晰。\
梁月向菲林士多的方向看了一眼，只得到了一张菲林士多招牌式的笑脸。\
And yet, the specifics of this history remain unclear. Liáng glances at Noire, only to be met with her signature unreadable smile.

**梁月**：……但无论如何，菲林士多导演和基金会并没有什么关系，她绝不可能自己潜入基金会盗出《三燕归巢》，这位先生或是其他人也是一样。\
**Liang Yue**: But Ms. Noire doesn't have anything to do with the Foundation. There's no way she could sneak into the ACD and steal the film. The same goes for this gentleman or any other outsider.

**梁月**：将《三燕归巢》等神秘学管理品盗出，并嫁祸给莱瑟姆小姐的一定是基金会的内部人士。\
**Liang Yue**: So, the thief who wants Ms. Latham to take the fall must work for the Foundation.

**梁月**：这一人物很可能是神秘学藏品管理部的人，这样才能够不为人知地盗出藏品。\
**Liang Yue**: In fact, since they stole the item without being noticed, they probably work for the ACD.

**梁月**：这一人物也必定是莱瑟姆小姐身边的人，这样才会知道莱瑟姆小姐特殊的“健忘症”体质，将她选为自己的替罪羊。\
**Liang Yue**: And they must be close to Ms. Latham to know enough about her amnesia to be able to take advantage of it.

**空脑袋**：——但神秘学藏品管理部有很多人，知道我情况的人也有很多，不能这样就断定是斯考特呀！\
**Loggerhead**: But loads of people at the ACD know about my condition. You can't pin it on Scott just from that.

这个始终一副傻乎乎好脾气模样的意识唤醒者，第一次采用了强硬的语气与激烈的言辞。\
For the first time, the ever-cheerful Loggerhead takes on a harsh, indignant tone.

她气愤地说完后，望向自己的好友。\
She stamps her foot and turns to her friend.

**空脑袋**：对不对，斯考特？这样说你也太过分了，也说点什么呀！\
**Loggerhead**: That's way too harsh, right, Scott? Right?

**空脑袋**：……斯考特？你为什么不说话？\
**Loggerhead**: Scott? Say something, will you?

**斯考特**：…………\
**Scott**: ...

她的好友低着头，没有回答这名茫然的意识唤醒者。\
Scott only stares at the floor as she tries to calm her quivering breath.

**斯考特**：……你是什么时候发现的？\
**Scott**: How long have you known?

斯考特终于挤出了她的第一句话。\
Scott has finally managed to force out a few words.

**梁月**：从莱瑟姆小姐告诉我你们是很好的朋友时。\
恕我直言，您的计划有许多漏洞。\
**Liang Yue**: Since Ms. Latham said you were good friends. With all due respect, your plan was far from perfect.

**斯考特**：…………唉，我就知道。\
你们把我拉到这里，其实就是想让这个男人指认我。\
**Scott**: Ugh, I knew it. You brought me along so this guy would call me out.

长叹一声后，斯考特抬起了头，语气中带着一种自暴自弃般的舒畅。\
After a long sigh, Scott lifts her head, speaking with a resigned kind of ease.

**斯考特**：你说得对，我搞砸了。你说我的计划有很多漏洞……那是当然的，因为所谓的“计划”从一开始就被打乱了。\
**Scott**: You're right. I messed up. My plan was far from perfect because, well, I couldn't stick to the so-called plan since the very beginning.

**斯考特**：我把东西藏在空脑袋那里后，才得到基金会已经发现了我所作所为、开始调查的消息。\
**Scott**: I didn't know the Foundation was already investigating the theft until after I'd hidden the items in Loggerhead's room.

**斯考特**：我只好故意把嫌疑引向这个笨蛋，但没想到那盘胶片居然被她不小心装进了行李里，带来了洛杉矶……而我居然被委派成了追查这件事的人。\
**Scott**: Then I had no choice but to use this idiot as the scapegoat. I never thought she'd accidentally bring the film to L.A., or that I'd be ordered to investigate the case.

**斯考特**：我早就联系好了这个中间人，交易的地点正好是洛杉矶，我想这也许是个机会，能够让我按照原计划把胶片出手……\
**Scott**: I got in touch with this guy a long time ago, and the trade site happened to be in L.A. too. So, my plan was to get the film back and sell it right afterwards.

**斯考特**：但现在看来，正是这份贪婪……和对这个笨蛋的优柔寡断，导致了节外生枝。\
**Scott**: But things didn't go as smoothly as I thought. I shouldn't have gotten greedy, or been so nice to this dummy.

她剐了空脑袋一眼，但很快移开了目光，像是不屑，又像是躲闪。\
She shoots a piercing glare at Loggerhead before quickly looking away—whether out of disdain or avoidance is unclear.

**空脑袋**：可是……可是……\
**Loggerhead**: But, but ...

**空脑袋**：我们不是朋友吗？\
**Loggerhead**: We're friends, aren't we?

她的声音很轻，就像是易碎的玻璃。\
但斯考特冷哼一声，毫不犹豫地将它摔了个稀巴烂。\
Her voice is as fragile as brittle glass. Scott shatters it with a scoff.

**斯考特**：谁和你是朋友？整天被人调侃，你居然还笑呵呵的……当我和你走在一起的时候，所有人都觉得我们是一个档次的！\
**Scott**: Friends? Don't be ridiculous. I don't know how you can act like nothing's wrong when literally everyone is laughing at you. And the fact that they thought that I was one of your kind.

**斯考特**：这简直是侮辱！\
我和你来往只是因为……只是因为没有其他的选择而已！\
**Scott**: Ugh! What an insult! I only hung out with you because ... because I had no choice.

**斯考特**：一个记忆只能够维持三天的健忘笨蛋……这不怪我，任何人如果想要做些坏事，并且需要一个替罪羊的时候，毫无疑问都会第一时间想到你。\
**Scott**: You're an idiot who forgets everything every three days. It's your own damn fault. Anyone looking for a scapegoat would immediately think of you.

**波蒂埃**：嘿，闭上你的嘴，少说那些混账话！\
**Poitier**: Quit it! I don't wanna hear any more of your BS.

在波蒂埃的呵斥下，斯考特冷哼一声，不再分给一旁呆若木鸡的“好友”分毫目光。\
Scott scoffs once more, refusing to look at her "friend" for even a second.

**梁月**：伸出手来吧，斯考特小姐。\
您方才所说的所有话，都将成为呈堂供词。\
**Liang Yue**: Hands up, Ms. Scott. Anything you say can and will be used against you in a court of law.

**梁月**：还是说——您打算负隅顽抗？\
**Liang Yue**: Wait, you're still going to fight?

年轻的基金会职员最终放弃了反抗，梁月推着她向波蒂埃停靠在唐人街外的警车走去。\
At last, Scott gives up her resistance. Liáng pushes her toward Poitier's patrol car parked around the corner.

就在她们即将踏出小巷时，空脑袋喊住了她们。\
As they're about to step out of the alley, Loggerhead calls out.

**空脑袋**：等等，斯考特！\
**Loggerhead**: Wait. Scott!

**空脑袋**：告诉我……你为什么要这么做？为什么要偷走基金会的东西？\
**Loggerhead**: I have to know, why did you steal from the Foundation?

**斯考特**：事到如今你问这个做什么？\
**Scott**: Does it matter?

斯考特回过头，诧异地冷笑了一声。\
Scott turns back, laughing coldly in disbelief.

**斯考特**：难道如果我有什么苦衷，会让你更好受一些？\
歇一歇吧，最让我讨厌的就是你那颗天真的傻脑瓜子。\
**Scott**: Would you feel better if I had a reason? Oh, please! Your ignorant, stupid little brain makes me sick.

**斯考特**：当然是为了钱，也是为了证明给那些小看我的人看，让他们知道我决不是个一事无成的废物。\
**Scott**: It was for the money, of course. And to prove to the others that I'm not a bloody fool like you.

**斯考特**：我会做到他们都做不到的事，让他们大吃一惊。\
那些号称万无一失的防盗术式根本不堪一击，只要——\
**Scott**: Imagine the shock on their faces when they discover that I did what none of them could. Those so-called unbreakable arcane security skills were easy to deal with as long as I ...

**斯考特**：只要……？\
**Scott**: I ...

她的话说到一半就止住了。斯考特的脸上逐渐浮现出疑惑的神情。\
Her words trail off, and a puzzled expression crosses her face.

**梁月**：只要怎样？你是怎么骗过基金会和神秘学藏品管理部的防盗术式的？\
**Liang Yue**: You what? How did you bypass the Foundation's security?

**斯考特**：我……不记得了。奇怪，怎么会这样？\
我只记得在走廊，有个女职员和我搭话……\
**Scott**: I don't remember. That's weird. How could I forget? All I remember is that an office lady talked to me in the corridor.

**梁月**：一个女职员？\
那是什么时候的事，她和你说了什么？\
**Liang Yue**: An office lady? When? What did you talk about?

**斯考特**：她……她拿出了一个东西给我看。\
有些晃眼，但很漂亮，那是……\
**Scott**: She ... She showed me something. It was a bit dazzling, but very beautiful. It was ...

**斯考特**：对了……对了！\
那是一颗——\
**Scott**: Oh, oh, right. It was a ...

尖细而锐利的银色丝线切割了空气，斯考特的话语戛然而止。\
A razor-sharp silver needle slices through the air, cutting her off in an instant.

**斯考特**：咕、呃……？\
**Scott**: Ahhhh—?

她茫然地抬起手，触碰扎入自己脖颈中的异物，不明白自己为何突然失去了声音。\
She raises a dazed hand, her fingertips touching the foreign object lodged in her throat, not understanding why her voice has suddenly vanished.

当意识到自己呼吸的能力也同样被剥夺时，她已经栽倒在了地上。\
By the time she's realized she can no longer breathe, her eyes roll back, and she falls to the ground.

皎月隐去了踪迹，只剩下聊胜于无的点点星光洒落在小巷之中，一切在转眼间归于了寂静，只有一个声音异常刺耳。\
Silence falls in the starlit alley. Then, another flash of silver whistles by.

**梁月**：……什么？\
**Liang Yue**: What?

手掌处传来抽痛，梁月这才意识到有和刺入斯考特咽喉中相似的东西，刺入了自己的掌心，令胶片从她的手中滑落。\
A sharp pain blooms in her palm. She looks down to see a sharp silver needle pierced in it. The film slips from her grasp.

塑料制的片盘碾过冰冷坚硬的地面，伴随着咔哒咔哒的声响滚向黑暗的深处。直到一只带着皮质手套的手将它捡了起来，轻柔地拂去上面的尘土。\
The reel rolls across the ground, clicking as it hurtles into the darkness, until a gloved hand picks it up and brushes it off.

**？？？**：真是的，幸亏没有摔坏，不然可就麻烦了。\
**???**: Phew! Still intact. You've got no idea how long I've been looking for this.

**梁月**：你……是……\
**Liang Yue**: You're ...

**奇星**：你好，警探小姐，我们又见面了。\
**Qi Xing**: Hey there, kid. We meet again.

那位曾经名噪一时的明星女演员，向梁月露出了一个明快而富有亲和力的笑容。\
The once-famous star smiles at Liáng with an easy, friendly charm.

**空脑袋**：斯考特……斯考特！\
**Loggerhead**: Scott! Scott!

**癞皮狗**：我的天哪，她是死了吗？\
**Pug Dog**: No f**king way. She dead?

**波蒂埃**：还活着，但……过一会儿就不一定了！\
我这就呼叫救护车和增援！\
**Poitier**: Not yet, but I doubt she can hold on much longer. I'll call an ambulance, and we're gonna need backup.

**梁月**：…………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

空脑袋的尖叫、癞皮狗的惊呼，以及波蒂埃紧张的声音钻进梁月的脑海中，激起了少许涟漪。\
Loggerhead's scream, Pug Dog's cry, and Poitier's tense voice all ring in Liáng's mind.

梁月理性的那一侧已经察觉到了眼下情形所代表的真相，感性的一面却在阻挠她将自己的结论整理成有条理的语言。\
Liáng's rationality has already grasped the reality of the situation, but her emotions are refusing to let her shape the conclusion into clear words.

**梁月**：……为什么你要做这种事？\
**Liang Yue**: Why are you doing this?

就在方才，空脑袋曾经对斯考特发出过类似的质问。\
当时的梁月曾在心底质疑过这个问题的意义。\
When Loggerhead posed a similar question to Scott, Liáng had questioned the inquiry.

无需追问恶人为恶的理由，错了就是错了。邪恶需要被消灭，鬼疫需要被驱逐，仅此而已——这就是梁月自小接受的教诲。\
There is no need to ask why evil chooses to do evil. What's wrong is wrong. Evil must be eradicated. Ghost plagues must be purged. That was the doctrine drilled into Liáng since childhood.

但现在她却无法不做出同样的事。\
But now, she finds herself forced to ask the same thing.

**梁月**：告诉我。我需要知道原因。\
**Liang Yue**: Tell me. I need a reason.

**奇星**：……这就要问我的这位老朋友了。\
**Qi Xing**: It's my old friend that you should be asking.

梁月看着奇星敛去笑容，用和望向自己时截然不同的冰冷目光看向一旁。\
Liáng watches as Qí Xīng's smile fades and her face turns steely.

**奇星**：——好久不见，菲林士多导演。\
**Qi Xing**: Long time no see, Noire.

**菲林士多**：……是呀，的确很久了。\
**Noire**: Yeah, it's been a while.

**菲林士多**：上次见面还是在她墓前的那回吧？\
我们应该多联系的。\
**Noire**: The last time we saw each other was in front of her grave, if memory serves? We really should keep in touch more often.

小巷中的空气如针刺般扎人。\
菲林士多面色如常地笑着，眼底却带着戒备。\
The air in the alley is sharp as a needle. Noire continues to smile, but a wariness lurks behind her eyes.

**菲林士多**：不过，你这就做得有些过分了。\
**Noire**: But you've gone too far this time, my friend.

她看向倒地的斯考特，微微摇了摇头。\
She glances at Scott's fallen body and gently shakes her head.

**菲林士多**：我可不记得有排这么一场戏。\
**Noire**: This isn't part of our story.

**奇星**：不是什么事情都要按照你的安排来的，导演。\
**Qi Xing**: This isn't a set, director. It's not your call.

奇星的话音未落，梁月便看到她抬起了手。\
银光如闪电般刺破黑暗——\
She raises a hand, and a flash of silver pierces through the darkness.

**梁月**：小心——！\
**Liang Yue**: Careful!

少女挡开银针，岿然站在轮椅面前。\
She leaps forward, deflects the needles, and stands firm in front of the wheelchair.

而奇星并不诧异。她微眯着眼睛，就像早已料到一切。\
Qí Xīng shows no surprise. She narrows her eyes a little, as if she foresaw this outcome.

**奇星**：是的，就得这样才行。\
执夜人小姐，很高兴在这里遇到您。\
**Qi Xing**: That's the spirit. This should be fun with you here, little vigil.

**奇星**：这一次，就让我们饰演好彼此的角色吧。\
**Qi Xing**: Let's all play our roles, shall we?

## SC-14 荧屏正发光 / Lit Screen, Lit Eyes

**波蒂埃**：该死！这是电影演员该有的水平吗？！\
**Poitier**: The hell?! I thought movie stars were just empty suits.

银色的锐利光雨再次斥退了梁月与波蒂埃二人的攻击。\
Another volley of silver needles streaks through the air, forcing Liáng and Poitier back.

奇星占据了小巷中间的位置，看似置身在梁月和波蒂埃的前后夹击之中，实则利用二人一前一后的位置关系进行牵制。\
Qí Xīng stands at the center of the alley. Though seemingly trapped between Liáng and Poitier, she skillfully uses their positioning to her advantage.

两名执法者难以顶着误伤同伴的风险开枪或是使用高杀伤力的神秘术攻击，战局僵持不下，几次都险些让奇星抓住破绽脱身。\
Neither officer can risk injuring the other by firing their gun or using an arcane skill, leaving the battle at a deadlock.

**梁月**：这样下去等不到支援到达了……波蒂埃教官，请掩护我！\
**Liang Yue**: We're not going to last much longer. I have to do something. Poitier, cover me.

**梁月**：——强梁既出，罔有不韪。\
**Liang Yue**: Arise Qiángliáng, swift and fierce!

险道兽强梁的祭器出现在了梁月的手上，古老的咒语被一字一顿地念出。\
With the ritual vessel of Qiángliáng in her hand, Liáng recites the ancient incantation, each syllable clear and deliberate.

**奇星**：！\
**Qi Xing**: ...!

她看到那个人猛地转向了自己的方向，抬起了手。\
Qí Xīng looks momentarily stunned.

——那是神秘术的起手式，梁月知道那些锐利的银光即将飞射而来。\
This is the beginning of an incantation. Liáng knows that more silver needles could come flying at her at any moment.

**梁月**：……斩杀凶咎——\
**Liang Yue**: Banish all evil ...

有一瞬间，她的心中产生了动摇。\
For a brief moment, hesitation creeps over her.

她曾经在儿时一遍又一遍地用憧憬的目光看着荧幕中那潇洒的身影，也曾不知道多少次模仿过电影中那分外飒爽的神秘术技巧。\
As a child, she sat before the screen and watched this figure over and over again, her eyes filled with admiration. She had mimicked her arcane skill countless times.

但她从来没有想到过有一天那些耀眼的银光会刺向自己。\
But she never imagined that, one day, those dazzling silver needles would be aimed at her.

**梁月**：枭截不祥！\
**Liang Yue**: ... and cleanse this place!

——但梁月还是念出了最后几个字。\
Yet, she still speaks the final words of the incantation.

随着最后的话音落下，文字将唤醒古老的契约，险道兽将应召前来。\
它将为梁氏后人所驱役，吞食世间诸般邪祟。\
With these words, an ancient contract will be upheld, and the Xiǎndào Beast will be called upon to devour all evil. As is her right as a descendant of the Liáng family.

——本该是这样的。\
At least, that's what's supposed to happen.

**梁月**：咦……？\
**Liang Yue**: What?

身旁仍一片空荡。\
But the alley remains as empty as it was before.

**奇星**：……！喂！\
**Qi Xing**: Hey!

**波蒂埃**：菜鸟，快躲开啊！\
**Poitier**: Rookie, watch out!

有人推开了她。她重重地摔在地上。\
紧随其后的是冲击。映入眼帘的是银光。钻入耳中的是什么人的喊叫。\
Someone pushes her aside. She hits the ground hard. A flash of silver. The sound of shouting.

然后是鲜血。倒地的声音。粘稠的感觉。温度。骚乱声……\
Then, blood. A body falling. A sticky sensation. Warmth. Chaos ...

……\
...

那之后的事情，梁月记得不是很清楚了。\
The events that follow are hazy in Liáng's memory.

**男子**：时辰还没到，站稳！\
**Enraged Man**: Training isn't over! Stand firm!

严厉的呵斥声刺破混沌的薄膜，令意识突兀地接续了起来。\
A sharp reprimand shatters her haze, pulling her back to focus.

**梁月**：那是……\
**Liang Yue**: That's ...

令人眼熟的小院。一个有着熟悉面孔的男人。\
A familiar courtyard. A man with a familiar face.

他的面前正站着一个小女孩。\
她扎着马步，汗水从额前滑落，腿已经力竭，开始晃晃悠悠地打颤。\
In front of him, a little girl stands in horse stance, sweat rolling down her forehead. Her legs are trembling.

但男子手上的黑檀木戒尺仍然毫不留情地拍在了女孩的肩膀上。\
Yet, the man's ebony ruler comes down mercilessly on the girl's shoulder.

**男子**：不像样！\
和你讲了多少次，要沉肩坠肘，心静体松！\
**Enraged Man**: Wrong! Shoulders and elbows down! Relax your body and mind. How many times do I have to repeat myself?

院子围墙上，露出了几个小脑袋，正边笑边捂住嘴巴，不时窃窃私语。\
Two small heads peek over the courtyard wall, giggling and whispering to each other.

**男孩**：嘘……看，她就要撑不住了。\
**Boy**: Shh. Look, she's gonna fall any second.

**女孩**：嘻嘻，活该！谁叫她向老师告密的。\
**Girl**: Heh heh, that's what she gets for saying that to the teacher.

他对着扎马步的女孩歪斜着表情，做出了一个大大的鬼脸。\
女孩本就早已疲惫不堪的双腿一垮，终于支撑不住，整个人仰倒在地上。\
The boy makes a goofy face at the girl holding the stance. The girl, already exhausted, finally loses her balance and collapses to the ground.

**男子**：疏于练功，三心二用，你看看你怠惰了多少……\
以这样的体魄，强梁又如何能服从你？\
**Enraged Man**: You don't come to training, you're distracted, and you're lazy. How could Qiángliáng obey such an undisciplined master?

**男子**：继续站，我等一会过来检查。\
扎不稳马步，今天晚上就不要吃饭了！\
**Enraged Man**: Get up. I'll come back later. If you can't do it by sundown, there will be no dinner tonight.

父亲失望地摇着头离去，只留下女孩躺在原地，气喘吁吁。\
The man, her father, shakes his head in disappointment and walks away, leaving the girl gasping for breath on the ground.

**女孩**：走吧走吧，没意思，她又要站一天了。\
要不要去录像厅？\
**Girl**: Let's go. She's gonna be there all day. Wanna go to the theater?

**男孩**：好呀！去街角那家吧，今天他们家放《神秘警探C07》！\
**Boy**: Sure! The one on the corner's playing Detective C07 today.

墙头上的孩子们也失去了对她的兴趣，嬉笑着跳下墙根跑走了。\
The children hop down from the wall, laughing as they scurry off.

**梁月**：……我也想去录像厅。\
**Liang Yue**: The theater? I want to go, too.

谁也没有听到女孩的声音。\
No one hears her voice.

除了她自己。\
No one but herself.

**梁月**：我想起来了。\
那个时候……我很讨厌强梁。\
**Liang Yue**: I remember it now. I hated Qiángliáng when I was little.

**梁月**：什么十二侲子之后、强梁之主，什么惩奸除恶、驱除鬼疫、光宗耀祖、履行使命……这些对一个孩子来说，都太过遥远了。\
**Liang Yue**: Father was always trying to teach me something, about the Twelve Zhènzǐ, the Master of Qiángliáng, fighting the wicked and dispelling evil, fulfilling the duty of my inheritance. I was only a child. It was all too difficult for me to understand.

**梁月**：没有孩子喜欢告密者和总是板着脸的小班长。当他们成群结队地嬉戏玩闹时，我只能一个人在一旁看着，假装自己并不在意。\
**Liang Yue**: The other kids hated me. I was a traitor, a class president who took the side of the adults and enforced the rules. They'd all hang out and have fun together while I was left alone. I envied them.

**梁月**：……但其实，我也想要跟他们一样。\
**Liang Yue**: Their lives were simple. I wanted that.

**梁月**：一角、两角……五角……\
**Liang Yue**: One cent, two cents ... five ...

小猪存钱罐被狠心地摔碎在地。女孩从它的残骸中一枚一枚地数出里面的硬币与一张张皱巴巴的纸钞。\
Her piggy bank lies smashed on the ground as she picks through the shards to count every coin.

瓷片的残骸中，半张破碎的面孔睁着无辜的双眼看着她。\
Amidst the broken porcelain, half of a shattered face stares up at her innocently.

**梁月**：对不起，小猪……\
**Liang Yue**: I'm sorry, Piggy.

女孩伸出手，小心翼翼地摸了摸小猪的面孔。似乎是在安抚，也像是在道别。\
She gently brushes her fingers over its face in a gesture of comfort—or farewell.

**梁月**：那天我没有理会父亲的要求，独自拿着积蓄找到了那些孩子说的街角的录像厅。\
**Liang Yue**: That day, I disobeyed Father, gathered up all my savings, and headed to the theater.

**梁月**：那就是我第一次看《神秘警探C07》。\
它的确很有意思，在观看的过程中，我也的确很开心。\
**Liang Yue**: That was the first time I watched Detective C07. It was amazing.

**梁月**：但我也知道，电影里演的都是假的。\
**Liang Yue**: But I knew. It was just fiction. Just an escape.

**梁月**：一部电影无法改变任何事。\
等电影结束后，我还是得回到那个院子里去。\
**Liang Yue**: It wouldn't change anything in my real life. Once the movie was over, I'd have to go back to the same home I had just left.

**梁月**：……我不想回去。\
所以直到片终字幕开始滚动，我也没有离开。\
**Liang Yue**: I didn't want to leave, so I stayed in my seat for the closing credits.

**梁月**：当那些字幕滚动完后，录像带仍在播放，屏幕重新亮了起来。\
**Liang Yue**: But the lights didn't come on when the credits ended. Rather, the silver screen lit up again and played something.

**梁月**：那是电影的花絮，作为主演的奇星，正接受记者的采访。\
**Liang Yue**: It was an interview with Ms. Qí Xīng.

**记者**：奇星小姐，有好多小观众喜欢你的作品，把你当作他们的英雄。\
**Reporter**: Ms. Qí Xīng, many children love your work and see you as their hero.

**记者**：但另一方面，不少成年人觉得你所饰演的警探C07每一次都能够击败恶人的结局过于理想化，反而缺乏了真实感。\
**Reporter**: Yet some adults say that the story of Detective C07 is too unrealistic because she always beats the villain.

**记者**：对此你怎么看呢？你觉得这会是警探C07系列电影的遗憾吗？\
**Reporter**: What's your opinion on this subject? Is it a flaw of the movie?

**奇星**：现实世界已经足够残酷，因此我们才会在电影的世界中寻求一个圆满的结局，寻求一个善有善报、恶有恶报的理想世界。\
**Qi Xing**: The real world's already a cruel and unfair place. Our movie's idealistic, yes, but it shows us a world where good is rewarded and evil is punished. We need that.

**奇星**：如果连在大荧幕上，我们都不被允许相信正义与公理，那么我们又还能相信什么呢？\
**Qi Xing**: If we can't accept justice and truth even in a fictional world, then what hope do we have for reality?

她注视着镜头，也注视着画面之外，笑容明媚而潇洒，眼神比星光还要明亮。\
Qí Xīng gazes into the camera, but also beyond it, her smile carefree, her eyes shining even brighter than the stars.

**奇星**：C07是正义的代言人，是锄强扶弱、匡扶正义的英雄，是在无论怎样的危机与险境之下，都能带来那个大家所期盼的圆满结局的人。\
**Qi Xing**: C07 is justice, a hero who fights evil and cares for the weak. She'll always bring a happy ending, no matter what she's faced with.

**奇星**：——我希望我们的电影和C07这个角色能够带给银幕前的观众们力量与勇气。\
**Qi Xing**: One of our goals with this movie, and with the character, was to inspire and encourage our viewers.

**奇星**：也许并不是每一个人都能够在现实世界中成为一个真正锄强扶弱的战士，这毕竟是一条十分艰难的道路。\
**Qi Xing**: We know that most people can't become a C07 in the real world. After all, it's an incredibly difficult path to take.

**奇星**：但我希望我们的电影和C07这个角色，至少能够让大家成为在生活中，给自己身边的人带来“圆满结局”的英雄。\
**Qi Xing**: But we hope that we can at least inspire people to become heroes in their own lives, to create happy endings for themselves and the people around them.

**梁月**：那是个夹杂在片终字幕中的很短一段采访，但当时奇星说的每一个字我都记忆犹新。\
**Liang Yue**: It was just a short interview like any other, but I still remember every word she said.

**梁月**：“身为强梁之主，应驱使险道兽强梁惩奸除恶、驱除鬼疫、守护世间安宁……”\
**Liang Yue**: "As the master of Qiángliáng, you must use your power to fight the wicked and dispel evil. It is your duty to maintain the peace of the world."

**梁月**：父亲无数次的耳提面命中所描绘的、那个没有面孔的形象终于清晰了起来。\
**Liang Yue**: Qiángliáng, the powerful being that had always been a blur to me, suddenly became clear.

**梁月**：我意识到，我不仅仅可以成为那个“给身边人带去圆满结局的英雄”……而且可以成为和电影里的C07一样，“给所有人带去圆满结局的英雄”。\
**Liang Yue**: I realized that I could be more than just a hero who creates happy endings for herself and the people around her. I could be the hero who creates happy endings for everyone, just like C07.

**梁月**：别人也许不行，但是我可以。因为我是梁家之后，强梁之主——那份令我不堪重负的诅咒，在那一天成为了一份祝福。\
**Liang Yue**: She was right. Not everyone can do that, but I could, because I was Yuè of the Liáng family, the master of Qiángliáng. On that day, the burden that had been crushing me suddenly became a blessing.

**梁月**：…………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

**梁月**：那么，到底是哪里出了错呢？\
**Liang Yue**: So, what went wrong?

意识开始被撕裂，刺目的银光无情地将她吞没。\
The image fades as another silver flash brings her back to reality.

警笛声。救护车的声音。血。血。血。止不住的鲜血。\
浸透警服的布料，淹没她的手。\
Sirens. An ambulance. Blood. Blood. Endless blood. It seeps through the fabric of her uniform, drenching her hands.

她听到什么人在喊叫。\
She hears someone shouting.

**梁月**：——坚持住，波蒂埃教官！求求您！\
**Liang Yue**: Stay with me, Poitier. Please!

**梁月**：为什么……为什么您要这么做？\
**Liang Yue**: Why? Why did you do that?

**梁月**：我以为你……我还以为你们讨厌我。\
**Liang Yue**: I-I thought you hated me.

**梁月**：总是这样的。\
**Liang Yue**: People always hate me.

现在梁月听清了。那是她自己的声音，是她在狼狈地喊叫着什么。\
Now she can hear clearly, she realizes it's her own voice, hoarse with desperation.

那个时候波蒂埃教官是怎么回答的来着？\
What did Poitier say to her back then?

血随着她艰难的呼吸，从口鼻中化作血沫被咳出。\
Blood bubbles from her mouth and nose with each painful breath.

**波蒂埃**：咳……原来你知道啊。\
**Poitier**: *cough* You could tell, huh?

**波蒂埃**：但那是……忘了吧，那是之前的事了。\
**Poitier**: But that's—*cough*—that's in the past. Forget it.

**波蒂埃**：那个时候我们不是还不了解你嘛……\
**Poitier**: We just didn't know you yet.

满是鲜血的手无力地拍了拍梁月的脸颊，随后落下。\
A bloodstained hand weakly pats Liáng's cheek before falling limp.

**梁月**：……波蒂埃教官？\
**Liang Yue**: Poitier?

**梁月**：等等，不要……波蒂埃教官——！\
**Liang Yue**: No! No!! Please! Poitier!

**波蒂埃**：叫那么惨做什么，我还没到要你来鸣枪礼的地步！\
**Poitier**: Ugh, will you shut up? I'm not dead yet.

**梁月**：呃……？！\
**Liang Yue**: Ugh!

难以想象是来自因伤卧床病号的雷霆一击，让梁月从睡梦中惊醒。\
A thunderous smack, unbelievable from someone confined to a hospital bed, jerks Liáng awake from her nightmare.

额头被弹过的地方一阵发痛，梁月茫然地环顾四周，映入眼帘的是素净的病房和一脸愠色的自家教官。\
Liáng's head throbs. Dazed, she looks around, taking in the sterile white of the hospital room and the irritated face of her instructor.

**波蒂埃**：怎么会有人来探望伤员，然后自己趴在这里睡着了的？\
我的腿都要麻了……还有，擦擦你的口水。\
**Poitier**: The hell you doing sleeping on my thigh, huh? Ugh, my leg's gone numb. And clean up the drool on your chin.

**梁月**：什么？抱歉——\
**Liang Yue**: What? Ah. I'm sorry.

**波蒂埃**：逗你的，你没有流口水。\
**Poitier**: Just kidding, boo. You're not drooling.

**梁月**：…………\
**Liang Yue**: ...

**波蒂埃**：好了，帮我把电视打开吧，在你睡得正香的时候，我都快闷死了。\
**Poitier**: Alright, turn on the TV for me. I was bored out of my mind waiting for you to wake up.

## SC-15 紧急播报 / This Just In

**空脑袋**：听说高个子警官小姐醒了？我给你们带了中餐外卖，你们一定饿了——\
**Loggerhead**: Tall Officer, are you up? I got you guys Chinese food. You must be hungry.

**波蒂埃**：嘘。\
**Poitier**: Shh.

病房中的两位警官，正全神贯注地盯着电视机屏幕里的画面。\
The two officers are both staring intently at the television screen.

她们手里的纸杯子，正被握出一圈圈褶皱。\
The paper cups in their hands are crumpled tight.

**记者**：现在近二十名待定罪的嫌疑犯，多数已经失去意识，正在紧急抢救。\
**Reporter**: Almost 20 suspects in the holding cell were injured. Most were found unconscious at the scene and are now in critical condition at the hospital.

**记者**：据说将无罪释放的炼金黑市操盘手“卡斯特”、芝加哥黑帮头目的亲信“郊狼杰森”也在其中……\
**Reporter**: The victims include arcane black market dealer Caster and Chicago gang leader Jason the Coyote, both of whom have since been acquitted of their crimes.

在记者的身后，是黑烟滚滚的车祸现场。\
火焰舔舐着地面上的机油，令路面升腾起一阵阵可怕的热浪。\
Behind the reporter, thick black smoke billows from the scene of a car accident. Flames lick at the oil spilled on the road, sending waves of searing heat into the air.

**医护人员**：别挡道，别挡道，挪开你们的摄像机！救护车，开过来一点！这些病人需要立即静脉通道补液，防止休克！\
**Medical Staff**: Cameras, out of the way, out of the way! The ambulance needs to come through. We need banana bags stat, or these people could go into shock.

**受伤的嫌疑犯Ⅰ**：啊、啊啊——！我的皮肤好烫！救救我，救救我！\
**Injured Suspect I**: Ah. My skin. It burns. Help, help!

**受伤的嫌疑犯Ⅱ**：干了这件事的王八蛋，无论你谁……你等着！我一定要扒了你的皮！\
**Injured Suspect II**: Whoever you are who did this, just wait and see. I'll, I'll tear you apart, you asshole!

医护人员推开记者，大汗淋漓地推着担架床。\
Medical personnel shove past the journalist as they hurry over with a stretcher.

嫌犯夹杂着痛哭哀号声的咒骂与怒吼被电视台的麦克风捕捉，那些声音中饱含的痛苦与怨毒令听者不禁寒毛直竖。\
The cursing and wailing of the deranged man behind the reporter echo in the background. It sends a chill down their spines.

**记者**：事故的原因被推测是遭遇“针人”袭击的受害者，因不明原因出现了精神异常的症状，纵火点燃了法院的羁押室。\
**Reporter**: The fire is speculated to have been started by a victim of a Nightpiercer attack who displayed signs of mental instability.

**记者**：然而与此同时，利贝尔街区的拘留所与唐人街警局也发生了相似的事件，另外两个现场的状况同样不容乐观。\
**Reporter**: At the same time, similar incidents have occurred at the Liber Street Detention Center and the Chinatown Police Station. The situations at both sites are similarly concerning.

**记者**：据悉，负责调查此事的神秘学犯罪科正在考虑这些事件的关联性。始终未能告破的“针人”连续袭击案件的嫌疑犯有着重大嫌疑。\
**Reporter**: It has been reported that the Division of Arcane Affairs is considering the potential connections between these incidents. The mysterious figure behind the unresolved Nightpiercer attacks remains their top suspect.

**记者**：和以往“针人”制造的袭击案受害者相同，这一次事件的受害者仍均为恶迹斑斑的犯罪分子。\
**Reporter**: As with the previous attacks attributed to the Nightpiercer, the victims of these incidents are once again notorious criminals with extensive records.

**记者**：然而面对“针人”明显升级的犯罪行为，支持“针人”的声音逐渐减少，越来越多的市民担忧日常生活及生命安全受到威胁。\
**Reporter**: However, in light of the Nightpiercer's escalating criminal activities, support for the figure is dwindling as concerns for safety rise.

**记者**：面对“针人”事件长期未得到破获的质疑声，在此次案件的新闻发布会中，神秘学犯罪科的埃尔登警长表示——\
**Reporter**: In response to ongoing skepticism regarding the lack of resolution in the Nightpiercer case, Deputy Chief Elden of the Division of Arcane Affairs stated during the press conference that—

电视遥控器上的关机键被躺在床上的病号毫不留情地按下。\
Poitier slams the power button on the remote before flicking it aside.

随后她将遥控器丢到一旁，粗暴地拔掉手背上的输液针头，抓起床边自己的制服就往身上套。\
She yanks the IV needle from her hand and grabs her uniform from the bedside.

**波蒂埃**：该死的，在我晕过去的那么一小段时间里，奇星就已经把整座城市都要搅得天翻地覆了吗！\
**Poitier**: F**k! I pass out for half a day, and Qí Xīng's already turned the city into her personal playground?

**波蒂埃**：菜鸟，拿上你的东西，现在可不是在床上睡大觉的时候了，我们也去加入调查——\
**Poitier**: Grab your stuff, rookie. We're hitting the road. Gotta find this b**ch before she kills someone.

**波蒂埃**：你为什么不动？\
**Poitier**: What, your feet stuck to the floor or something?

风风火火的波蒂埃，看到梁月仍然僵坐在原地，这才停下了动作。\
而梁月抿了抿嘴唇，在波蒂埃狐疑的注视下艰难地开了口。\
Poitier stops only when she notices Liáng still sitting motionless. Liáng purses her lips, struggling to speak under Poitier's skeptical gaze.

**梁月**：……其实，埃尔登警长已经下达了指令，将我们排除在作战计划之外了。\
**Liang Yue**: Deputy Chief Elden took us off the case. It was an official order.

事件需要倒回到数小时前，神秘学犯罪科的办公室中一反往日的喧嚣，安静得落针可闻。\
A few hours earlier, the L.A. office for the Division of Arcane Affairs fell into an eerie silence.

**埃尔登警长**：——昨日深夜，来自圣洛夫基金会神秘学藏品管理部的康斯坦丝·斯考特小姐在一场非法神秘学物品交易的现场遭遇了袭击，如今仍未脱离生命危险。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Early this morning, Constance Scott, a staff member of the Foundation's Arcanum Containment Department, was assaulted during an illegal arcane object trade. She's still in critical condition.

**埃尔登警长**：经过鉴识科的确认，袭击者在现场残留的神秘术痕迹，与被命名为“针人”的连续袭击案犯人留下的痕迹一致。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Forensic Services has confirmed that the arcane skill traces found at the scene of the attack match those left by the suspect in the ongoing Nightpiercer case.

**埃尔登警长**：根据在场的菲林士多女士以及见习执夜人梁月的指认，我们已经确认原B级通缉犯“针人”的真实身份。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Thanks to Noire and our Vigiles cadet Liáng Yuè, who were both at the scene of the attack, we've been able to confirm the identity of the Nightpiercer.

**埃尔登警长**：真名奇星，女性，29岁，出生于香港，原电影演员。\
她曾出演过《神秘警探C07》系列的主角，算是小有名气。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Name's Qí Xīng, a 29-year-old former movie actress from Hong Kong. She played the lead role in the Detective C07 series, where she gained a reasonable amount of fame.

**埃尔登警长**：但在这个系列结束后，她的事业却并不顺利，出演的几部电影都反响平平，最终于数年前息影。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: She was in a few more movies after that, but no big hits. She officially retired from acting a few years ago.

**埃尔登警长**：行为分析科认为，是事业失败导致的落差让她的心理失衡，将电影中自己饰演的角色和自己混淆了。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: The BAU's come to the conclusion that she's confused herself with her movie character—possibly a result of a mental imbalance caused by the setbacks in her career.

**埃尔登警长**：她错以为自己是电影里那个“锄强扶弱的正义英雄”C07，对自己认为是邪恶的存在予以“制裁”，是义警型的犯罪者。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: She thinks she's the real-life C07, the hero who fights evil and cares for the weak. In short, we have a "vigilante" on our hands.

**埃尔登警长**：雪上加霜的是，基金会神秘学藏品管理部的“小小纰漏”导致危险神秘学管理品——“被诅咒的胶片”《三燕归巢》流落到了我们的城市中。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Thanks to a minor mistake from the Foundation's Arcanum Containment Department, we also have a dangerous arcane item, a cursed film reel called Reunion of the Three Swallows, somewhere in the city.

**埃尔登警长**：经过见习执夜人梁月的调查，昨日遇袭的康斯坦丝·斯考特小姐被证实正是监守自盗的犯人。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Liáng has confirmed that Constance Scott, the staff member who was assaulted by Qí Xīng yesterday, is the perpetrator of the theft.

**埃尔登警长**：唐人街近日出现了大量精神状态异常的患者，被意外触发的神秘学管理品《三燕归巢》正是罪魁祸首。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: As you're all aware, there's been an explosion in mental disorders in Chinatown. We now know that their source is the cursed film reel.

**埃尔登警长**：如今它落入了奇星之手，这让我们的嫌犯的危险度又上升了一个台阶。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: It's currently in Qí Xīng's possession, which makes her even more dangerous.

**埃尔登警长**：它是一件与嫌犯颇有渊源的物品，我们有理由怀疑获得《三燕归巢》本身就是她的目的之一。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Having learned about the history behind this arcane film, we have reason to believe that obtaining it was one of her motives.

**埃尔登警长**：在昨晚危险神秘学管理品《三燕归巢》落入嫌犯之手后，城中已经出现了多个符合“针人”作案规律与习惯的袭击事件。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Since the film's been in her possession, there have been multiple assaults around the city, all matching the patterns of the Nightpiercer.

**埃尔登警长**：不同的是，这一次我们的受害者不仅遭到了身体上的折磨，还陷入了和《三燕归巢》受害者症状相似的精神异常状态。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: But there's one key difference. This time, the victims all showed the same mental disorder as the victims of the film.

**埃尔登警长**：嫌犯疑似能够一定程度上操控《三燕归巢》的力量为己用，而她的作案频率和力度也正在急速上升。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: We believe that the suspect is able to control the film's power to some extent, and she's using it to commit escalating crimes at a much higher frequency.

**埃尔登警长**：趁她采取更极端、危险的手段之前，我们必须先一步行动。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: We need to act before the situation gets out of control.

**埃尔登警长**：基金会和夜巡特遣的援兵已在路上，但在他们赶到之前，我们需要自己保护我们的城市。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Reinforcements from the Foundation and the Vigiles Bureau are already on the way. We will do whatever we can to protect our city before they arrive.

他停顿了片刻，目光扫过面前的每一个身影，一个又一个名字从他的口中被点出。\
He pauses for a moment as he sweeps his gaze over the officers before him.

**埃尔登警长**：……最后还有詹姆斯以及卡特，你们负责专门处理这件事，我亲自带队。\
其他人的工作安排不变，坚守你们的岗位。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: James, Carter, I'm putting you on the case. You'll be taking direct orders from me. The rest of you stick to your posts.

**梁月**：埃尔登警长，我想要请问——\
**Liang Yue**: Excuse me, Deputy Chief Elden. I need to ask you something.

**埃尔登警长**：我知道你要问什么。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: I already know what it is.

在梁月开口之前，埃尔登抢先了一步。\
他的开场白和梁月预想的不同，语气甚至称得上是平和。\
Before Liáng can speak, Elden cuts her off. His tone is calmer than she expected.

**埃尔登警长**：你和波蒂埃率先察觉了唐人街一带发生的事件，并立刻进行了调查。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: You and Poitier saw that something was going on in Chinatown and started an investigation yourselves.

**埃尔登警长**：你们找到基金会神秘学藏品管理部监守自盗案件的真正犯人，并且阻止了一场本可能走向更糟糕后果的袭击事件。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: You found the culprit behind the ACD theft and stopped an assault that could've ended much worse.

**埃尔登警长**：在这一点上，你们做得很好。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: You've done a great job.

但他的话锋一转。\
But then his tone shifts.

**埃尔登警长**：然而在袭击事件发生的当时，你本有机会当场抓捕嫌犯，却没能做到。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: But there's one key thing you failed to do. You had a chance to apprehend the Nightpiercer right then and there, but somehow she slipped through your fingers.

**埃尔登警长**：根据你的报告和目击者的证言，你未能在和嫌犯对抗时成功施展神秘术召唤出自己的密友“险道兽强梁”。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: According to your report and the witnesses' statements, you failed to summon your legendary beast when you confronted the suspect.

**埃尔登警长**：你的失误导致了抓捕失败，也令你的搭档承受了计划之外的伤害。\
而在抓捕“针人”的行动中，我需要的是更加稳定、更加可靠的警员。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: As a result, not only did the suspect get away, but your partner sustained an avoidable injury. I need my best, most reliable officers on this case.

停顿片刻，他做出了最终宣判。\
After a brief pause, he delivers his final verdict.

**埃尔登警长**：——所以很抱歉，梁。\
这一次的作战计划中，不会有你们的位置。\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Sorry, Liáng, but you don't make the cut. The two of you will be excluded from the operation.

**波蒂埃**：这根本胡扯！这可是我们的案子，结果我们要被排除在外？\
**Poitier**: This is bulls**t! He can't cut us out. This is our case!

**波蒂埃**：我不接受！\
**Poitier**: No. We're doing this.

**空脑袋**：你不要乱来呀！波……波波警官！\
医生说虽然你没有什么大碍，但还是需要卧床一段时间休养呢！\
**Loggerhead**: Calm down, Ms. Po ... Ms. Potty! Even if you feel fine, the doctor said you had to stay in bed for at least a few days.

**波蒂埃**：我叫波蒂埃！而且我好得很，根本不需要什么休——\
**Poitier**: The name's Poitier. And I'm fine, okay? Stop trying to—

**波蒂埃**：咳、咳咳咳！\
**Poitier**: *cough*

事实胜于雄辩，梁月将套上警服正欲蹦下病床的波蒂埃又按了回去，这次波蒂埃没有反抗。\
Facts speak louder than words. Liáng gently leads Poitier back down onto the bed. This time, Poitier doesn't resist.

**波蒂埃**：该死……所以到底是怎么一回事，为什么那个时候你的强梁没有出现？\
**Poitier**: Damn it. So what went wrong? How come your friend, Tángláng, was it?—didn't show up?

**梁月**：若心智不坚，私欲不克，强梁恐会反噬其主——我的父亲总是对我再三叮嘱，但看起来强梁识破了我的动摇。\
**Liang Yue**: Qiángliáng must've sensed my hesitation and refused my summon. You see, if its master can't overcome their selfish desires with an unwavering heart, it can turn on them. Father used to warn me about it.

**梁月**：——但我保证，这样的事绝不会再发生。\
**Liang Yue**: But that won't happen again, I promise.

波蒂埃眯起眼睛，注视了梁月片刻。\
Poitier narrows her eyes as she studies Liáng for a moment.

**波蒂埃**：……好吧，既然你这么说。\
所以你是什么打算？\
**Poitier**: Heh heh. If you say so, what're you gonna do now?

梁月深吸了一口气，给出了她的答案。\
Liáng takes a deep breath.

**梁月**：我会继续追查这件事，亲自找到奇星小姐。\
**Liang Yue**: I'll continue with the investigation. I need to find Qí Xīng.

**空脑袋**：咦？\
但是那个凶巴巴的大叔不是说不让你参加作战计划吗？\
**Loggerhead**: What? But that angry grandpa already pulled you off the case.

**梁月**：我必须要这么做。\
**Liang Yue**: I have to do this.

**波蒂埃**：为了什么？为了完成你身为那强梁之主、惩奸除恶的职责吗？\
**Poitier**: What for? Because of your duty to fight evil as the master of Qiángliáng?

波蒂埃皱起了眉，显然她并不喜欢自己的这个推测。\
但梁月却出乎她意料地，摇了摇头。\
Poitier furrows her brow. But to her surprise, Liáng shakes her head.

**梁月**：不管所谓家族的使命，还是“警探C07”，它们都曾一度是我的路标。\
因为有了它们，今天的我才会站在这里。\
**Liang Yue**: I've always had two things guiding me: my duty as a member of the Liáng family and the spirit of C07.

**梁月**：但如今强梁一度无视了我的呼唤，C07和奇星小姐的形象也已不再光辉，那些引领我来到此处的东西都已经不再确凿坚实。\
**Liang Yue**: But now, Qiángliáng has ignored my summon, and Qí Xīng has turned out to be anything but a hero. They were once the beacons of my life, but not anymore.

**梁月**：正因为如此——也许这是一个机会。\
**Liang Yue**: This could be a setback, yes, or, it could be an opportunity.

**梁月**：是我有生以来第一次能够抛开其他所有，只专注于寻找“我”想要做什么的机会。\
**Liang Yue**: For the first time in my life, I can think about what I really want without having to consider anything else.

短暂的错愕后，病床上的警员笑了出来。\
After a brief moment of surprise, Poitier lets out a laugh.

**波蒂埃**：你知道吗，菜鸟。\
每次你说那些什么强梁之主的使命云云的话时，我都觉得别扭得不行。\
**Poitier**: You know what, rookie, it always grinds my gears when you talk about your duty and all that stuff.

**波蒂埃**：但你现在这样，就挺顺眼的。\
**Poitier**: But what you're saying now? I like it.

**梁月**：您……不阻拦我吗？\
**Liang Yue**: Aren't you going to stop me?

**波蒂埃**：为什么要阻拦？\
说到底这本来就是我们开始的案子，跟到最后又有什么不对？\
**Poitier**: Why would I? It's our case, isn't it? There's nothing wrong with doing our job.

**波蒂埃**：如果埃尔登问起来，你就说你刚好路过发现了嫌犯，顺手制服了就行了呗！\
**Poitier**: If Elden b**ches about it, just tell him you bumped into the crook when you were strolling around the city.

**梁月**：……还能这样？\
**Liang Yue**: Seriously?

**波蒂埃**：有什么不能的？\
**Poitier**: Yeah. Nothing wrong with that, is there?

**波蒂埃**：——那么现在，和我说说你的计划吧。\
你打算怎么做？\
**Poitier**: So what's the game plan, huh? What're you gonna do?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：……怎么还是这一幕，拍了得有十几遍了吧？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: This scene again? They must've done a dozen takes already, right?

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：是啊，我不懂演技和电影，但我看得出来那个演员太紧张了。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Yeah. I'm no movie expert, but even I can tell the actor's nervous as hell.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：换了谁能不紧张呢？\
一个危险通缉犯，带着一个同样危险又诡异的神秘学管理品……\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Of course, he is. Anyone would be nervous if they knew a wanted criminal could show up at any time and mess you up with arcanum.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：埃尔登为了避免恐慌，没有公开那张“被诅咒的胶片”和其他详细消息，但那个香港导演居然一回来就和剧组的人说了。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Elden tried to keep the details of the case a secret, but that director from Hong Kong told her crew about it as soon as she came back.

唐人街的某条小巷中，两个身着警服的身影分外显眼。\
The two uniformed figures stand in a narrow alley in Chinatown.

他们为保护潜在的被袭击目标菲林士多而来，但却被以“可能妨碍拍摄”为由委婉地拒之门外，如今只能够透过微敞的大门确认片场内的情况。\
They came to protect the potential target of an attack, Noire, but were politely turned away on the grounds of "disrupting filming." Now, they can only confirm the situation inside the set by peering through the slightly ajar door.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：虽然他们的确是有知情权没错啦……但她这么一搞，剧组的那些临时演员立刻就逃跑了近一半，剩下的那些必然也没有心思投入拍戏了。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: I mean, I guess they have the right to know, and to run. Half of the extras got the hell out as fast as they could, and look at the other half. They're too nervous to work.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：可不是嘛——咦，那不是那个见习执夜人女孩吗？她来这里做什么？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: I know. Hey, that's the Vigiles cadet, isn't it? What's she doing here?

**菲林士多**：我听门口的那两位警官说了，你们是来履行协助我拍摄的约定的。\
**Noire**: The officers said you're here to help. Is that right?

**菲林士多**：这可真是太棒了，我这边正缺人手。\
跟我来，我们先去把戏服换上。\
**Noire**: Excellent. We could really use a hand right now. Come, let's get you in costume.

大名鼎鼎的菲林士多导演带着一如往日的和善笑容接待了她的客人。\
Noire greets her guest with her usual amiable smile.

因提前与梁月达成了配合抓捕的协议，菲林士多并未被以涉嫌参与非法神秘学物品交易的罪名起诉。\
Having reached an agreement with Liáng to cooperate in an arrest, Noire has not been charged for her illegal trading of the arcane object.

听说今早她自警局返回了片场后，做的第一件事就是照常拍摄。\
After being released from custody this morning, she immediately returned to filming.

**梁月**：我十分愿意配合您的拍摄，但现在……我有些更加重要的事想要询问您。\
**Liang Yue**: I'm more than happy to help, but first, I have something important to ask you.

菲林士多停下了将轮椅调转方向的动作。\
Noire pauses.

**菲林士多**：这次你倒是开诚布公。\
**Noire**: Right to the point this time, I see.

**梁月**：我不认为事到如今还有遮遮掩掩的必要。\
事已至此，您能够回答我当时的那个问题了吗？\
**Liang Yue**: I don't think there's any need to tiptoe around each other anymore. Could you answer me directly this time?

**梁月**：当年在您、奇星小姐以及那张“被诅咒的胶片”《三燕归巢》的制作者何日君小姐之间，究竟发生了什么？\
**Liang Yue**: What happened between you, Qí Xīng, and Hé Rìjūn, the creator of Reunion of the Three Swallows?

**梁月**：为什么何日君小姐会死？为什么您和奇星小姐都想要得到《三燕归巢》？\
又为什么……奇星小姐会做出这样的事？\
**Liang Yue**: How did she die? Why do you and Ms. Qí Xīng both want that film? And why is she doing this?

菲林士多看着梁月，脸上那种习惯性的笑容淡去了几分。\
Noire looks at Liáng, her usual smile fading slightly.

**菲林士多**：知道之后，你想要做什么呢？\
**Noire**: What do you plan to do with my answers?

**梁月**：……对奇星小姐来说，也许我只不过是成千上万看过她电影的人中的一个。\
**Liang Yue**: To Qí Xīng, I'm probably just another fan.

**梁月**：但对我来说，她和她曾经扮演的角色有着特殊的意义。\
**Liang Yue**: But to me, she and her character mean something.

**梁月**：我想要问她为什么。\
我要亲手抓住奇星小姐，问她为什么要这样做，弄清楚真相。\
**Liang Yue**: I need to know why. I have to arrest her and find out the truth.

**梁月**：也许……一切还能够挽回。\
为了做到这一点，菲林士多女士，我需要您的协助。\
**Liang Yue**: Maybe I can still fix things, but, Ms. Noire, I need your help if I'm going to do it.

这一次，梁月不再有所保留。\
说完这些后，她屏住呼吸，等待着菲林士多的回应。\
This time, Liáng says exactly what she's thinking. She holds her breath as she awaits Noire's response.

**菲林士多**：所以你的意思是说，你想要了解她。\
**Noire**: You mean, you want to know more about her.

**菲林士多**：你想要了解电影幕后，那些演员和剧组人员真正的模样……\
我曾经告诉你，这并不是我会推荐的行为。\
**Noire**: To peek behind the scenes—learn what really happened behind all the movie magic. I told you it's not a good idea.

**菲林士多**：我们的作品之所以诞生，既是为了表达自身，也是为了给人欣赏品评。无论是掌声与赞美，还是鄙夷与唾骂，我们早已做好了心理准备。\
**Noire**: We create works not just to express ourselves, but to entertain. And when we release them to the public, we open ourselves to all kinds of commentary, whether they be sweet or bitter.

**菲林士多**：但作品背后那些活生生的人，却没有被搬到放大镜下供人观赏取乐的义务。\
他们并不是为此而被谁刻意制造出来的。\
**Noire**: But the people behind the characters, behind the production, they are not for entertainment. Their lives are not fiction.

**梁月**：所以……您的意思是拒绝？\
**Liang Yue**: Is that a no?

**菲林士多**：我还没说完呢。\
**Noire**: I haven't finished.

她挑了挑眉，笑得从容，又似乎带着几分调皮。\
She raises an eyebrow, a hint of mischief growing behind her smile.

**菲林士多**：虽然对于试图跨越台前幕后界限的行为我并不推崇，但若是抛开这层身份，仅在两个个体之间讨论这个问题……\
**Noire**: Though I don't advocate trying to cross the line between on and off screen, if we cast aside your relationship as fan and actress and treat you simply as individuals ...

**菲林士多**：我想要了解你——嗯，真不错。\
在我听来，这比什么样的情话都更加动人。\
**Noire**: Saying "I want to know more about you" sounds rather beautiful. It's touching, really.

**菲林士多**：——我可以回答你的问题。\
跟我来吧，执夜人小姐。\
**Noire**: I'll answer your questions, Ms. Liáng. Follow me.

## SC-16 小人物纪录 / Before the Spotlight

**菲林士多**：我想我们的事需要从十一年前说起。\
那个时候我们还未成名，一切都很艰难，但也很美好。\
**Noire**: Our story began 11 years ago. Life was tough, as it is for all young artists.

**菲林士多**：——就像所有故事的最初那样。\
**Noire**: But, like the beginning of many stories, there was a kind of beauty in it.

**菲林士多**：“又一新浪潮导演处女作亮相，《糊涂》虽然底子极佳，但由于大胆创新过度，导致内容诡异颠覆……\
**Noire**: "Another New Wave director has made a splash with her debut movie. Nitwit boasts an excellent foundation, but it may have reached a little too far with its bizarre and unconventional story ..."

**菲林士多**：“即使业内有赞，但大众实在难以欣赏，最终票房惨淡收场，实属糊涂……”\
**Noire**: "While some have praised its daring approach, it has proven too much for the general audience to appreciate, leading to a disappointing box office performance and living up to its title, Nitwit."

**菲林士多**：哈，我能说什么呢？没品味的东西。\
**Noire**: Hah, what can I say? They've got no taste.

那张报纸被她随手扔到了桌边，响亮的声音引来了邻桌人诧异的目光。\
She casually tosses the newspaper onto the table, the loud thud drawing surprised glances from the nearby diners.

**菲林士多**：好吧，想要叫好又叫座，的确需要妥协一些内容。\
可问题是我向来最不擅长，也不喜欢妥协——\
**Noire**: Okay. I guess compromise is inevitable if I want to sell more tickets, but that's not exactly my strong suit.

**？？？**：菲林士多？是你吗？\
**???**: Noire? Is that you?

**何日君**：真是巧，没想到会在这里碰到你。\
这算是近期最让我开心的事了。\
**He Rijun**: What a surprise! It's so good to see you again.

**菲林士多**：你是……泰瑞莎！\
你怎么在这里，你也回国了？\
**Noire**: Teresa?! What are you doing here? When did you come back to Hong Kong?

**菲林士多**：泰瑞莎——用执夜人小姐你所熟悉的名字来称呼的话，就是何日君。\
**Noire**: Teresa, or as you know her by, Hé Rìjūn ...

**菲林士多**：《神秘警探C07》的编剧，我的好友，同时……\
也是那张“被诅咒的胶片”《三燕归巢》的创作者。\
**Noire**: ... was a dear friend of mine, the scriptwriter of Detective C07, and the creator of the cursed film—Reunion of the Three Swallows.

**菲林士多**：咦？\
这个剧本……确实写得不错。有意思。\
**Noire**: Hmm. This is a pretty good script. Interesting.

**菲林士多**：我和泰瑞莎是在电影学院留学期间认识的，我们上同一堂剧作课。\
**Noire**: Teresa and I met while we were studying abroad at a film academy. We took the same scriptwriting class.

**菲林士多**：她总是一个人来上课，挑最不起眼的位置落座……所以最初我们并不认识。\
**Noire**: We didn't talk much at first. She always sat in the corner on her own.

**菲林士多**：最先见到她的名字，是在老师将她的剧本作为优秀范例发给我们看的时候。\
**Noire**: I only got to know her after our teacher showed a script to the class as an example of excellent work.

**菲林士多**：作者的名字是……泰瑞莎。\
**Noire**: The writer's name: Teresa.

**菲林士多**：泰瑞莎写的东西很细腻，却不会让人觉得小家子气。\
她的故事总是轻松的、有趣的……也是温暖的。\
**Noire**: Her stories could strike a balance between the details and the big picture. They were engaging, lighthearted, and warm.

**菲林士多**：所以当我们在那家小餐厅重逢的时候，我立刻就意识到——就是她了。\
**Noire**: So, in that moment, when we met again at the restaurant, I realized she was the one I'd been looking for.

**菲林士多**：那个时候泰瑞莎在一家小出版社做编辑，我直接把她拉到了我的电影工作室。三个月后，她拿来了《神秘警探C07》第一部最初的剧本。\
**Noire**: At that time, she was an editor at a small press. I invited her to join my studio, and three months later, she put the first edition of Detective C07 on my table.

**何日君**：所以……你觉得怎么样？\
要是你觉得哪里不好，我都可以改——\
**He Rijun**: So? What do you think? Just tell me if you want to change anything. I can—

**菲林士多**：我在想主演要选谁。\
**Noire**: I'm thinking about who should play the heroine.

**何日君**：嗯？\
**He Rijun**: Hmm?

**菲林士多**：这个剧本很好，比我想象中的要更好。\
我们就拍这个。\
**Noire**: Your script is remarkable—even better than I expected. Let's shoot it.

**菲林士多**：剧本有了，但主演的人选迟迟没有定下来。我和泰瑞莎物色了许多演员，甚至也考虑过那些知名女星，但都觉得不合适。\
**Noire**: So we had the script, but we couldn't decide who would play the heroine. We held endless auditions, even considered some famous actresses, but none of them fit.

**菲林士多**：——直到那一天的晚上。\
**Noire**: Until that night.

**何日君**：刚才的那几个人，你怎么想？\
我觉得最后的那个似乎还可以……\
**He Rijun**: What did you think of today's candidates? The last one seems okay to me.

**菲林士多**：她不行，少了那股锐气。你也看出来了吧？\
**Noire**: No. She's missing that edge. You can see it too, right?

**菲林士多**：既然你也看出来了，就不要勉强自己同意。\
我不想凑合。\
**Noire**: We're not making lemonade from lemons. At least I'm not.

**何日君**：可是……万一那个完全符合我们想象的完美人选，并不存在呢？\
万一她只存在于我们的想象中呢？\
**He Rijun**: But what if she doesn't even exist? What if our perfect actress only lives in our imaginations?

**菲林士多**：……那我就会一直找。\
直到她出生在现实世界中为止。\
**Noire**: Then we'll keep looking until she's born.

**混混Ⅰ**：诶哟！\
**Hooligan I**: Agh!

**混混Ⅱ**：你你你……你怎么打人？\
**Hooligan II**: Y-You—What're you doing?

**？？？**：我是打你了，怎样？\
手脚不干不净，这里不欢迎你们。\
**???**: I'm kicking your ass. Got a problem with that, perverts?

**？？？**：还不快滚？\
**???**: F**k off!

**混混Ⅰ**：你……你给我等着，这事没完！\
**Hooligan I**: J-Just you wait! We'll come back! You'll see!

那几人留下毫无新意的无趣叫嚣后，狼狈地跑走了。\
随后，他们被丢出来的门后探出一张忧心忡忡的面孔。\
After throwing out a few uninspired threats, the hooligans flee in disgrace. Behind the door, a worried face peeks out.

**老板**：哎呀！这下可麻烦了，那几个人是附近有名的流氓，肯定不会善罢甘休。\
**Restaurant Owner**: You really shouldn't have done that. Those guys live in the neighborhood. They won't just let you off the hook after this.

**老板**：我知道你看不惯那几个人对那个靓女说些不干不净的话，但……\
人家都忍了，你生什么气啊？这下之后我这生意还怎么做？\
**Restaurant Owner**: I know you just wanted to help that girl, but she didn't say anything. Why did you have to make such a scene? What if they come back and tear up the restaurant?

**老板**：阿星，你害惨我了呀！\
**Restaurant Owner**: *sigh* You've gotten me into big trouble, Ā Xīng.

**奇星**：……你放心，老板。\
我会辞职，他们再找来，你就让他们来找我。\
**Qi Xing**: Don't worry, boss. I'll quit. If they come again, tell them to come find me.

**奇星**：……给，这是店门钥匙，以后您可记得早些来开门，否则那些老主顾们都要等了。\
**Qi Xing**: Here's my key. Remember to open early. Your regulars don't like to wait.

**老板**：阿星，你这……唉！\
**Restaurant Owner**: Ā Xīng, what are you ... *sigh*

餐厅老板最终没有挽留。\
那名少女头也不回地走下门前的阶梯——随后，被拦了下来。\
The restaurant owner resigns to taking the key in silence. Without a backward glance, the girl steps down from the door—only to be quickly stopped.

**菲林士多**：看起来你丢了工作。\
**Noire**: Looks like you just lost your job.

**奇星**：……你是谁？关你什么事？\
**Qi Xing**: Yeah, and what's it to you? What do you want?

**菲林士多**：能给你一个工作的人。你对演电影有兴趣吗？\
**Noire**: To offer you a new one. Are you interested in acting?

**菲林士多**：那时候阿星很惊讶，她没有立刻回复，说要考虑考虑。\
泰瑞莎就把自己手上的那一部剧本给了她，让她回家先看看。\
**Noire**: Ā Xīng was surprised when I made the offer. She said she needed to think about it, so Teresa gave her a copy of the script.

**菲林士多**：第二天她就找上了门来，说她做。\
**Noire**: The next day, she knocked on our door and took the offer.

**菲林士多**：后来我们打听了关于阿星的事，知道了她家里条件不好，父亲进了监狱，母亲的精神也有问题，十几岁起她就要养家。\
**Noire**: Later, we learned that Ā Xīng was born into a poor family. Her father was in prison, and her mother had mental issues. She'd been the breadwinner for the family since she was a kid.

**菲林士多**：因为她父亲的关系，很多麻烦会不请自来……所以她每天最常做的事情不是打工，就是和人打架。\
**Noire**: Her father's reputation would often get her into trouble. So, usually, she was either on the way to a job or to a fight.

旧事勾起曾经的回忆，菲林士多颇为感慨似的笑了笑。\
As memories surface, Noire lets out a sentimental smile.

**菲林士多**：电影里的C07总是笑着的，自信又潇洒。\
但其实最开始的时候，阿星从来不笑。\
**Noire**: The C07 you saw always had a confident smile on her face, but in actual fact, Ā Xīng almost never smiled at the beginning.

**菲林士多**：别的演员懂得该入戏时入戏，该抽离角色时就应当及时脱身……但阿星却没有。\
**Noire**: An actor should learn to commit to the moment in front of the camera and come back to reality behind it. But Ā Xīng didn't.

**菲林士多**：她没有给自己设置那个“抽离角色”的逃脱按钮。\
一年三百六十五天，她都在扮演C07。\
**Noire**: She didn't come back to reality. She's never once stopped playing the role of C07 since then, 24 hours a day, 7 days a week.

**菲林士多**：她学会笑了，但却是像C07那样的笑。\
她做事更机灵，而非过去那样横冲直撞——但却是像C07那样的“机灵”。\
**Noire**: She started to smile the way C07 smiled. She went from brash and reckless to sly and methodical—just like C07.

**菲林士多**：警长先生和那些行为分析科的朋友们，弄错了一件事。\
阿星并不是混淆了自己和角色。\
**Noire**: The Deputy Chief and the BAU made a mistake. Ā Xīng has not confused herself with her character.

**菲林士多**：在电影圈摸爬滚打这么多年，我见过不少这样的人。他们错以为自己真是那些他们短暂扮演的、光鲜亮丽的角色，于是忘乎所以。\
**Noire**: After all these years in the movie industry, I've seen a lot of actors get carried away by the glitz and glamor of their characters.

**菲林士多**：阿星却恰恰相反，她把C07这个角色看得比自己更加重要。\
**Noire**: But Ā Xīng is different. She values C07 even more than herself.

**菲林士多**：——为此，她不惜抹杀了自我。\
**Noire**: So much so that, ultimately, it eclipsed her own consciousness.

**菲林士多**：执夜人小姐，你之前曾经询问过我，那些围绕着我和泰瑞莎以及阿星的传闻是否是真的。现在我可以回答你了。\
**Noire**: Ms. Liáng, you asked me which rumors about C07 and the three of us were true. Now I can give you an answer.

**菲林士多**：——是的。它们中的大部分都是真的。\
**Noire**: Most of them were.

菲林士多操控自己的轮椅来到办公桌前，从最下方的抽屉中取出了一只文件袋，将它递给了梁月。\
Noire maneuvers her wheelchair to the desk, pulls out a file from the bottom drawer, and hands it to Liáng.

文件袋颇有分量，里面躺着一本有些老旧的册子，但当梁月试图将它抽出来的时候，先摸到的却是一张同样有些年头了的照片。\
The file is heavy. Liáng opens it up to find an aged photograph.

**梁月**：这是……？\
**Liang Yue**: Is this ...?

那是一张三人的合照，照片中人的身份呼之欲出。\
Three women pose together. Their identities are obvious.

**菲林士多**：我们三个那时候小有名气，所以总有很多双眼睛盯着。\
而人总是经不起用放大镜去看的——每个人都有缺点，我们也不例外。\
**Noire**: We drew a lot of attention after the release of C07. Put a magnifying glass up to anyone, and you'll always find imperfections. We were no exception.

**菲林士多**：阿星太执着，和我一样不懂得妥协。我们两个产生分歧的时候，总是弄得惊天动地，让夹在中间的泰瑞莎很是难做。\
**Noire**: Ā Xīng was as stubborn and uncompromising as I was. When we disagreed, it would blow up into a huge argument, neither one of us giving in to the other. Poor Teresa was always caught in the middle.

**菲林士多**：那个时候的我也是一样，只懂得朝着锚定的方向一个劲走，却不懂得、也不屑于停下来看看四周。\
**Noire**: I was too young, too bullheaded, to realize the consequences that this might cause. I tore a path forward, often ignoring the people around me.

**菲林士多**：泰瑞莎则是性格太好了。\
别人说什么她都照单全收，憋在心里，最后把自己划得伤痕累累。\
**Noire**: Teresa, on the other hand, was kindhearted, perhaps too much so. She never got angry, no matter what people said. She just bottled it up inside and let it eat away at her.

菲林士多望着照片上三人的笑脸，自己脸上的笑容却掺了几分感慨和一丝微不可察的伤感。\
Noire gazes at the smiling faces in the photo, her expression tinged with nostalgia and the faintest hint of sorrow.

**菲林士多**：泰瑞莎不喜欢拍照。她总是对自己的外貌没有自信，所以我们的合照也没有几张。\
**Noire**: She didn't like taking photos. She was self-conscious about her appearance, so we only have a few together.

**菲林士多**：这是在C07第二部拍摄期间拍的，那几乎是我们最好的时候。\
虽然没有想过能够永远并肩，但我们也没有考虑过要在什么时候分道扬镳。\
**Noire**: This one was taken when we were shooting C07 II. We were so close back then. Of course, we knew we'd have to part ways eventually, but we didn't concern ourselves with that.

**菲林士多**：——可那些我们各自怀抱的缺陷，却在看不到的地方制造了无数龟裂。\
等我们察觉到的时候，已经无法挽回了。\
**Noire**: Even then, our shortcomings had started to hurt our relationship. But by the time we realized it, the damage had been done.

**奇星**：不行，这个结局还是太怪了。\
C07不应该是这样的！\
**Qi Xing**: No! This ending makes no sense. C07 would never do that.

**菲林士多**：……那是在拍摄C07第三部的时候，阿星看到那个结局便极力反对。\
**Noire**: When we were making C07 III, Ā Xīng was up in arms about the ending.

**菲林士多**：电影的最后，C07在社火游行中遇到了逃脱法律制裁的狡猾罪犯。她本想要亲自动手，却因为见到了对方和家人团圆的身影，最终放弃了。\
**Noire**: In the sequence, C07 tracks a criminal through a Shèhuǒ Parade, hoping to finish him off herself. But when she finds him sitting at home with his family, she changes her mind.

**菲林士多**：——阿星并不喜欢这个结局。\
**Noire**: Ā Xīng didn't like it.

**菲林士多**：她说C07会让恶人得到应有的惩罚，而不是最终无奈地被现实打败。\
我们为此爆发了无数次争吵，最终也没能达成一致。\
**Noire**: She said that C07 would punish the villain for what he's done, that she would never change her mind. We had countless arguments over this ending, and, of course, we never reached a conclusion.

**菲林士多**：行了，行了！\
到此为止吧，我们这样吵下去也没有意义。\
**Noire**: Alright, alright! Enough! We're not getting anywhere with this.

**菲林士多**：我有个提议。\
**Noire**: I have an idea.

**菲林士多**：——所以我稍微用了一些手段。\
**Noire**: So I cheated.

**菲林士多**：如果是现在的我，一定会选择更巧妙的方式解决。\
**Noire**: Were I in the same position now, I'd solve the problem more delicately.

**菲林士多**：但那个时候的我是个混球，只把电影本身看作第一位。\
除此之外的东西——例如主演的心情，并不在我的考量范围内。\
**Noire**: But I was a jerk back then. The only thing that mattered was the movie. I couldn't care less about what people thought, including my heroine.

**菲林士多**：我让泰瑞莎又写了另外一个版本的结局。我哄阿星说两个版本都拍一条，最后大家一起来看看效果，再决定用哪一版。\
**Noire**: I asked Teresa to write an alternative ending and told Ā Xīng that we'd shoot both endings and pick the better one together.

**菲林士多**：阿星同意了。\
**Noire**: She agreed.

**梁月**：……但后来电影却直接上映了。\
采用的结局，是最初剧本中写的版本。\
**Liang Yue**: But you didn't keep your word. You released the movie with the original ending.

**菲林士多**：电影最后大受好评，但阿星却认为这是我和泰瑞莎的背叛。\
她在首映式直接翻了脸，宣布退出我们三个一起成立的新艺术公司。\
**Noire**: It turned out to be very popular, but Ā Xīng saw it as a betrayal. At the premiere, she announced she was quitting the New Art Company that the three of us had founded together.

**菲林士多**：而我没有阻止她。\
**Noire**: I didn't stop her.

**菲林士多**：——但泰瑞莎一直试图让我们重归于好，就像曾经的每一次那样。\
**Noire**: Teresa tried to mend our relationship, like she always did.

**何日君**：我又写了一部剧本，不是C07的续作，而是一部新的故事。\
如果你们觉得有意思，我们的下一部电影可以就拍它。\
**He Rijun**: I wrote a new story, not for C07—a completely new one. If you're interested, maybe we can use it for our next movie.

**何日君**：我还自己拍了一部片花，虽然是很简单的东西，可能拍得也不好，但……也许我们可以一起看看。\
**He Rijun**: I made a sizzle reel. It's pretty short, probably not as good as the ones we usually make, but shall we watch it together?

**菲林士多**：那部新的故事就是《三燕归巢》。\
**Noire**: It was her proof of concept for Reunion of the Three Swallows.

**菲林士多**：我知道泰瑞莎一直想要结束C07系列，写她自己想要写的东西。\
**Noire**: I knew Teresa had always wanted to put an end to the C07 series and write something she was really passionate about.

**菲林士多**：也许她也认为一个完全不同于C07的故事，可以让阿星从那个角色中走出来，重新找回自己……\
**Noire**: Perhaps she thought a new story would help Ā Xīng move away from C07 and become herself again.

**菲林士多**：但不巧，她来找我们的时候，阿星刚好和我大吵了一架。\
**Noire**: Unfortunately, when she came to show us the script, Ā Xīng and I were in the middle of a fight.

**奇星**：不了，我不会再拍你们的电影了。\
**Qi Xing**: No! I'm not acting in any more of your movies.

**何日君**：阿星，等等——唔！\
**He Rijun**: Ā Xīng, wait! Ugh!

**菲林士多**：从来在泰瑞莎面前都十分乖巧的阿星，当时推开了她愤然离去。\
**Noire**: Ā Xīng had always been kind to Teresa, but on that day, she pushed her out of the doorway and stormed off.

**菲林士多**：而我当时……我说过了，那个时候的我是个混球，说话总是不客气。\
我只是接过她的剧本，粗略地翻了翻。\
**Noire**: While I ... Well, as I said, I was a jerk. I flipped through her script, and a flurry of harsh words left my mouth.

**菲林士多**：……怎么还是上次的那个类型？\
**Noire**: Really? This type of story again?

**菲林士多**：我说过了，你不适合写这种故事。\
**Noire**: I told you this isn't your strong suit.

**何日君**：……！\
**He Rijun**: ...!

那部剧本连带那盘胶片，被彼时的菲林士多塞回了何日君的怀中，再没有多看一眼。\
The script, along with the reel, is shoved back into Hé Rìjūn's hands without a second glance.

**菲林士多**：无论是我还是阿星，最终都没有看到泰瑞莎拍摄的那部所谓“很简单的”片花究竟是什么样的。\
**Noire**: In the end, neither Ā Xīng nor I cared enough to watch Teresa's sizzle reel, even though she tried so hard to present it to us.

**菲林士多**：而那就是我们最后一次见到泰瑞莎了。\
**Noire**: That was the last time we saw Teresa.

**梁月**：……那场大火。\
**Liang Yue**: That fire ...

**菲林士多**：没错。\
这也是我在听说那盘胶片再次出现后，不顾代价想要将它弄到手的原因。\
**Noire**: Yes. That's why I'd pay any price to get that film.

**菲林士多**：《三燕归巢》的剧本已经在火海中化为灰烬，我只是想要看看泰瑞莎当时究竟想要一个怎样的故事。\
**Noire**: Her script was burned to ashes in the fire. I need to know what story she was trying to tell.

**菲林士多**：我猜阿星也是一样。\
**Noire**: I suppose Ā Xīng feels the same.

菲林士多向梁月示意那只文件袋。\
Noire gestures toward the file.

**菲林士多**：这就是之前你和那位高个子的警官造访时，说想要看的东西。\
**Noire**: This is what you wanted to see last time you and your officer friend visited me.

**梁月**：您是说那封“威胁信”？\
**Liang Yue**: You mean the threatening letter?

**菲林士多**：这并不是信。\
**Noire**: It's not a letter, actually.

梁月放下手中的照片，将文件袋里剩余的东西拿了出来。\
那是一本有些年头了的册子，封皮已经泛黄。\
Liáng sets down the photo and pulls out the remaining contents of the file. It's an aged script, its cover yellowed by time.

翻动了两页后，熟悉的台词映入眼帘。\
梁月立刻明白了手中的东西所代表的含义。\
As she flips through, familiar lines of dialogue meet her eyes. In an instant, she understands the significance of what she's holding.

**梁月**：这是……《神秘警探C07》第一部的剧本。\
**Liang Yue**: It's the script of Detective C07 I.

**菲林士多**：初版。是泰瑞莎给阿星的那一本。\
**Noire**: The original—the one Teresa handed to Ā Xīng all those years ago.

**梁月**：……\
**Liang Yue**: ...

在屏幕上观看过那部电影无数次，梁月从来没有预料到过有一天，一切的原点竟然会被自己捧在手中。\
Liáng never imagined that, one day, she would be holding the origin of the very film that inspired her as a child.
