**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：我们都知道了——你做得漂亮。很高兴能有你这样的人加入我们科，现在我们最不期望到来的就是你的实习截止日期了。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: I gotta say, you've done an awesome job. Folks at the department have all been talking about it. We're proud of you. Please tell me there's some way to postpone the end of your field training.

这是今天梁月握住的第二只手了。\
This is the second hand Liáng has shaken today.

**梁月**：……谢谢，您过奖了。\
您找我们是？\
**Liang Yue**: Th-Thank you. That's very kind. Um. What brings you here?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：埃尔登警长让我来喊你们。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Deputy Chief Elden, of course. Who else?

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：基金会的增援已经赶到，奇星小姐之后会交给他们那边负责协调审讯、定罪和量刑的事宜，那张让人头疼的胶片也会被带回基金会。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: Foundation staff have arrived. They're gonna take over Qí Xīng's interrogation and everything. They're gonna take the film reel back to their headquarters, too.

**神秘学警察Ⅰ**：——但在那之前，你们的请求被同意了。\
我们将会放映一次那盘胶片《三燕归巢》。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer I**: But your request has been approved. We can watch Reunion of the Three Swallows before they take it away.

**埃尔登警长**：……该死，神秘学犯罪科的办公室可不是电影院，哪里来的这么多人？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: For crying out loud, the DAA isn't a movie theater. Where'd all these people come from?

埃尔登的目光扫过面前的众人，不禁咒骂出声。\
Elden scans the group before him.

**菲林士多**：我很抱歉，警长先生，是我将各位喊来的。\
**Noire**: My apologies, sir. I invited them.

**菲林士多**：泰瑞莎最后的作品在短时间内，恐怕只有这么一次展示在人前的机会了，作为她的好友，我希望能够有尽可能多的观众作为见证。\
**Noire**: This may be the only chance for Teresa's last work to be shown to the public. I want as many people to see it as possible.

**菲林士多**：这是每个创作者的愿望，也是我的私心，还请您原谅。\
**Noire**: Every filmmaker wants their work to be shown to the world. I appreciate your understanding.

埃尔登还想要说些什么，但被泥鯭的士抢了先。\
Before Elden can respond, An-an cuts in.

**泥鯭的士**：有什么关系嘛，阿sir！在这里的都是了解事件内情的人，我们也很想知道，那张胶片原本拍的东西到底是什么。\
**An-an Lee**: Come on, Ā sir, it's no big deal. Everyone here knows what really happened. We just want to know what the film's about.

**民间侦探**：我可是在电视上看见了，“我代表神秘学犯罪科，期待着来自你们的意见与帮助”……难道说现在心怀正义与热情的市民，连点知情权都没有了？\
**Private Investigator**: Yeah, didn't you say something on TV about assistance and feedback? You'd be going back on your word if you ignored us now.

**埃尔登警长**：周先生，你真是越来越巧舌如簧了啊，嗯？\
**Deputy Chief Elden**: Hey, don't you go talking circles around me again.

尽管不再像是过去那样充满了火药味，但二人间再次剑拔弩张了起来。\
Even in this harmonious scene, the two men can't help but bicker.

一旁的波蒂埃不禁翻了个白眼——但率先及时制止了这场争吵的，是一旁身着基金会制服的身影。\
Poitier rolls her eyes. Luckily, the two are quickly interrupted by a woman in a Foundation uniform.

**基金会职员**：没关系的，埃尔登警长。\
**Foundation Staff**: No need to worry, Deputy Chief Elden.

**基金会职员**：经过我们的检测，这张胶片《三燕归巢》在经由执夜人见习生梁小姐的术式处理后，如今已经不具备干扰现实的能力。\
**Foundation Staff**: After thorough examination, we've determined that the film reel no longer possesses the ability to twist reality.

**基金会职员**：这一次叨扰各位的事件与我们的工作失误逃不开干系，而正如周先生所说，各位当然拥有知晓事件真相的权力。\
**Foundation Staff**: It was our negligence that allowed the film to be taken in the first place, so, as Mr. Zhōu said, the people deserve to know the truth.

**基金会职员**：因此在签署保密协议后，诸位便可以先行进入房间。\
放映将在十五分钟后开始。\
**Foundation Staff**: Besides, every viewer is required to sign this confidentiality agreement before entering the screening room. Alright, everyone, please hurry. The movie starts in fifteen minutes.

**泥鯭的士**：——听着就像是“电影即将开场”一样，太棒了！\
我可不会错过这个，算我一个。\
**An-an Lee**: Oh, I'm pumped. No way I'm missing this. Gimme a pen.

在泥鯭的士第一个跳到办公桌前后，那些仍然在观望着的神秘学警察与来自唐人街的民间侦探们互相看了看，相继加入到了排在办公桌前的队伍之中。\
An-an heads over to the desk, and the DAA officers and Chinatown private detectives follow suit.

但梁月与一旁的菲林士多并不着急，她们早就签署了保密协议——因为那份协议最初就是由她们草拟的。\
Liáng and Noire, on the other hand, hang back. They already signed the confidentiality agreement. After all, they are the ones who drafted it.

**菲林士多**：谢谢你，执夜人小姐。\
**Noire**: You have my thanks, vigil.

**菲林士多**：如果没有你帮助我一起争取，恐怕我和阿星并不一定能够获得这次观看泰瑞莎遗作的机会。\
**Noire**: If it weren't for you, I doubt Ā Xīng and I would have had this chance to watch our good friend's swan song.

**菲林士多**：另外……我还必须感谢你帮助我阻止了阿星，帮助我守住了自己的誓言。\
**Noire**: I also have to thank you for helping me stop Ā Xīng and for helping me keep my promise.

**梁月**：誓言？\
**Liang Yue**: Your promise?

菲林士多伸出手，抚摸自己的双腿。\
Noire pats her hands on her thighs.

**菲林士多**：是的，我曾经对着这双腿立下的誓言。\
**Noire**: Yes, I swore on these two legs.

**菲林士多**：过去的我执着于追求“最好的电影”，将人放在其次……但那是错误的。\
**Noire**: In the past, all I cared about was making the best film. I saw everyone, even my actors and writers, as tools to reach that goal. But I was wrong.

**菲林士多**：这个世界上没有“最好的电影”，只有“更好的电影”。\
而为了拍出“更好的电影”，我需要的是人。\
**Noire**: There's no such thing as a best film, only a better film. And to make a better film, I need a team around me.

**菲林士多**：重要的不是“这一部”“那一部”的电影，而是拍电影的人。\
**Noire**: What matters most is the people who make the film, not the film itself.

她回头，向犯罪科深处的那扇房门望去。\
She turns her head and looks toward the bolted door at the other end of the room.

**菲林士多**：只要还活着，就有未来。\
也许我可以帮阿星请个律师，争取让她少判几年。\
**Noire**: But as long as we're living, there's still a future. Maybe I should hire a good lawyer for Ā Xīng. They can probably secure a shorter sentence.

**菲林士多**：等到她出来……也许她会不愿意，但搞不好我们还可以合作。\
**Noire**: When she's free again, both physically and mentally, perhaps we can make a movie together, just like old times.

梁月几乎是目瞪口呆。\
Liáng is momentarily stunned.

**梁月**：您的意思是还要找奇星小姐拍电影？\
恕我直言，菲林士多女士，那恐怕会是很久很久以后了……\
**Liang Yue**: Are you sure? With all due respect, Ms. Noire, that will probably be a very long time from now.

**菲林士多**：谁说得准呢？\
就算到时候我们都变成老奶奶了，只要能动弹，就能拍电影嘛。\
**Noire**: So? Even if we're old ladies by then, as long as we can still move, I'm certain we can make movies.

**菲林士多**：当然，我对梁小姐你也十分中意。\
如果你今后有正式进军电影界的想法，请务必联系我。\
**Noire**: Speaking of which, you'd make an excellent addition to my crew, Ms. Liáng. Don't hesitate to contact me if you reconsider your career choice.

**梁月**：多谢您的赏识，菲林士多导演。但我想我还是停留在欣赏电影的层面就够了，短时间内我并没有转行的打算。\
**Liang Yue**: You're very generous, Ms. Noire. But I think I'll stick to being a fan for the time being.

**梁月**：不过我倒是很期待您的下一部作品。\
**Liang Yue**: I look forward to seeing what you do next.

**菲林士多**：它不会让你失望的。\
**Noire**: You won't be disappointed.

**菲林士多**：……说起来，你见到莱瑟姆小姐了吗？\
我邀请了她，但她并没有接电话，想来是又把手机忘在房间里了。\
**Noire**: By the way, have you seen Ms. Latham lately? I tried to invite her, but she didn't pick up the phone. She must've left it in her room again.

**梁月**：我刚才在医院碰到了她。斯考特小姐恢复了意识，她急匆匆地前去探望了。\
**Liang Yue**: Actually, I ran into her at the hospital earlier. Ms. Scott just regained consciousness. She wanted to visit her.

听到梁月的回答，菲林士多收起了笑容，露出了若有所思的表情。\
Noire's smile fades slightly, and a contemplative expression comes over her.

**菲林士多**：那个女孩，斯考特……\
我始终觉得，她的身上还有什么我们没能挖掘出来的秘密。\
**Noire**: Ms. Scott ... Something tells me that there's still an unsolved mystery there.

**梁月**：……您是指您之前提到过的，这一系列事件背后的隐情？\
**Liang Yue**: You mean a truth hidden behind all these incidents?

**菲林士多**：是啊。如果用象棋来比喻，我们就像是“兵”，巧攻渡河，因此逃离了原本被规划好的路线，得了一条生路。\
**Noire**: Yes. Like a chessboard, we are the pawns placed on the front line. Somehow, we've managed to fight our way out, escaping our planned doom.

**菲林士多**：——但我们还是没能看到在这盘棋上对弈的执棋人。\
我不喜欢这种感觉。\
**Noire**: But who is the player who placed us there? They're still a mystery, watching us from the shadows. I don't like this feeling.

**梁月**：……我会持续关注这件事的。\
**Liang Yue**: I'll keep an eye on the matter.

**梁月**：这起事件随后将会交给正式执夜人来负责，如果背后还有什么阴谋，想必他们也一定能够发现。\
**Liang Yue**: I already made a detailed report to my superiors. If there's anything else going on, I'm sure the Vigiles will put a stop to it.

**菲林士多**：希望如此。\
**Noire**: I suppose we'll have to wait and see.

菲林士多的表情并未舒展，似乎“夜巡特遣管理局”的名号并没能带给她更多的信心。梁月心生疑惑，正欲追问，却听到波蒂埃的招呼声。\
Noire's expression does not ease. It seems the title Vigiles Bureau doesn't bring her much confidence. Before Liáng can inquire further, Poitier calls her.

**波蒂埃**：嘿，梁！还有菲林士多导演，大家都已经搞定了，就等你们就位后开场了。\
**Poitier**: Hey, you two, get your asses in the screening room. We're all waiting for you.

**梁月**：这就来！\
**Liang Yue**: On our way.

**菲林士多**：……没有什么事情比一场即将开演的电影更紧要的了。\
我们走吧，执夜人小姐。\
**Noire**: Nothing's more important than a movie that's about to start. Let's go, vigil.

她们相视一笑，走向那间临时的影院。\
They exchange a smile and enter the makeshift theater together.

## SC-22 无署名访客 / Anonymous Visitor

**空脑袋**：斯考特……斯考特……奇怪，难道不是这个方向吗？\
**Loggerhead**: Scott's ward, Scott's ward. Did I take a wrong turn?

**空脑袋**：抱歉打扰一下，请问康斯坦丝·斯考特的病房是在哪里？\
我有些迷路了……\
**Loggerhead**: Oh, excuse me, doctor. Could you tell me where Constance Scott's ward is? I'm kinda lost.

**医生**：哦，那间病房并不在这个区域。\
您需要从这里向前走，在拐角处左拐，再在下一个拐角处向右。\
**Doctor**: You're in the wrong area. You need to go straight forward this way, take a left at the corner, and a right at the next.

**空脑袋**：向前，向左，再向右……好的，我记住了。\
谢谢您！\
**Loggerhead**: Forward, left, then right. Okay. I'll remember it now. Thanks for the help.

**医生**：不客气。\
**Doctor**: Sure.

身着亮黄色外套、顶着显眼机械脑袋的少女道过谢后，口中不断重复着方才得知的路线，迈步走开。\
Loggerhead makes her way down the hallway, muttering the directions to herself as she goes.

——但她走到一半，忽然停下了脚步，疑惑地回头看了一眼。\
But then, she stops and turns back in confusion.

**空脑袋**：奇怪。\
刚才的那名医生，我是不是曾经和她说过话？\
**Loggerhead**: Hm, that's odd. Why do I feel like I talked to that doctor a few days ago?

**空脑袋**：……不对，应该是我又记错了吧？\
上次的那位女士应该更温柔一些。\
**Loggerhead**: Must just be my bad memory. The lady last time was more friendly.

绰号“空脑袋”的少女歪了歪头，很快决定将这个小小的疑问从大脑中清空出去。\
She tilts her head before quickly, deciding to let it go.

**空脑袋**：等等！\
她刚才说怎么走来着？\
**Loggerhead**: Wait, which way did she say again?

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：抱歉，医生。\
但如果我没有记错，现在还不到要例行检查的时间？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Sorry, doctor, it isn't time for the routine checkup yet.

**医生**：是呀。昨天的体检报告出来了，数据上有一些波动。\
**Doctor**: You're right, but yesterday's medical report showed some concerning fluctuations in the patient's data.

**医生**：虽然可能并无大碍，但我们还是需要确认一下病人的状态作确定。\
**Doctor**: It's probably nothing serious, but we should conduct a clinical check on the patient just in case.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：请稍等，我向您的上级确认一下。\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Please wait a moment. Let me verify this with your superior.

**医生**：我理解，警官。\
没有什么比小心谨慎行事更重要的了，毕竟里面的可是重要的案件相关人员。\
**Doctor**: Of course, officer. You can never be too cautious, especially when the patient's involved in a sensitive case.

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：是啊。\
多谢您的理……解……\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Yeah. Thanks for your un ... der ...

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：唔……？\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: Ugh ...?

隔着门板传来的对话声，中断在了一个并不自然的位置。\
The patient inside the ward hears the conversation outside the door come to an abrupt halt.

病床上双手被铐在栏杆上的患者本百无聊赖地盯着窗外，但意识到这一点后，她不禁收回目光，望向紧闭的房门。\
She sits with her hands cuffed to the railing, turning her head away from the window and toward the closed door before her.

**斯考特**：……怎么了？\
**Scott**: What's wrong?

门外不再传来声音。\
There is no response from the other side.

数秒后，门把转动，她病房的房门被轻轻地打开。\
站在门口的是一个她隐约有些印象的普通医生。\
Several seconds later, the doorknob turns. Standing in the doorway is a doctor. She looks vaguely familiar.

**医生**：您好，斯考特小姐。今天您感觉如何？\
**Doctor**: Good afternoon, Ms. Scott. How are you feeling today?

**神秘学警察Ⅱ**：……\
**Arcane Affairs Officer II**: ...

但在门被重新关上之前，斯考特瞥见站在门口的神秘学警察直视着前方，没有分给这个方向半点余光。\
Before the door is closed again, Scott catches a glimpse of the Arcane Affairs Officer staring straight ahead. He doesn't so much as glance in her direction.

——有什么地方不对劲。斯考特立刻直起了身子。\
Something is wrong. Scott shoots up straight.

**斯考特**：你是谁？\
**Scott**: Who are you?

**医生**：有人让我给您送来这束花。\
**Doctor**: Someone brought you these flowers.

**斯考特**：花？\
**Scott**: Flowers?

她这才注意到女医生的手上捧着一只玻璃花瓶，插在里面的白色花束洁净无瑕，清新动人。\
Only then does she notice that the doctor is holding a glass vase filled with pure white flowers, fresh and delicate.

**斯考特**：不对……这太奇怪了。\
**Scott**: No. Something's not right.

**斯考特**：我听到你和那个警员的对话了，刚才你还说你是来给我检查身体状况的，但拿着一只花瓶要怎么检——\
**Scott**: I heard what you said to the officer. How are you supposed to do a medical check with a flower ...

**斯考特**：……查…………\
**Scott**: ... vase ...

**斯考特**：…………\
**Scott**: ...

斯考特隐约听到自己的声音也被吞没了，但她无暇顾及。\
因为她的全部注意力，都伴随着她的视线钉在了那只花瓶的身上。\
Scott vaguely hears her own voice being swallowed, but somehow, she doesn't care. All her attention is locked on the vase.

不是花，而是花瓶。明明看起来只是寻常的玻璃制品，在阳光的照射下，却如同水晶般美丽，折射出梦幻般的色彩。\
Not the flowers, but the vase itself. At first glance, it looked like any other glass item. But now that it's under the sunlight, it is shimmering like crystal, refracting dreamlike colors around the ward.

**斯考特**：就像是……水晶……？\
**Scott**: Is this ... crystal?

头脑中阻隔着一部分记忆的高墙，如同肥皂泡般“啵”的一声破碎、消失。\
A barrier blocking off her memories suddenly bursts.

**斯考特**：……是您，女士。\
**Scott**: It's you, madame.

**斯考特**：您说过除非出了什么意外，否则您不会再联系我了。\
是出了什么事吗？是出售给您的那样东西有什么毛病吗？\
**Scott**: You said you wouldn't contact me unless something bad happened. Is there something wrong with the object you bought?

**？？？**：不，它很完美，你帮了我大忙。\
**???**: No, it is perfect. You have been of superb help.

**斯考特**：这是我的荣幸，女士。\
另外我必须要感叹您的高瞻远瞩，您真是料事如神。\
**Scott**: It was my honor to serve you, madame. And I must say, you have incredible foresight.

**斯考特**：我失手了，被夜巡特遣的人抓住了……但他们并没有问出什么东西，因为我根本不记得。\
**Scott**: The Vigiles caught me, but they couldn't get any useful information, because I can't remember any.

**？？？**：但你看起来仍然身处麻烦之中。\
**???**: But you still seem to be in a rather precarious situation.

**斯考特**：呃，是的……但您不用担心！\
我会想办法解决的，这点小事，不用劳烦您。\
**Scott**: Y-Yes, but you needn't worry. I can handle this myself.

**？？？**：那就再好不过了。\
**???**: That is good to hear.

传信术的对面不再传来声音了。若不是自花瓶中仍折射出令她隐隐头晕目眩的光，她也许会以为对方已经切断了这仅被允许单方面发起的通讯。\
The other end of the communication incantation falls silent. If not for the light still refracting from the vase, she might have thought the other party already hung up.

**斯考特**：对了！前些天，我还遇到了玛蒂尔达小姐。\
**Scott**: By the way, I met Matilda not long ago.

**斯考特**：她……很担心您。您并没有将您的近况告知她吗？\
**Scott**: She was worried about you. Have you not contacted her?

**？？？**：没有这个必要。\
**???**: That is not necessary.

**？？？**：如果她能更坚强和更敏锐一些，那么她便能够自己发现。\
**???**: Were she more perceptive, she would have already discovered me herself. She will find me when she's ready.

对方听上去并不如斯考特所想的那样，对这个话题感兴趣。\
The voice on the other side shows little interest in the topic.

这让斯考特在心中窃喜，却也不得不绞尽脑汁，寻找着下一个能够多少延长这场对话的借口。\
Scott smirks to herself but struggles to find another excuse to prolong the conversation.

——但实际上，已经没有这个必要了。\
But her moment has already passed.

**斯考特**：……嗯？\
**Scott**: Hm?

视野中的色彩扭曲了，意识开始旋转。\
The colors twist, and her consciousness begins to spiral.

**斯考特**：我要……做什么来着？\
**Scott**: *sigh* What was I doing again?

**？？？**：我这次联系你，是为了向你表示感谢。\
**???**: I am contacting you to express my gratitude.

**？？？**：谢谢你，斯考特小姐。\
同时请相信我，你绝不像是你内心自认为的那样愚钝。\
**???**: Thank you very much, Ms. Scott. And please believe me, you are far more gifted than you think.

从房间中某处色彩与光线不自然地扭曲的位置上，传来一名女子的声音。\
清雅，高贵，似曾相识。\
The woman's voice rings out from a particularly distorted and colorful spot in the room. It is elegant, dignified, and strangely familiar.

**斯考特**：你是……？\
**Scott**: Wh-Who are you?

那个声音没有回答她。\
The voice does not answer.

**？？？**：但那些黑色猎犬的鼻子比我想象中的还要灵敏。\
我想我们的关系就要到此为止了——因此这一次，我也是来道别的。\
**???**: However, those black dogs have a keener sense of smell than I thought. I'm afraid our relationship has come to an end.

**？？？**：再见了，斯考特小姐。\
**???**: Goodbye, Ms. Scott.

**斯考特**：等等——\
**Scott**: Huh? W-Wait!

子弹将玻璃花瓶击成了碎片，梦与现实一同破碎，撒落一地。\
A bullet shatters the vase, shattering the dream and crashing her back to reality.

病房的房门不知何时，已经悄无声息地打开了。一双黑色的皮靴踏着碎落满地的花瓶碎片，来到昏厥的斯考特病床前。\
At some point, the door was silently opened. A pair of black leather boots steps over the shards of the broken vase and comes to a stop at Scott's bedside.

**黑鹮**：跑得还挺快。\
看来这条鱼比我们想象中的还要大。\
**Black Ibis**: Ha, they run fast, that's for sure. Looks like this fish is bigger than we thought.

**黑鹮**：怎么样，他们两个情况如何？\
**Black Ibis**: Have you figured out what happened to the two officers?

身着漆黑制服的女子回过头，看向身后的副手。\
The woman turns to her cadet.

同样身着漆黑制服的男子，正将方才造访这间病房的医生，与原本守在门外的神秘学警察扶到一旁。他们同样已经陷入了昏睡。\
A man, also dressed in the same black uniform, is dragging the unconscious body of the doctor who visited earlier beside that of the DAA officer who had been keeping guard outside.

**副手**：中了某种催眠术，施术者水平相当高，无法回溯，恐怕查不出来什么。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: They're under some kind of hypnosis. Caster's no amateur, either. Arcane fluctuations are impossible to trace.

**黑鹮**：哦？不错……相当不错。\
**Black Ibis**: Not bad. Not bad at all.

女子俯身捡起地上的一片玻璃碎片，勾起唇角连连点头。\
这引发了一旁副手的不满。\
She crouches down to pick up a shard of glass. As she examines it, her mouth curls into a smile.

**副手**：还不错呢？这一次费了这样大的周章，明明早知道斯考特就是犯人，还非要将计就计，用她引出什么“背后的人”……\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Not bad? This is really bad. We already knew Scott was the culprit, but you just had to use her as bait to "reel in the fish hiding in the darkness."

**副手**：这下好了吧！\
斯考特让那个罪魁祸首消除了记忆，这条线等于是断了。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Now all we have is Scott with no memories of what happened and a stone-cold trail. Truly genius!

**副手**：而且我早就说过，没有必要特意瞒着梁。她也是你带的学徒，既然她刚巧在洛杉矶这边实习，让她协助我们显然是个更好的主意。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: And I still don't get why you're keeping all this from Liáng. She's your cadet and right here in the city. We should've had her join the investigation.

**副手**：哼，我到时要看看，等她知道这一切的来龙去脉后，你要怎么和她交代！\
话说在前面，这次我可不会为你说好话了。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Ha, I can't wait to see her face when she finds out what's been going on. And I'm not defending you this time, either.

面对副手的指责，女子却一脸无辜。\
Faced with her cadet's accusations, the woman feigns innocence.

**黑鹮**：什么怎么交代？\
这些都是对她的考验呀。\
**Black Ibis**: Defending me? There's nothing to defend.

**黑鹮**：我们的计划原本就是“引蛇出洞”。若是告诉了梁，她的行动就必然会出现不自然的地方，搞不好就会打草惊蛇。\
**Black Ibis**: If we'd told her about our plan, she would've started acting differently and spooked our fish.

**黑鹮**：再说本来这次的实习项目，考察的就是她是否能够在没有其他执夜人支援的情况下独当一面——而她也通过这次的事情证明了，她可以。\
**Black Ibis**: Besides, the whole point of her field training program in the LAPD was to see if she could handle things on her own. And she's proven that she can.

**黑鹮**：我看那些神秘学犯罪科的家伙挺喜欢她的，那个警长嘴上不说，最后一定也会给她个不错的评价。这不是挺好吗？\
**Black Ibis**: The Division of Arcane Affairs seems to adore her, so I'm sure the Deputy Chief will give her an excellent write-up. Everything's turned out great, hasn't it?

**黑鹮**：唉，作为她的导师，我可是用心良苦。\
你不要把我说得像是什么不负责任的人一样呀。\
**Black Ibis**: See how considerate I am? How I always do things in my cadets' best interests? How could you make me out to be such a heartless, irresponsible monster?

女子装模做样地摆出了一副痛心的表情，这让她的副手没忍住翻了一个白眼。\
She exaggerates a sorrowful expression, which only makes her cadet roll his eyes in exasperation.

**黑鹮**：别这样嘛，这次的事件我已经有头绪了。\
**Black Ibis**: Oh, don't give me that look. Anyway, I think I've got an idea as to what's going on.

**副手**：……你的意思是？\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Really?

女子收起了方才胡闹的神色，扬起嘴角。\
The woman drops her act and smiles knowingly.

**黑鹮**：这是一条大鱼，我们的线不够结实，让那家伙跑了——但光是确认了这塘池子里有这么一条庞然大物的存在，这次就已经收获颇丰了。\
**Black Ibis**: Our big fish got away, yes, but just confirming that a fish this big exists has already made this worth our time.

**黑鹮**：包括这次将唐人街弄得天翻地覆的那盘胶片，以及那个在圣保罗被司辰打了个稀巴烂的发条玩具，一共有五件神秘学管理品失窃。\
**Black Ibis**: Now, back to the stolen arcane items. There are five in total, including the cursed film reel and the wind-up toy that the Timekeeper shattered.

**黑鹮**：告诉我，鲍勃。\
你觉得我们在追查的那名幕后黑手，是这五个东西都需要吗？\
**Black Ibis**: Tell me, Bob, does our fish need all five arcane items?

**副手**：我叫阿兰，不叫鲍勃！\
你到底什么时候能够记住？\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: It's Alan, not Bob. How many times do I have to tell you?

**副手**：……我的答案是，不。那个发条玩具已经报废，这次的胶片也成功被我那名前途无量的小师妹回收。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: And to answer your question, no, I don't think so. The wind-up toy's already been destroyed, and the film reel's been recovered by a fellow cadet.

**副手**：它们的确惹出了不少麻烦，但我看不出它们引发的事件之间有什么共通之处。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: These items did cause a few problems, but I don't see any common thread between the incidents they caused.

**黑鹮**：你说得对，布莱恩。\
它们明显是陪跑，是障眼法，是无关紧要的弃子。\
**Black Ibis**: Correct, Brian. Those two items were probably just decoys to divert our attention.

**副手**：我叫阿兰。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Again, it's Alan.

女子没有理会副手的纠正，继续侃侃而谈了下去。\
Ignoring her cadet's correction, she goes on.

**黑鹮**：夫藏木于林，人皆视而不见……\
我们的幕后黑手在那五件东西之中，真正想要的恐怕也只有一件。\
**Black Ibis**: A clever fish knows how to muddy the waters to hide itself. Of the five objects, they probably only need one.

**黑鹮**：猜猜看，巴克。最有可能的是哪一个？\
**Black Ibis**: Take a guess, Buck. Which one do they need?

**副手**：我叫阿兰，不是B，是A……\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: It's Alan! A-L-A-N! There isn't even a single B in it.

副手一边无奈地反驳，一边思索了起来。\
The cadet sighs, half in reluctance, half in realization.

**副手**：剩下的三件物品中最有可能的……等等，难道是？\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Well, out of the three, which one is—Wait, could it be?!

**黑鹮**：你猜对了。\
**Black Ibis**: Bingo.

她从自己副手瞬间难看起来的脸色中，判断出对方找到了那个答案。\
From the way her cadet's face darkens, she can tell he has found the answer.

**副手**：但那个传说是真的吗？它真的能够用在“那个”仪式中？\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Does that mean the legend's real? It can really be used in "that" ritual?

**黑鹮**：现在看来，恐怕是的。\
**Black Ibis**: It would seem so.

**副手**：……所以，是重塑之手。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: So, it's Manus Vindictae again.

他念出那个名字，表情凝重。\
He speaks the name, his expression grim.

**副手**：至少是能够查阅到神秘学藏品管理部档案，甚至是能够拿到藏品管理部防护术式机密文件的基金会高层中——有重塑之手的人。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: They must've planted a mole somewhere among the Foundation's elites, someone with clearance to the Arcanum Containment Department.

**黑鹮**：这倒不一定。\
**Black Ibis**: Hm. It seems our fish doesn't wear the black robe.

女子摸了摸下巴，给出了一个令自己的副手再次大跌眼镜的答复。\
The woman taps her chin. This response makes her cadet's eyes widen in disbelief.

**副手**：什么？可……难道除了他们之外，还有其他势力有动机举行“那个仪式”，同时具有从基金会的眼皮底下盗走东西的能力？我实在不这么认为。\
**Black Ibis's Cadet**: Huh? So you're saying there's someone behind all this who wants to perform "that" ritual and somehow has the means to steal from the Foundation? There's just no way.

**黑鹮**：东西应当最终是要去向重塑之手没错，但我们的这只老鼠……我想他，或是她却不一定完全和重塑之手站在同一阵线。\
**Black Ibis**: The stolen items would probably go to the Manus eventually, but I have a hunch that our wily fish isn't totally on their side.

**黑鹮**：重塑之手一度相当重用那个用发条玩具唤出的恶魔，明眼人都看得出她的价值。\
**Black Ibis**: Manus Vindictae obviously considered the succubus a valuable asset before she got away, right?

**黑鹮**：如果我们的嫌疑人完全效忠于重塑之手，那件封印物就不会辗转一番才来到启明会的人手中了。\
**Black Ibis**: So if our fish was a die-hard loyalist, they would've delivered the wind-up toy to their master straightway, rather than letting it be passed around all over the place.

**黑鹮**：虽然与重塑之手有所勾结，但我们追踪的那位恐怕亦有着自己的目的。\
**Black Ibis**: While our fish is in collusion with Manus Vindictae, they're swimming in murky waters. They may be pursuing their own agenda.

女子扬起嘴角，将手中的那枚玻璃碎片弹飞。\
She curls her lips into a smile and flicks the shard of glass from between her fingers.

**黑鹮**：事情开始有趣起来了，不是吗？\
**Black Ibis**: Things are starting to get interesting, aren't they?

**黑鹮**：所以我才说——这相当不错。\
**Black Ibis**: Like I said earlier, not bad at all.

片刻后，两个黑衣人的身影从病房中消失了。\
With that, the two figures in black vanish out the door.
